- *He **avoids** **sinning**.* (Él evita pecar.)
- *She **considers** **moving** to a new city.* (Ella considera mudarse a una nueva ciudad.)
- *I don't **mind** **praying** with you.* (No me importa orar contigo.)
- *We **appreciate** **helping** the poor.* (Apreciamos ayudar a los pobres.)
- *They **risk losing** everything.* (Arriesgan perderlo todo.)
- *I **prefer reading** the Bible in the morning.* (Prefiero leer la Biblia por la mañana.)

**Edificación:** Jesús fue tentado pero no pecó. Aprendemos a usar verbos seguidos de gerundio para hablar de cómo evitamos el pecado y buscamos la santidad.

---

### Lección 34 – "He Used to Pray Before Dawn"
**Gramática focal:** *Used to* para hábitos pasados vs. *be used to* para familiaridad.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He used to pray before dawn."* (Adaptado de Marcos 1:35)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"Very early in the morning, while it was still dark, Jesus got up, left the house and went off to a solitary place, where he prayed."* (Marcos 1:35, EASY)

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| early | temprano | still dark | todavía oscuro |
| got up | se levantó | left | dejó / se fue |
| solitary | solitario | prayed | oró |

**Uso de *used to* y *be used to*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *used to + infinitivo* | Hábito pasado (ya no ocurre) | *He **used to pray** before dawn.* |
| *didn't use to + infinitivo* | Negativa de hábito pasado | *She **didn't use to pray**.* |
| *be used to + -ing* | Estar acostumbrado a | *He **is used to praying**.* |
| *get used to + -ing* | Acostumbrarse a | *She **is getting used to praying**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **used to** teach in the temple."* (Juan 7:14, adaptado) – Solía enseñar en el templo.
2. *"We **used to** worship in that place."* (Juan 4:20, adaptado) – Solíamos adorar en ese lugar.
3. *"I **am not used to** praying in public."* (Mateo 6:5, adaptado) – No estoy acostumbrado a orar en público.
4. *"She **was used to** waiting."* (Lucas 2:37, adaptado) – Estaba acostumbrada a esperar.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **used to** pray every morning before work.* (Solía orar cada mañana antes del trabajo.)
- *He **used to** read the Bible daily.* (Solía leer la Biblia diariamente.)
- *She **didn't use to** go to church.* (No solía ir a la iglesia.)
- *I **am used to** waking up early to pray.* (Estoy acostumbrado a despertarme temprano para orar.)
- *They **are getting used to** the new pastor.* (Se están acostumbrando al nuevo pastor.)

**Edificación:** Jesús se levantaba temprano para orar. Aprendemos a usar "used to" para hablar de hábitos espirituales pasados y "be used to" para la familiaridad con la vida de fe.

---

### Lección 35 – Repaso: "He Went on Teaching"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de gerundios e infinitivos.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He went on teaching."* (Adaptado de Marcos 2:13)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando verbos seguidos de gerundio e infinitivo.

**Ejemplo:**
- *He **stopped to pray**.*
- *He **kept praying**.*
- *I **enjoy reading** the Bible.*
- *She **decided to become** a missionary.*
- *We **need to pray** more.*
- *He **avoided sinning**.*
- *I **used to pray** before meals.*
- *She **is used to preaching**.*
- *They **finished singing**.*
- *He **goes on preaching**.*

---

## UNIDAD 8: CONECTORES Y CLAUSULAS COMPLEJAS
*Lecciones 36 a 40*

---

### Lección 36 – "Although He Was Crucified"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de contraste (*although, though, even though, despite, in spite of*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Although he was crucified, he rose again."* (Adaptado de Romanos 6:9-10)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"For we know that since Christ was raised from the dead, he cannot die again; death no longer has mastery over him. The death he died, he died to sin once for all; but the life he lives, he lives to God. In the same way, count yourselves dead to sin but alive to God in Christ Jesus."* (Romanos 6:9-11, EASY)

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| raised | resucitado | cannot die | no puede morir |
| mastery | dominio | once for all | de una vez por todas |
| count yourselves | consideraos | alive to God | vivos para Dios |

**Conectores de contraste:**

| Conector | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *although* | + cláusula (sujeto + verbo) | ***Although** he was crucified, he rose.* |
| *though* | + cláusula (informal) | ***Though** he was weak, he was strong.* |
| *even though* | + cláusula (énfasis) | ***Even though** he died, he lives.* |
| *despite* | + sustantivo / -ing | ***Despite** the cross, he overcame.* |
| *in spite of* | + sustantivo / -ing | ***In spite of** death, he lives.* |
| *however* | + cláusula (con coma) | *He was crucified. **However**, he rose.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Although** he was a Son, he learned obedience."* (Hebreos 5:8) – Aunque era Hijo, aprendió obediencia.
2. *"**Even though** I walk through the darkest valley, I will fear no evil."* (Salmo 23:4) – Aunque ande en valle de sombra de muerte, no temeré mal alguno.
3. *"**Though** he was rich, he became poor for us."* (2 Corintios 8:9, adaptado) – Aunque era rico, se hizo pobre por nosotros.
4. *"**Despite** the persecution, they rejoiced."* (Hechos 5:41, adaptado) – A pesar de la persecución, se regocijaron.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Expresar contraste en la vida de fe):**

- ***Although** I am weak, God is strong.* (Aunque soy débil, Dios es fuerte.)
- ***Even though** I suffer, I have peace.* (Aunque sufro, tengo paz.)
- *I keep praying **despite** my doubts.* (Sigo orando a pesar de mis dudas.)
- *He is faithful, **however** he is also just.* (Él es fiel; sin embargo, también es justo.)
- ***In spite of** my failures, God loves me.* (A pesar de mis fracasos, Dios me ama.)

**Edificación:** Pablo celebra que, aunque Cristo fue crucificado, resucitó. Aprendemos a usar conectores de contraste para expresar la paradoja de la cruz: muerte que da vida, debilidad que es fortaleza.

---

### Lección 37 – "For God So Loved the World"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de causa y consecuencia (*because, since, as, therefore, so, thus*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"For God so loved the world that he gave his one and only Son."* — **Juan 3:16**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"For God so loved the world that he gave his one and only Son, that whoever believes in him shall not perish but have eternal life. For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world, but to save the world through him."* (Juan 3:16-17, EASY)

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| loved | amó | gave | dio |
| Son | Hijo | believes | cree |
| perish | perecer | eternal life | vida eterna |
| condemn | condenar | save | salvar |

**Conectores de causa y consecuencia:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *because* | Causa directa | *He came **because** he loved us.* |
| *since* | Causa (dada por hecha) | ***Since** he loved us, he came.* |
| *as* | Causa (informal) | ***As** he died for us, we live.* |
| *for* | Causa (formal, explicación) | *He died, **for** he loved us.* |
| *therefore* | Consecuencia | *He loved us; **therefore**, he died.* |
| *so* | Consecuencia | *He loved us, **so** he died.* |
| *thus* | Consecuencia (formal) | *He died; **thus** we are saved.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Because** he lives, we will live."* (Juan 14:19, adaptado) – Porque él vive, nosotros viviremos.
2. *"**Since** we have been justified by faith, we have peace."* (Romanos 5:1) – Justificados, pues, por la fe, tenemos paz.
3. *"God is love. **Therefore**, we should love one another."* (1 Juan 4:16, adaptado) – Dios es amor; por lo tanto, debemos amarnos unos a otros.
4. *"He loved us, **so** he gave his Son."* (Juan 3:16, adaptado) – Nos amó, así que dio a su Hijo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***Because** I believe in God, I have hope.* (Porque creo en Dios, tengo esperanza.)
- ***Since** God is faithful, I trust him.* (Ya que Dios es fiel, confío en él.)
- *He died for us; **therefore**, we should live for him.* (Murió por nosotros; por lo tanto, debemos vivir para él.)
- *I pray every day, **so** I have peace.* (Oro cada día, así que tengo paz.)
- ***For** God loves us, we are not alone.* (Porque Dios nos ama, no estamos solos.)

**Edificación:** Juan explica la razón del amor de Dios: "Porque de tal manera amó Dios al mundo". Aprendemos a usar conectores de causa y consecuencia para explicar nuestra fe y su impacto en nuestra vida.

---

### Lección 38 – "He Died so That We Might Live"
**Gramática focal:** *So that* y *in order to* para expresar propósito.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He died so that we might live."* (Adaptado de 2 Corintios 5:15)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"And he died for all, that those who live should no longer live for themselves but for him who died for them and was raised again. So from now on we regard no one from a worldly point of view. Though we once regarded Christ in this way, we do so no longer. Therefore, if anyone is in Christ, the new creation has come: The old has gone, the new is here!"* (2 Corintios 5:15-17, EASY)

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| died | murió | might live | pudiera vivir |
| regard | considerar | worldly | mundano |
| point of view | punto de vista | once | una vez |
| new creation | nueva creación | old has gone | lo viejo pasó |

**Conectores de propósito:**

| Conector | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *so that* | + cláusula (sujeto + verbo) | *He died **so that** we might live.* |
| *in order that* | + cláusula (formal) | *He died **in order that** we might be saved.* |
| *in order to* | + infinitivo | *He died **in order to** save us.* |
| *to* | + infinitivo | *He came **to** save us.* |

**Regla:** Después de *so that* o *in order that* se usa a menudo *may, might, can, could, will, would*.

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He came **so that** we might have life."* (Juan 10:10) – Vino para que tengamos vida.
2. *"I am sending you **so that** they may see."* (Juan 11:42, adaptado) – Te envío para que vean.
3. *"The Spirit was given **in order to** help us."* (Juan 14:26, adaptado) – El Espíritu fue dado para ayudarnos.
4. *"They prayed **to** receive the Holy Spirit."* (Hechos 8:15, adaptado) – Oraron para recibir el Espíritu Santo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I read the Bible **so that** I might know God better.* (Leo la Biblia para que pueda conocer mejor a Dios.)
- *I pray **in order to** have peace.* (Oro para tener paz.)
- *I go to church **to** worship God.* (Voy a la iglesia para adorar a Dios.)
- *He studies theology **so that** he can preach.* (Estudia teología para poder predicar.)
- *We serve others **so that** they may see God's love.* (Servimos a otros para que vean el amor de Dios.)

**Edificación:** Pablo declara que Cristo murió para que nosotros vivamos para Él. Aprendemos a usar conectores de propósito para expresar el significado y la intención detrás de las acciones de Dios y las nuestras.

---

### Lección 39 – "He Has Risen, Just as He Said"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de comparación y modo (*as, just as, like, as if, as though*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He has risen, just as he said."* — **Mateo 28:6** (adaptado)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"The angel said to the women, 'Do not be afraid, for I know that you are looking for Jesus, who was crucified. He is not here; he has risen, just as he said. Come and see the place where he lay. Then go quickly and tell his disciples: He has risen from the dead and is going ahead of you into Galilee. There you will see him. Now I have told you.'"* (Mateo 28:5-7, EASY)

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| angel | ángel | women | mujeres |
| looking for | buscando | crucified | crucificado |
| risen | resucitado | lay | yació |
| told | dijo | | |

**Conectores de comparación y modo:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *just as* | Exactamente como | *He rose **just as** he said.* |
| *as* | Como (manera) | *Do **as** I have done.* |
| *like* | Como (similar a) | *He is **like** a shepherd.* |
| *as if* | Como si | *He spoke **as if** he knew.* |
| *as though* | Como si | *They acted **as though** they had seen.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"Do to others **as** you would have them do to you."* (Mateo 7:12) – Haced a otros como queréis que os hagan.
2. *"God is **like** a father."* (Salmo 103:13, adaptado) – Dios es como un padre.
3. *"He looks **as if** he is a stranger."* (Lucas 24:28-29, adaptado) – Parecía como si fuera un extraño.
4. *"They acted **as though** they didn't believe."* (Hechos 17:32, adaptado) – Actuaron como si no creyeran.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I trust God **just as** he has promised.* (Confío en Dios tal como ha prometido.)
- *Love others **as** you love yourself.* (Ama a otros como te amas a ti mismo.)
- *He is **like** a father to me.* (Él es como un padre para mí.)
- *She prays **as if** she were speaking to a friend.* (Ella ora como si estuviera hablando con un amigo.)
- *They went **as though** they had been sent.* (Fueron como si hubieran sido enviados.)

**Edificación:** El ángel declaró: "Ha resucitado, tal como dijo". Aprendemos a usar conectores de comparación para afirmar que Dios cumple sus promesas exactamente como las ha dicho.

---

### Lección 40 – Repaso Final: "I Am the Way"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de todos los temas del nivel B1.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I am the way and the truth and the life. No one comes to the Father except through me."* — **Juan 14:6**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura):** 
> *"Jesus answered, 'I am the way and the truth and the life. No one comes to the Father except through me. If you really know me, you will know my Father as well. From now on, you do know him and have seen him.' Philip said, 'Lord, show us the Father and that will be enough for us.' Jesus answered, 'Don't you know me, Philip, even after I have been among you such a long time? Anyone who has seen me has seen the Father. How can you say, "Show us the Father"? Don't you believe that I am in the Father, and that the Father is in me?'"* (Juan 14:6-10, EASY)

**Vocabulario final:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| way | camino | truth | verdad |
| life | vida | except | excepto |
| through me | por medio de mí | know | conocer |
| show | mostrar | enough | suficiente |
| believe | creer | | |

---

## Actividad Final de Evaluación

El estudiante debe escribir un testimonio personal de **20-25 oraciones** que incluya todas las siguientes estructuras del nivel B1:

1. **Past Perfect** (*had + past participle*)
2. **Past Perfect Continuous** (*had been + -ing*)
3. **Tercer condicional** (*If + past perfect, would have + pp*)
4. **I wish / If only** (para el pasado)
5. **Modal de deducción en pasado** (*must have, might have, could have*)
6. **Should have / Shouldn't have**
7. **Relative Clause** (non-defining, con *who/which*)
8. **Voz pasiva** (en al menos dos tiempos diferentes)
9. **Discurso indirecto** (reportando algo que alguien dijo)
10. **Gerundio o infinitivo** (con cambio de significado)
11. **Used to** (hábito pasado)
12. **Conector de contraste** (*although, despite, etc.*)
13. **Conector de causa o consecuencia** (*because, therefore, so*)
14. **Conector de propósito** (*so that, in order to*)

**Ejemplo de testimonio (para guía):**

> *"I **used to** live without hope. I **had never read** the Bible before I met my pastor. He **told me that God loved** me and that Jesus **had died** for my sins. **Although** I was skeptical, I decided to read the Gospel of John. I **wish I had known** this truth earlier! If I **had known**, I **would have changed** my life sooner. I **must have been** searching for meaning without knowing it. I **should have listened** to the gospel years ago. 
>
> *My pastor, **who** is a wise man, explained the Scriptures to me. The Bible, **which** I now read every day, has transformed my life. I **have been given** a new identity in Christ. The old things **have passed away**; I **have been made** a new creation. 
>
> *I **remember thinking** that religion was just rules, but I was wrong. I **stopped to pray** one morning and everything changed. I began **to pray** regularly. I **am used to reading** the Bible now. 
>
> *I read the Bible every day **so that** I might grow in my faith. **Because** I trust in Jesus, I have peace. He died **so that** we might live. **Therefore**, I will follow him all my life. He said, 'I am the way.' I **believe** him."*

---

## Apéndice 1: Tabla de Backshifting (Discurso Indirecto)

| Directo (Presente) | Indirecto (Pasado) | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *"I **am**..."* | *He said he **was**...* | *"I am the light."* → *He said he was the light.* |
| *"I **have**..."* | *He said he **had**...* | *"I have seen."* → *He said he had seen.* |
| *"I **will**..."* | *He said he **would**...* | *"I will come."* → *He said he would come.* |
| *"I **can**..."* | *He said he **could**...* | *"I can help."* → *He said he could help.* |
| *"I **may**..."* | *He said he **might**...* | *"I may come."* → *He said he might come.* |
| *"I **must**..."* | *He said he **had to**...* | *"I must go."* → *He said he had to go.* |
| *"I **am going**..."* | *He said he **was going**...* | *"I am going."* → *He said he was going.* |
| *"I **saw**..."* | *He said he **had seen**...* | *"I saw him."* → *He said he had seen him.* |

---

## Apéndice 2: Verbos con Gerundio e Infinitivo (B1)

| Verbo | + Infinitivo | + Gerundio |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *stop* | *Stop to pray* (para orar) | *Stop praying* (dejar de orar) |
| *remember* | *Remember to pray* (antes) | *Remember praying* (después) |
| *forget* | *Forget to pray* (antes) | *Forget praying* (después) |
| *try* | *Try to pray* (esfuerzo) | *Try praying* (experimentar) |
| *regret* | *Regret to say* (disculpa) | *Regret saying* (lamentar) |
| *go on* | *Go on to say* (nuevo tema) | *Go on saying* (continuar) |
| *like* | *Like to pray* (hábito) | *Like praying* (disfrute) |
| *prefer* | *Prefer to pray* (en general) | *Prefer praying* (en específico) |

---

## Apéndice 3: Conectores Esenciales para B1

| Conector | Categoría | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *although / though / even though* | Contraste | Aunque |
| *despite / in spite of* | Contraste | A pesar de |
| *however* | Contraste | Sin embargo |
| *because / since / as* | Causa | Porque / ya que / como |
| *therefore / so / thus* | Consecuencia | Por lo tanto / así que |
| *so that / in order to* | Propósito | Para que / para |
| *if* | Condición | Si |
| *unless* | Condición negativa | A menos que |
| *as long as* | Condición positiva | Siempre que |
| *when / while / as* | Tiempo | Cuando / mientras |
| *before / after* | Tiempo | Antes de / después de |

---

## Conclusión del Curso

Al completar este nivel B1, el estudiante será capaz de:

- Comprender los puntos principales de textos claros y en lengua estándar sobre asuntos cotidianos, incluyendo la Biblia en una versión adaptada.
- Producir textos simples y coherentes sobre temas que le son familiares o de interés personal, incluyendo su fe y testimonios.
- Describir experiencias, acontecimientos, deseos, aspiraciones y opiniones brevemente, justificándolos.

**Edificación Final:**

> *"Y conoceréis la verdad, y la verdad os hará libres."* — Juan 8:32

El estudiante ha recorrido un camino desde el nivel A1 hasta el B1. Ahora puede leer la Biblia en inglés con comprensión significativa, puede discutir su fe con otros en inglés y puede seguir creciendo en el conocimiento de la Palabra. Este curso ha sido un instrumento para que la Palabra de Dios more abundantemente en su corazón en el idioma inglés.

**"Toda la Escritura es inspirada por Dios y útil para enseñar, para redargüir, para corregir, para instruir en justicia."** – 2 Timoteo 3:
# CURSO DE INGLÉS BÍBLICO – NIVEL B2 (MCER)

## Documento Maestro del Estudiante

---

## Introducción

Este curso es la continuación natural del **Nivel B1** y está diseñado para llevar al estudiante desde un nivel intermedio alto (B1) hasta un **nivel intermedio superior (B2)** del Marco Común Europeo de Referencia (MCER). En este nivel, el estudiante pasa de ser un "usuario independiente" a un "usuario independiente avanzado" con la capacidad de comprender textos complejos y expresarse con fluidez y espontaneidad.

**Versión de la Biblia recomendada:** 
- **English Standard Version (ESV)** – para precisión teológica y riqueza literaria.
- **Nueva Versión Internacional (NVI/NIV)** – para claridad y equilibrio.
- **New Living Translation (NLT)** – para pasajes narrativos y poéticos.
- **EasyEnglish Bible (EASY)** – como texto de apoyo para estructuras difíciles.

**Metodología:**
> *"Leemos la Biblia para aprender inglés, y no al revés."*

Cada lección se centra en **un pasaje bíblico extenso (5-10 versículos)** que contiene la estructura gramatical objetivo. La dinámica es:
1. **Lectura extensiva** del pasaje en inglés (versión ESV/NIV)
2. **Análisis textual** – identificar vocabulario clave, estructuras gramaticales y estilo
3. **Extracción de frases útiles** para la expresión oral y escrita
4. **Aplicación al contexto cotidiano** del estudiante
5. **Producción escrita y oral** – el estudiante expresa su fe usando las estructuras avanzadas
6. **Discusión teológica** – el estudiante utiliza el inglés para profundizar en la comprensión de la Escritura

---

## Estructura del Curso

**Total de lecciones:** 40 lecciones

**Unidades:** 8 unidades de 5 lecciones cada una

**Duración estimada por lección:** 3 - 3.5 horas de instrucción + 3-4 horas de trabajo autónomo

**Duración total estimada:** 120-140 horas de instrucción + 120-160 horas de trabajo autónomo

---

## Contenido Gramatical del Nivel B2

| Categoría | Estructuras B2 |
|:---|:---|
| **Tiempos Verbales** | Future Perfect (*will have + pp*); Future Perfect Continuous (*will have been + -ing*); Past Perfect Continuous (*had been + -ing* – profundización) |
| **Voz Pasiva** | Pasiva con modales (*must have been done*); Pasiva con reporting verbs (*is said to be, is believed to have*); Pasiva con gerundios e infinitivos (*being done, to be done*); Pasiva con verbos ditransitivos |
| **Condicionales** | Tercer condicional (profundización); Condicionales mixtos avanzados (*If + past perfect, would + infinitive* / *If + past simple, would have + pp*); *Unless, provided that, as long as, in case* |
| **Subjuntivo** | *I wish / If only* (pasado, presente, futuro); *It's time + past*; *Would rather*; *As if / as though* + past subjunctive |
| **Inversión y Énfasis** | Inversión con adverbios negativos (*Never have I seen...*); *Only then, Not only... but also*; *Cleft sentences* (*It was Jesus who...* / *What I believe is...*) |
| **Gerundios/Infinitivos** | Gerundios e infinitivos pasivos (*being loved, to be loved*); Verb patterns avanzados (*consider doing, pretend to do*); Verbos con preposición + gerundio (*insist on, succeed in, apologize for*) |
| **Discurso Indirecto** | Reporting verbs avanzados (*claim, deny, admit, suggest, insist, warn, advise, persuade, encourage*); Backshifting con todos los tiempos; Preguntas indirectas complejas |
| **Conectores** | Conectores de adición (*moreover, furthermore, in addition, besides*); Contraste (*nevertheless, nonetheless, whereas, while, yet*); Causa/consecuencia (*consequently, as a result, owing to, due to*); Propósito (*with a view to, with the intention of*); Concesión (*albeit, notwithstanding*) |

---

## UNIDAD 1: TIEMPOS VERBALES AVANZADOS
*Lecciones 1 a 5*

---

### Lección 1 – "He Will Have Finished the Work"
**Gramática focal:** Future Perfect (*will have + past participle*) para acciones completadas antes de un momento futuro específico.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He will have finished the work that I have given him."* (Adaptado de Juan 17:4 – *"I have brought you glory on earth by finishing the work you gave me to do."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 17:1-5, ESV):** 
> *"When Jesus had spoken these words, he lifted up his eyes to heaven, and said, 'Father, the hour has come; glorify your Son that the Son may glorify you, since you have given him authority over all flesh, to give eternal life to all whom you have given him. And this is eternal life, that they know you the only true God, and Jesus Christ whom you have sent. I glorified you on earth, having accomplished the work that you gave me to do. And now, Father, glorify me in your own presence with the glory that I had with you before the world existed.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| glorify | glorificar | authority | autoridad |
| flesh | carne (humanidad) | eternal life | vida eterna |
| accomplished | cumplido / realizado | presence | presencia |
| existed | existió | | |

**Uso del Future Perfect:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *will have + past participle* | Acción completada antes de un punto específico en el futuro | *He **will have finished** the work by the time we arrive.* |
| *will not have + pp* | Negativa | *They **will not have heard** the news by then.* |
| *Will + sujeto + have + pp?* | Pregunta | ***Will** he **have completed** it by Friday?* |

**Línea del tiempo:**

| Momento | Evento |
|:---|:---|
| Ahora (presente) | Jesús ora, dice que ha cumplido la obra |
| Futuro (punto de referencia) | "El momento en que regrese" |
| Antes de ese punto | "Habrá terminado la obra" (Future Perfect) |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con Future Perfect:**

1. *"He **will have** **judged** the world in righteousness."* (Hechos 17:31, adaptado) – Juzgará al mundo con justicia (acción futura, pero podemos expresar como completada en el punto de referencia: *will have judged*).
2. *"They **will have** **heard** the gospel by then."* (Mateo 24:14, adaptado) – Habrán oído el evangelio para entonces.
3. *"The Son of Man **will have** **come** in his glory."* (Mateo 25:31, adaptado) – El Hijo del Hombre habrá venido en su gloria.
4. *"The Father **will have** **given** them to me."* (Juan 17:2, adaptado) – El Padre me los habrá dado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Usar Future Perfect para expresar logros futuros):**

- *By the time I finish this course, I **will have read** the entire Bible in English.* (Para cuando termine este curso, habré leído toda la Biblia en inglés.)
- *She **will have prayed** for one hour by the time he arrives.* (Ella habrá orado una hora para cuando él llegue.)
- *By next year, we **will have attended** the church for ten years.* (Para el año que viene, habremos asistido a la iglesia por diez años.)
- *He **will have finished** his theology studies by 2027.* (Él habrá terminado sus estudios de teología para 2027.)
- *They **will have planted** a thousand trees by the end of the project.* (Habrán plantado mil árboles para el final del proyecto.)

**Edificación:** Jesús habla de la obra que el Padre le dio. Él "cumple" (accomplished) la obra en la cruz, pero en el contexto de la oración, Jesús ya ve la obra como completada. Aprendemos a usar el Future Perfect para expresar confianza en que Dios completará su obra en nosotros.

---

### Lección 2 – "We Will Have Been Changed"
**Gramática focal:** Future Perfect Continuous (*will have been + -ing*) para acciones en progreso hasta un punto futuro.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"We will have been changed."* (Adaptado de 1 Corintios 15:52 – *"We shall all be changed, in a moment, in the twinkling of an eye"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Corintios 15:50-54, ESV):** 
> *"I tell you this, brothers: flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of God, nor does the perishable inherit the imperishable. Behold! I tell you a mystery. We shall not all sleep, but we shall all be changed, in a moment, in the twinkling of an eye, at the last trumpet. For the trumpet will sound, and the dead will be raised imperishable, and we shall be changed. For this perishable body must put on the imperishable, and this mortal body must put on immortality. When the perishable puts on the imperishable, and the mortal puts on immortality, then shall come to pass the saying that is written: 'Death is swallowed up in victory.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| inherit | heredar | perishable | perecedero |
| imperishable | imperecedero | mystery | misterio |
| trumpet | trompeta | raised | resucitado |
| mortal | mortal | immortality | inmortalidad |
| swallowed up | engullido | victory | victoria |

**Uso del Future Perfect Continuous:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *will have been + -ing* | Acción en curso hasta un punto futuro | *By then, she **will have been praying** for three hours.* |
| *will not have been + -ing* | Negativa | *He **won't have been waiting** long.* |
| *Will + sujeto + have been + -ing?* | Pregunta | ***Will** you **have been studying** long?* |

**Contraste: Future Perfect Simple vs Continuous**

| Tiempo | Enfoque | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *will have finished* | Acción completada | *He **will have finished** the work.* |
| *will have been working* | Duración/Progreso | *He **will have been working** for ten hours.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con Future Perfect Continuous (adaptados):**

1. *"The angels **will have been worshiping** for eternity."* (Apocalipsis 4:8, adaptado) – Los ángeles habrán estado adorando por la eternidad.
2. *"The saints **will have been reigning** with Christ for a thousand years."* (Apocalipsis 20:6, adaptado) – Los santos habrán estado reinando con Cristo por mil años.
3. *"The Lord **will have been** **patient** with us all along."* (2 Pedro 3:9, adaptado) – El Señor habrá sido paciente con nosotros todo el tiempo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *By the time we finish this unit, we **will have been studying** English for six months.* (Para cuando terminemos esta unidad, habremos estado estudiando inglés por seis meses.)
- *She **will have been serving** in the church for twenty years by next anniversary.* (Ella habrá estado sirviendo en la iglesia por veinte años para el próximo aniversario.)
- *He **will have been praying** for his family every day for a decade.* (Habrá estado orando por su familia todos los días por una década.)
- *I **will have been reading** the Bible for two hours by the time you arrive.* (Habré estado leyendo la Biblia por dos horas para cuando llegues.)
- *They **will have been** **waiting** for the Lord's return with hope.* (Habrán estado esperando el regreso del Señor con esperanza.)

**Edificación:** Pablo habla de un momento de transformación repentina. Aprendemos a usar el Future Perfect Continuous para hablar de la perseverancia en la fe hasta el día en que Cristo vuelva.

---

### Lección 3 – "He Had Been Teaching Them"
**Gramática focal:** Past Perfect Continuous (*had been + -ing*) para acciones continuas en el pasado con duración.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He had been teaching them for a long time."* (Adaptado de Lucas 19:47 – *"He was teaching daily in the temple"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Lucas 19:45-48, ESV):** 
> *"And he entered the temple and began to drive out those who sold, saying to them, 'It is written, "My house shall be a house of prayer," but you have made it a den of robbers.' And he was teaching daily in the temple. The chief priests and the scribes and the principal men of the people were seeking to destroy him, but they did not find anything they could do, for all the people were hanging on his words."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| entered | entró | drive out | expulsar |
| sold | vendían | den of robbers | cueva de ladrones |
| chief priests | sumos sacerdotes | scribes | escribas |
| seeking | buscando | destroy | destruir |
| hanging on | pendientes / aferrados | | |

**Uso del Past Perfect Continuous:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *had been + -ing* | Acción continua en el pasado con duración | *He **had been teaching** for hours when they came.* |
| *hadn't been + -ing* | Negativa | *She **hadn't been sleeping** well.* |
| *Had + sujeto + been + -ing?* | Pregunta | ***Had** he **been praying**?* |

**Contraste: Past Perfect Simple vs Continuous**

| Tiempo | Enfoque | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *had taught* | Acción completada | *He **had taught** them many things.* |
| *had been teaching* | Duración/Progreso | *He **had been teaching** them for hours.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con Past Perfect Continuous:**

1. *"They **had been waiting** for the Messiah for centuries."* (Lucas 2:25, adaptado) – Habían estado esperando al Mesías por siglos.
2. *"The disciples **had been arguing** about who was the greatest."* (Marcos 9:33-34, adaptado) – Los discípulos habían estado discutiendo quién era el más grande.
3. *"Jesus **had been healing** the sick all day."* (Marcos 1:32-34, adaptado) – Jesús había estado sanando a los enfermos todo el día.
4. *"Moses **had been leading** the people for forty years."* (Deuteronomio 8:2, adaptado) – Moisés había estado guiando al pueblo por cuarenta años.
5. *"The prophets **had been speaking** God's word."* (Hebreos 1:1, adaptado) – Los profetas habían estado hablando la palabra de Dios.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Expresar duración de acciones pasadas):**

- *I **had been praying** for two hours before I received the answer.* (Había estado orando por dos horas antes de recibir la respuesta.)
- *She **had been reading** the Bible for years before she truly understood it.* (Había estado leyendo la Biblia por años antes de entenderla realmente.)
- *We **had been waiting** for the pastor to arrive.* (Habíamos estado esperando a que llegara el pastor.)
- *He **had been struggling** with doubt before he found faith.* (Había estado luchando con dudas antes de encontrar la fe.)
- *They **had been serving** in the church for decades.* (Habían estado sirviendo en la iglesia por décadas.)

**Edificación:** Jesús enseñaba diariamente en el templo. Aprendemos a usar el Past Perfect Continuous para hablar de la perseverancia en la enseñanza, la oración y el servicio a lo largo del tiempo.

---

### Lección 4 – "Before Abraham Was, I Am"
**Gramática focal:** Contrastes temporales avanzados: Past Simple vs. Past Perfect vs. Present.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Before Abraham was, I am."* — **Juan 8:58**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 8:52-59, ESV):** 
> *"The Jews said to him, 'Now we know that you have a demon! Abraham died, as did the prophets, yet you say, "If anyone keeps my word, he will never taste death." Are you greater than our father Abraham, who died? And the prophets died! Who do you make yourself out to be?' Jesus answered, 'If I glorify myself, my glory is nothing. It is my Father who glorifies me, of whom you say, "He is our God." But you have not known him. I know him. If I were to say that I do not know him, I would be a liar like you. But I do know him and I keep his word. Your father Abraham rejoiced that he would see my day. He saw it and was glad.' So the Jews said to him, 'You are not yet fifty years old, and have you seen Abraham?' Jesus said to them, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, before Abraham was, I am.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| demon | demonio | prophets | profetas |
| taste death | probar muerte | greater | más grande |
| glorify | glorificar | liar | mentiroso |
| rejoiced | se regocijó | glad | contento |

**Línea del tiempo (Contraste de tiempos):**

| Tiempo verbal | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Present Simple** | Verdad eterna | *I **am**.* |
| **Past Simple** | Evento completado en el pasado | *Abraham **was**.* |
| **Past Perfect** | Evento anterior a otro en el pasado | *He **had rejoiced**.* |

**El "Yo Soy" (I Am) de Jesús:**
Jesús usa el Present Simple "I am" para referirse a su existencia eterna, en contraste con el pasado de Abraham. Esta es una declaración de divinidad que conecta con el nombre de Dios en Éxodo 3:14.

**Más ejemplos bíblicos de contrastes temporales:**

1. *"He **was** in the world, and the world **was** made through him, yet the world **did not know** him."* (Juan 1:10) – Contraste entre la creación (pasado) y el desconocimiento (pasado).
2. *"Before I **formed** you in the womb, I **knew** you."* (Jeremías 1:5) – Past Perfect implícito: antes de formar, ya conocía.
3. *"I **have come** that they **may have** life."* (Juan 10:10) – Presente perfecto (acción reciente) + presente (resultado).

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Contrastar tiempos en narración):**

- *Before I **became** a Christian, I **had not known** God's love.* (Antes de hacerme cristiano, no había conocido el amor de Dios.)
- *I **have been** a believer for ten years now, but before that I **was** an atheist.* (He sido creyente por diez años, pero antes era ateo.)
- *When I **was** young, I **did not** understand the Bible, but now I **read** it every day.* (Cuando era joven, no entendía la Biblia, pero ahora la leo cada día.)
- *She **had been praying** for years before she **saw** the answer.* (Había estado orando por años antes de ver la respuesta.)
- *They **will have** **completed** the project by the time we **arrive**.* (Habrán completado el proyecto para cuando lleguemos.)

**Edificación:** Jesús declara su eternidad: "Antes que Abraham fuese, yo soy". Aprendemos a usar los contrastes temporales para expresar la naturaleza eterna de Dios y nuestra propia historia de fe.

---

### Lección 5 – Repaso: "The One Who Will Come"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de Future Perfect, Future Perfect Continuous y Past Perfect Continuous.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The one who will come has already been prepared."* (Adaptado de Apocalipsis 1:8 – *"I am the Alpha and the Omega... who is and who was and who is to come"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Apocalipsis 1:1-8, ESV):** 
> *"The revelation of Jesus Christ, which God gave him to show to his servants the things that must soon take place. He made it known by sending his angel to his servant John, who bore witness to the word of God and to the testimony of Jesus Christ, even to all that he saw. Blessed is the one who reads aloud the words of this prophecy, and blessed are those who hear, and who keep what is written in it, for the time is near. John to the seven churches that are in Asia: Grace to you and peace from him who is and who was and who is to come, and from the seven spirits who are before his throne, and from Jesus Christ the faithful witness, the firstborn of the dead, and the ruler of kings on earth. To him who loves us and has freed us from our sins by his blood and made us a kingdom, priests to his God and Father, to him be glory and dominion forever and ever. Amen. Behold, he is coming with the clouds, and every eye will see him, even those who pierced him, and all tribes of the earth will wail on account of him. Even so. Amen. 'I am the Alpha and the Omega,' says the Lord God, 'who is and who was and who is to come, the Almighty.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| revelation | revelación | servants | siervos |
| soon | pronto | bore witness | dio testimonio |
| testimony | testimonio | blessed | bienaventurado |
| prophecy | profecía | grace | gracia |
| peace | paz | throne | trono |
| faithful | fiel | witness | testigo |
| firstborn | primogénito | ruler | gobernante |
| freed | liberado | blood | sangre |
| dominion | dominio | forever | para siempre |
| clouds | nubes | pierced | traspasaron |
| tribes | tribus | wail | lamentar |
| Alpha | Alfa (primera letra griega) | Omega | Omega (última) |
| Almighty | Todopoderoso | | |

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 8 oraciones usando cada una de las siguientes estructuras:

1. **Future Perfect** (*will have + pp*) – *By the time Jesus returns, the gospel **will have been** preached to all nations.*
2. **Future Perfect Continuous** (*will have been + -ing*) – *The angels **will have been** worshiping for all eternity.*
3. **Past Perfect Continuous** (*had been + -ing*) – *Before John wrote the Revelation, he **had been** in exile for many years.*
4. **Past Perfect** (*had + pp*) – *He **had seen** the vision before he wrote it down.*
5. **Contraste temporal** – *Before I **was** saved, I **had not known** the truth, but now I **have** peace.*

---

## UNIDAD 2: VOZ PASIVA AVANZADA
*Lecciones 6 a 10*

---

### Lección 6 – "He Must Have Been Crucified"
**Gramática focal:** Voz pasiva con modales en pasado (*must have been done, might have been done, should have been done, could have been done*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He must have been crucified."* (Adaptado de Hechos 2:23 – *"You put him to death by nailing him to the cross"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 2:22-24, ESV):** 
> *"Men of Israel, hear these words: Jesus of Nazareth, a man attested to you by God with mighty works and wonders and signs that God did through him in your midst, as you yourselves know—this Jesus, delivered up according to the definite plan and foreknowledge of God, you crucified and killed by the hands of lawless men. God raised him up, loosing the pangs of death, because it was not possible for him to be held by it."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| attested | atestiguado / confirmado | midst | medio / entre |
| delivered up | entregado | definite | definitivo / determinado |
| foreknowledge | presciencia | lawless | sin ley / inicuos |
| loosing | soltando | pangs | dolores / angustias |
| held | retenido | | |

**Voz pasiva con modales en pasado:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *must have been + pp* | Certeza (95%) – deducción lógica | *He **must have been crucified**.* |
| *might have been + pp* | Posibilidad (40-60%) | *He **might have been** the Messiah.* |
| *may have been + pp* | Posibilidad (50%) | *He **may have been** buried.* |
| *could have been + pp* | Posibilidad/Capacidad (70%) | *He **could have been saved**.* |
| *should have been + pp* | Obligación no cumplida | *He **should have been** honored.* |
| *would have been + pp* | Resultado hipotético | *He **would have been** killed.* |
| *can't have been + pp* | Certeza negativa (95%) | *He **can't have been** the one.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **must have been** the Son of God."* (Mateo 27:54, adaptado) – Debía haber sido el Hijo de Dios.
2. *"The tomb **should have been** guarded."* (Mateo 27:65, adaptado) – La tumba debería haber sido guardada.
3. *"The cross **could have been** avoided."* (Mateo 26:53, adaptado) – La cruz podría haber sido evitada.
4. *"The prophecies **might have been** fulfilled."* (Lucas 24:25-27, adaptado) – Las profecías podrían haber sido cumplidas.
5. *"The message **must have been** proclaimed."* (Romanos 10:14-15, adaptado) – El mensaje debió haber sido proclamado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **must have been** praying before the exam.* (Debe haber estado orando antes del examen.)
- *She **might have been** saved by grace.* (Puede haber sido salvada por gracia.)
- *The church **should have been** built nearer the city.* (La iglesia debería haber sido construida más cerca de la ciudad.)
- *The book **could have been** written by Paul.* (El libro podría haber sido escrito por Pablo.)
- *They **can't have been** the ones who lied.* (No pueden haber sido ellos los que mintieron.)

**Edificación:** Pedro declara que Jesús fue crucificado según el plan de Dios. Aprendemos a usar modales en pasiva para expresar certeza, posibilidad y obligación sobre eventos pasados en la historia de la salvación.

---

### Lección 7 – "He Is Said to Have Risen"
**Gramática focal:** Voz pasiva con reporting verbs (*is said to, is believed to, is thought to, is reported to, is known to*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He is said to have risen from the dead."* (Adaptado de Lucas 24:34 – *"The Lord has risen indeed!"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Lucas 24:13-35, extracto):** 
> *"That very day two of them were going to a village named Emmaus, about seven miles from Jerusalem, and they were talking with each other about all these things that had happened. While they were talking and discussing together, Jesus himself drew near and went with them. But their eyes were kept from recognizing him. And he said to them, 'What is this conversation that you are holding with each other as you walk?' And they stood still, looking sad. Then one of them, named Cleopas, answered him, 'Are you the only visitor to Jerusalem who does not know the things that have happened there in these days?' And he said to them, 'What things?' And they said to him, 'Concerning Jesus of Nazareth, a man who was a prophet mighty in deed and word before God and all the people, and how our chief priests and rulers delivered him up to be condemned to death, and crucified him. But we had hoped that he was the one to redeem Israel. Yes, and besides all this, it is now the third day since these things happened. Moreover, some women of our company amazed us. They were at the tomb early in the morning, and when they did not find his body, they came back saying that they had even seen a vision of angels, who said that he was alive.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| village | aldea | discussing | discutiendo |
| drew near | se acercó | recognizing | reconociendo |
| stood still | se detuvieron | sad | triste |
| visitor | visitante | prophet | profeta |
| redeem | redimir | amazed | asombrados |
| vision | visión | alive | vivo |

**Voz pasiva con reporting verbs (estructura personal):**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *He is said to + infinitive* | Se dice que él... | *He **is said to have risen**.* |
| *He is believed to + infinitive* | Se cree que él... | *He **is believed to be** the Messiah.* |
| *He is thought to + infinitive* | Se piensa que él... | *He **is thought to have** **written** the letter.* |
| *He is reported to + infinitive* | Se reporta que él... | *He **is reported to have** **died**.* |
| *He is known to + infinitive* | Se sabe que él... | *He **is known to have** **healed**.* |

**Estructura impersonal (It is said that...):**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *It is said that + cláusula* | ***It is said that** he rose from the dead.* |
| *It is believed that + cláusula* | ***It is believed that** Jesus is the Son of God.* |
| *It is thought that + cláusula* | ***It is thought that** he wrote the Gospel.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **is believed to have** been the Son of God."* (Juan 20:31, adaptado) – Se cree que él fue el Hijo de Dios.
2. *"They **are known to have** followed Jesus."* (Hechos 4:13, adaptado) – Se sabe que ellos siguieron a Jesús.
3. *"The tomb **is reported to have** been empty."* (Mateo 28:11-15, adaptado) – Se reporta que la tumba estaba vacía.
4. *"The apostles **are said to have** preached boldly."* (Hechos 4:31, adaptado) – Se dice que los apóstoles predicaron con valentía.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **is said to have** read the entire Bible.* (Se dice que él ha leído toda la Biblia.)
- *She **is believed to have** been healed by God.* (Se cree que ella fue sanada por Dios.)
- *The church **is thought to have** been built in 1990.* (Se piensa que la iglesia fue construida en 1990.)
- *They **are reported to have** seen a miracle.* (Se reporta que ellos vieron un milagro.)
- *Paul **is known to have** written many letters.* (Se sabe que Pablo escribió muchas cartas.)
- ***It is said that** Jesus rose from the dead.* (Se dice que Jesús resucitó de entre los muertos.)

**Edificación:** Los discípulos en el camino a Emaús reportaron: "¡Se dice que Jesús ha resucitado!". Aprendemos a usar la voz pasiva con reporting verbs para hablar de lo que se cree, se sabe y se reporta sobre la fe cristiana.

---

### Lección 8 – "He Was Given Authority"
**Gramática focal:** Voz pasiva con verbos ditransitivos (dos objetos) – *give, send, show, tell, offer, promise, teach*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He was given authority, glory, and sovereign power."* — **Daniel 7:14**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Daniel 7:13-14, ESV):** 
> *"I saw in the night visions, and behold, with the clouds of heaven there came one like a son of man, and he came to the Ancient of Days and was presented before him. And to him was given dominion and glory and a kingdom, that all peoples, nations, and languages should serve him; his dominion is an everlasting dominion, which shall not pass away, and his kingdom one that shall not be destroyed."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| visions | visiones | behold | he aquí |
| Ancient of Days | Anciano de Días | presented | presentado |
| dominion | dominio | glory | gloria |
| kingdom | reino | peoples | pueblos |
| nations | naciones | languages | lenguas |
| everlasting | eterno | pass away | pasar / desaparecer |
| destroyed | destruido | | |

**Voz pasiva con verbos ditransitivos:**

| Verbo | Activa (dos objetos) | Pasiva (Objeto directo como sujeto) | Pasiva (Objeto indirecto como sujeto) |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *give* | *God gave **us** a promise.* | *A promise **was given to us**.* | *We **were given** a promise.* |
| *send* | *God sent **them** a prophet.* | *A prophet **was sent to them**.* | *They **were sent** a prophet.* |
| *show* | *He showed **me** the vision.* | *The vision **was shown to me**.* | *I **was shown** the vision.* |
| *tell* | *He told **us** the parable.* | *The parable **was told to us**.* | *We **were told** the parable.* |
| *offer* | *He offered **them** salvation.* | *Salvation **was offered to them**.* | *They **were offered** salvation.* |
| *promise* | *God promised **Abraham** a son.* | *A son **was promised to Abraham**.* | *Abraham **was promised** a son.* |
| *teach* | *He taught **the disciples** a lesson.* | *A lesson **was taught to the disciples**.* | *The disciples **were taught** a lesson.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"The law **was given** to Moses."* (Juan 1:17) – La ley fue dada a Moisés.
2. *"The disciples **were told** to wait."* (Hechos 1:4) – A los discípulos se les dijo que esperaran.
3. *"We **have been given** the Holy Spirit."* (Romanos 5:5) – Se nos ha dado el Espíritu Santo.
4. *"The kingdom **was promised** to Abraham."* (Gálatas 3:29, adaptado) – El reino fue prometido a Abraham.
5. *"They **were shown** the way."* (Mateo 2:9-10, adaptado) – Se les mostró el camino.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **was given** a Bible for my birthday.* (Me dieron una Biblia para mi cumpleaños.)
- *We **were told** to pray without ceasing.* (Se nos dijo que oráramos sin cesar.)
- *She **was sent** a message of hope.* (Le fue enviado un mensaje de esperanza.)
- *The truth **was shown** to me.* (La verdad me fue mostrada.)
- *They **were offered** forgiveness.* (Se les ofreció perdón.)
- *A great promise **was given** to us.* (Una gran promesa nos fue dada.)

**Edificación:** Daniel vio que al Hijo del Hombre le fue dado dominio, gloria y un reino. Aprendemos a usar la voz pasiva con verbos ditransitivos para expresar lo que se nos ha dado, mostrado y prometido en la fe.

---

### Lección 9 – "Being Led by the Spirit"
**Gramática focal:** Pasiva con gerundios e infinitivos (*being + pp, to be + pp, having been + pp*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Being led by the Spirit, Jesus went into the wilderness."* (Adaptado de Mateo 4:1 – *"Then Jesus was led by the Spirit into the wilderness"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 4:1-11, ESV, extracto):** 
> *"Then Jesus was led up by the Spirit into the wilderness to be tempted by the devil. And after fasting forty days and forty nights, he was hungry. And the tempter came and said to him, 'If you are the Son of God, command these stones to become loaves of bread.' But he answered, 'It is written, "Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word that comes from the mouth of God."' Then the devil took him to the holy city and set him on the pinnacle of the temple and said to him, 'If you are the Son of God, throw yourself down, for it is written, "He will command his angels concerning you," and "On their hands they will bear you up, lest you strike your foot against a stone."' Jesus said to him, 'Again it is written, "You shall not put the Lord your God to the test."' Again, the devil took him to a very high mountain and showed him all the kingdoms of the world and their glory. And he said to him, 'All these I will give you, if you will fall down and worship me.' Then Jesus said to him, 'Be gone, Satan! For it is written, "You shall worship the Lord your God and him only shall you serve."' Then the devil left him, and behold, angels came and were ministering to him."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| wilderness | desierto | tempted | tentado |
| fasting | ayunando | hungry | hambriento |
| tempter | tentador | command | ordenar |
| stones | piedras | loaves | panes |
| pinnacle | pináculo | throw yourself | tirarte |
| angels | ángeles | ministering | sirviendo / ministrando |

**Pasiva con gerundios e infinitivos:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Being + pp* | Pasiva como gerundio (acción pasiva en progreso) | ***Being led** by the Spirit, Jesus went...* |
| *To be + pp* | Pasiva como infinitivo | *He went **to be tempted**.* |
| *Having been + pp* | Pasiva como gerundio perfectivo (acción completada) | ***Having been led** by the Spirit, he...* |
| *to have been + pp* | Pasiva perfectiva como infinitivo | *He is said **to have been tempted**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Being filled** with the Holy Spirit, they spoke boldly."* (Hechos 4:31, adaptado) – Siendo llenos del Espíritu Santo, hablaron con valentía.
2. *"He came **to be baptized** by John."* (Mateo 3:13) – Vino para ser bautizado por Juan.
3. *"**Having been justified** by faith, we have peace with God."* (Romanos 5:1) – Habiendo sido justificados por la fe, tenemos paz con Dios.
4. *"They are **to be saved** through faith."* (Efesios 2:8, adaptado) – Ellos son para ser salvos por fe.
5. *"**Being persecuted**, we are not abandoned."* (2 Corintios 4:9, adaptado) – Siendo perseguidos, no somos abandonados.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Pasiva con gerundios e infinitivos):**

- ***Being saved** by grace, I have peace.* (Siendo salvado por gracia, tengo paz.)
- *He came **to be healed** by Jesus.* (Vino para ser sanado por Jesús.)
- ***Having been forgiven**, I forgive others.* (Habiendo sido perdonado, perdono a otros.)
- *They are **to be taught** the truth.* (Ellos son para ser enseñados en la verdad.)
- ***Being led** by God, I follow his path.* (Siendo guiado por Dios, sigo su camino.)
- *The church is **to be built** on the rock.* (La iglesia es para ser edificada sobre la roca.)

**Edificación:** Jesús fue guiado por el Espíritu al desierto para ser tentado. Aprendemos a usar la voz pasiva con gerundios e infinitivos para hablar del proceso de ser guiado, ser probado y ser fortalecido en la fe.

---

### Lección 10 – Repaso: "It Is Written"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de todos los tipos de voz pasiva.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"It is written: 'Man shall not live by bread alone.'"* — **Mateo 4:4**

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes formas de voz pasiva sobre la vida de Jesús.

**Ejemplo:**
- *Jesus **was born** in Bethlehem.* (Pasado simple)
- *He **was led** by the Spirit into the wilderness.* (Pasado simple)
- *He **was tempted** by the devil.* (Pasado simple)
- *He **must have been** the Son of God.* (Modal + pasiva)
- *He **is believed to have** healed the sick.* (Reporting verb + pasiva)
- *He **was given** authority by the Father.* (Ditransitivo)
- ***Being baptized**, he received the Holy Spirit.* (Gerundio pasivo)
- *He came **to be crucified**.* (Infinitivo pasivo)
- ***Having been raised**, he appeared to his disciples.* (Gerundio perfectivo)
- *The gospel **is preached** to all nations.* (Presente pasiva)

---

## UNIDAD 3: CONDICIONALES MIXTOS Y SUBJUNTIVO
*Lecciones 11 a 15*

---

### Lección 11 – "If I Had Not Come"
**Gramática focal:** Tercer condicional (profundización) – *If + past perfect, would have + past participle*; uso de *could have, might have* en el resultado.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"If I had not come and spoken to them, they would not have been guilty of sin."* — **Juan 15:22**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 15:18-25, ESV, extracto):** 
> *"If the world hates you, know that it has hated me before it hated you. If you were of the world, the world would love you as its own; but because you are not of the world, but I chose you out of the world, therefore the world hates you. Remember the word that I said to you: 'A servant is not greater than his master.' If they persecuted me, they will also persecute you. If they kept my word, they will also keep yours. But all these things they will do to you on account of my name, because they do not know him who sent me. If I had not come and spoken to them, they would not have been guilty of sin, but now they have no excuse for their sin. Whoever hates me hates my Father also. If I had not done among them the works that no one else did, they would not have been guilty of sin, but now they have seen and hated both me and my Father. But the word that is written in their Law must be fulfilled: 'They hated me without a cause.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| hates | odia | chose | escogió |
| persecuted | perseguido | account of | por causa de |
| excuse | excusa | guilty | culpable |
| works | obras | fulfilled | cumplido |
| without a cause | sin causa | | |

**Tercer condicional (repaso y profundización):**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *If + past perfect, would have + pp* | Situación hipotética en el pasado | *If I **had not come**, they **would not have** been guilty.* |
| *If + past perfect, could have + pp* | Capacidad pasada no utilizada | *If they **had listened**, they **could have** believed.* |
| *If + past perfect, might have + pp* | Posibilidad pasada | *If he **had known**, he **might have helped**.* |
| *If + past perfect, should have + pp* | Obligación pasada no cumplida | *If we **had prayed**, we **should have seen**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos de tercer condicional:**

1. *"If you **had known** me, you **would have known** my Father."* (Juan 14:7) – Si me hubierais conocido, habríais conocido a mi Padre.
2. *"If I **had not done** the works, they **would not have** **believed**."* (Juan 10:37-38, adaptado) – Si no hubiera hecho las obras, no habrían creído.
3. *"If they **had understood** the Scriptures, they **would not have** crucified the Lord."* (1 Corintios 2:8) – Si hubieran entendido las Escrituras, no habrían crucificado al Señor.
4. *"If we **had repented**, we **would have been** forgiven."* (Hechos 3:19, adaptado) – Si nos hubiéramos arrepentido, habríamos sido perdonados.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Arrepentimiento y reflexión):**

- *If I **had prayed** more, I **would have** had more peace.* (Si hubiera orado más, habría tenido más paz.)
- *If she **had listened** to the advice, she **might have** avoided the mistake.* (Si hubiera escuchado el consejo, podría haber evitado el error.)
- *If we **had trusted** God, we **could have** avoided many problems.* (Si hubiéramos confiado en Dios, podríamos haber evitado muchos problemas.)
- *If he **had known** the truth, he **wouldn't have** left.* (Si hubiera conocido la verdad, no se habría ido.)
- *If they **had been** more faithful, they **would have seen** more miracles.* (Si hubieran sido más fieles, habrían visto más milagros.)

**Edificación:** Jesús dice que si no hubiera venido y hablado, no tendrían pecado. Aprendemos a usar el tercer condicional para reflexionar sobre cómo la revelación de Dios nos hace responsables y cómo la fe responde a su gracia.

---

### Lección 12 – "If We Had Not Believed"
**Gramática focal:** Condicionales mixtos avanzados (condición en pasado, resultado en presente; condición en presente, resultado en pasado).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"If we had not believed, we would not be saved today."* (Adaptado de Romanos 10:9-10)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 10:8-15, ESV):** 
> *"But what does it say? 'The word is near you, in your mouth and in your heart' (that is, the word of faith that we proclaim); because, if you confess with your mouth that Jesus is Lord and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead, you will be saved. For with the heart one believes and is justified, and with the mouth one confesses and is saved. For the Scripture says, 'Everyone who believes in him will not be put to shame.' For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek; for the same Lord is Lord of all, bestowing his riches on all who call on him. For 'everyone who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved.' How then will they call on him in whom they have not believed? And how are they to believe in him of whom they have never heard? And how are they to hear without someone preaching? And how are they to preach unless they are sent? As it is written, 'How beautiful are the feet of those who preach the good news!'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| confess | confesar | justify | justificar |
| put to shame | avergonzado | distinction | distinción |
| bestowing | otorgando | riches | riquezas |
| call on | invocar | preach | predicar |
| sent | enviado | beautiful | hermosos |
| feet | pies | good news | buenas noticias |

**Condicionales mixtos:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *If + past perfect, would + infinitive* | Condición pasada → Resultado presente | *If we **had not believed**, we **would not be** saved today.* |
| *If + past simple, would have + pp* | Condición presente → Resultado pasado | *If I **were** more faithful, I **would have seen** more.* |
| *If + past perfect, would be + -ing* | Condición pasada → Resultado presente continuo | *If he **had obeyed**, he **would be living** in peace.* |

**Más ejemplos de condicionales mixtos:**

1. *"If I **had known** the truth, I **would be** a different person now."* (Juan 8:32, adaptado) – Si hubiera conocido la verdad, sería una persona diferente ahora.
2. *"If they **had believed** in me, they **would have** eternal life."* (Juan 3:16, adaptado) – Si hubieran creído en mí, tendrían vida eterna.
3. *"If we **were** stronger in faith, we **would have** overcome earlier."* (Mateo 17:20, adaptado) – Si fuéramos más fuertes en fe, habríamos vencido antes.
4. *"If Jesus **had not died**, we **would be** lost."* (Romanos 5:8-9, adaptado) – Si Jesús no hubiera muerto, estaríamos perdidos.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Condicionales mixtos):**

- *If I **had studied** theology, I **would be** a pastor now.* (Si hubiera estudiado teología, sería pastor ahora.)
- *If she **were** more patient, she **would have** waited.* (Si fuera más paciente, habría esperado.)
- *If we **had prayed** more, we **would** not **be** so anxious.* (Si hubiéramos orado más, no estaríamos tan ansiosos.)
- *If he **had listened** to God, he **would have** peace.* (Si hubiera escuchado a Dios, tendría paz.)
- *If they **were** true disciples, they **would have** followed his teachings.* (Si fueran verdaderos discípulos, habrían seguido sus enseñanzas.)

**Edificación:** Pablo explica que la salvación viene por la fe. Aprendemos a usar condicionales mixtos para expresar cómo decisiones pasadas afectan nuestro presente y cómo nuestro carácter presente refleja el pasado.

---

### Lección 13 – "I Wish I Had Known"
**Gramática focal:** *I wish / If only* para expresar deseos en pasado, presente y futuro; *It's time* + pasado.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I wish I had known the truth earlier."* (Adaptado de Juan 8:32 – *"You will know the truth, and the truth will set you free."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 8:31-36, ESV):** 
> *"So Jesus said to the Jews who had believed him, 'If you abide in my word, you are truly my disciples, and you will know the truth, and the truth will set you free.' They answered him, 'We are offspring of Abraham and have never been enslaved to anyone. How is it that you say, "You will become free"?' Jesus answered them, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, everyone who practices sin is a slave to sin. The slave does not remain in the house forever; the son remains forever. So if the Son sets you free, you will be free indeed.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| abide | permanecer | truly | verdaderamente |
| disciples | discípulos | set free | liberar |
| offspring | descendencia | enslaved | esclavizado |
| practices | practica | slave | esclavo |
| remain | permanecer | indeed | ciertamente |

**Estructura de *I wish* y *If only*:**

| Tiempo | Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **Pasado** | *wish + past perfect* | Deseo sobre el pasado (arrepentimiento) | *I wish I **had known**.* |
| **Presente** | *wish + past simple* | Deseo sobre el presente (situación irreal) | *I wish I **were** free.* |
| **Futuro** | *wish + would + infinitivo* | Deseo sobre el futuro (queja o esperanza) | *I wish he **would** come.* |
| **Pasado (enfático)** | *If only + past perfect* | Deseo enfático sobre el pasado | *If only I **had believed**!* |

**Uso de *It's time* + past:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *It's time + past simple* | Es hora de que... | ***It's time** we **prayed**.* |
| *It's about time + past simple* | Ya es hora de que... | ***It's about time** we **changed**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con deseos:**

1. *"I wish you **had listened** to me!"* (Deuteronomio 5:29, adaptado) – ¡Ojalá me hubierais escuchado!
2. *"If only we **had remained** in Egypt!"* (Éxodo 16:3) – ¡Ojalá nos hubiéramos quedado en Egipto!
3. *"I wish they **would** know me."* (Oseas 5:4, adaptado) – Ojalá me conocieran.
4. *"If only I **were** like before!"* (Job 29:2) – ¡Ojalá fuera como antes!

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Expresar deseos y arrepentimiento):**

- *I wish I **had read** the Bible earlier.* (Ojalá hubiera leído la Biblia antes.)
- *I wish I **were** more faithful.* (Ojalá fuera más fiel.)
- *I wish she **would** come to church.* (Ojalá ella viniera a la iglesia.)
- *If only we **had prayed** more.* (¡Ojalá hubiéramos orado más!)
- *It's time we **repented**.* (Es hora de que nos arrepintamos.)
- *It's about time we **started** serving.* (Ya es hora de que empecemos a servir.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos dice: "Conoceréis la verdad, y la verdad os hará libres". Aprendemos a usar "I wish" para expresar nuestro deseo de haber conocido la verdad antes, y para pedir a Dios que otros también la conozcan.

---

### Lección 14 – "He Acts as If He Were God"
**Gramática focal:** *As if / as though* + subjuntivo pasado; *would rather* + pasado; *I suggest that he + subjuntivo* (presente).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He acts as if he were God."* (Adaptado de Juan 5:18 – *"He was even calling God his own Father, making himself equal with God."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 5:17-24, ESV):** 
> *"But Jesus answered them, 'My Father is working until now, and I am working.' This was why the Jews were seeking all the more to kill him, because not only was he breaking the Sabbath, but he was even calling God his own Father, making himself equal with God. So Jesus said to them, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, the Son can do nothing of his own accord, but only what he sees the Father doing. For whatever the Father does, that the Son does likewise. For the Father loves the Son and shows him all that he himself is doing. And greater works than these will he show him, so that you may marvel. For as the Father raises the dead and gives them life, so also the Son gives life to whom he will. For the Father judges no one, but has given all judgment to the Son, that all may honor the Son, just as they honor the Father. Whoever does not honor the Son does not honor the Father who sent him. Truly, truly, I say to you, whoever hears my word and believes him who sent me has eternal life. He does not come into judgment, but has passed from death to life.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| seeking | buscando | breaking | quebrantando |
| Sabbath | Sábado | own accord | propia iniciativa |
| likewise | igualmente | marvel | maravillarse |
| raises | resucita | judges | juzga |
| judgment | juicio | honor | honrar |
| passed | pasado | death | muerte |

**Estructuras de *as if / as though*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *as if + past simple* | Situación irreal en el presente | *He acts **as if he were** God.* |
| *as if + past perfect* | Situación irreal en el pasado | *She looked **as if she had seen** a ghost.* |
| *as if + present* | Situación posible (real) | *He looks **as if he is** tired.* |

**Uso de *would rather*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *would rather + past simple* | Preferencia sobre el presente/futuro (con otra persona) | *I **would rather** you **came** early.* |
| *would rather + infinitive* | Preferencia del sujeto | *I **would rather** **pray**.* |
| *would rather have + pp* | Preferencia sobre el pasado | *I **would rather have** **gone**.* |

**Subjuntivo presente en que-cláusulas:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *I suggest that + sujeto + base form* | Sugerencia formal | *I suggest that he **pray**.* |
| *It is important that + sujeto + base form* | Importancia | *It is important that we **believe**.* |
| *They insist that + sujeto + base form* | Insistencia | *They insist that he **come**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He spoke **as if he were** the Messiah."* (Juan 4:25-26, adaptado) – Habló como si fuera el Mesías.
2. *"I **would rather** you **believed**."* (Juan 6:29, adaptado) – Preferiría que creyerais.
3. *"It is important that we **love** one another."* (Juan 15:12, adaptado) – Es importante que nos amemos unos a otros.
4. *"She acted **as though she had seen** an angel."* (Hechos 12:13-15, adaptado) – Actuó como si hubiera visto un ángel.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He preaches **as if he were** an apostle.* (Predica como si fuera un apóstol.)
- *She prays **as though she had** known God for years.* (Ora como si conociera a Dios por años.)
- *I **would rather** you **prayed** with me.* (Preferiría que oraras conmigo.)
- *I suggest that we **read** the Bible together.* (Sugiero que leamos la Biblia juntos.)
- *It is essential that everyone **believes** in him.* (Es esencial que todos crean en él.)
- *He looks **as if he had seen** a miracle.* (Parece como si hubiera visto un milagro.)

**Edificación:** Jesús actuó y habló como si fuera igual a Dios, porque Él lo es. Aprendemos a usar estas estructuras para expresar cómo percibimos la fe y cómo sugerimos acciones espirituales.

---

### Lección 15 – Repaso: "I Wish You Would Believe"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de condicionales mixtos, *wish*, *if only*, *as if*, *would rather*, subjuntivo.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I wish you would believe."* (Adaptado de Juan 6:36 – *"You have seen me and yet do not believe."*)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes estructuras de esta unidad.

**Ejemplo:**
- *If I **had known** the truth, I **would have** believed earlier.* (Tercer condicional)
- *If I **had believed**, I **would be** saved now.* (Mixto)
- *I wish I **had prayed** more.* (*wish* + pasado)
- *If only we **had listened**!* (*If only* + pasado)
- *I wish he **would** come to church.* (*wish* + futuro)
- *He acts **as if he were** a saint.* (*as if* + presente)
- *She looked **as though she had seen** Jesus.* (*as if* + pasado)
- *I **would rather** you **prayed** with us.* (*would rather*)
- *I suggest that he **repent**.* (Subjuntivo)
- *It is time we **confessed** our sins.* (*It's time* + pasado)

---

## UNIDAD 4: INVERSIÓN Y ESTRUCTURAS ENFÁTICAS
*Lecciones 16 a 20*

---

### Lección 16 – "Never Have I Seen Such Faith"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión con adverbios negativos (*never, seldom, rarely, hardly, scarcely, no sooner... than, not only... but also*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Never have I seen such faith in Israel."* (Adaptado de Mateo 8:10 – *"I have not found anyone in Israel with such great faith."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 8:5-13, ESV):** 
> *"When he had entered Capernaum, a centurion came forward to him, appealing to him, 'Lord, my servant is lying paralyzed at home, suffering terribly.' And he said to him, 'I will come and heal him.' But the centurion replied, 'Lord, I am not worthy to have you come under my roof, but only say the word, and my servant will be healed. For I too am a man under authority, with soldiers under me. And I say to one, "Go," and he goes, and to another, "Come," and he comes, and to my servant, "Do this," and he does it.' When Jesus heard this, he marveled and said to those who followed him, 'Truly, I tell you, with no one in Israel have I found such faith. I tell you, many will come from east and west and recline at table with Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob in the kingdom of heaven, while the sons of the kingdom will be thrown into the outer darkness. In that place there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.' And to the centurion Jesus said, 'Go; let it be done for you as you have believed.' And the servant was healed at that very hour."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| centurion | centurión | appealing | suplicando |
| paralyzed | paralizado | suffering | sufriendo |
| worthy | digno | roof | techo |
| authority | autoridad | soldiers | soldados |
| marveled | se maravilló | recline at table | reclinarse a la mesa |
| outer darkness | tinieblas exteriores | weeping | llanto |
| gnashing | crujir | | |

**Inversión con adverbios negativos:**

| Adverbio | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Never* | *Never + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Never have I seen** such faith.* |
| *Seldom* | *Seldom + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Seldom have we seen** miracles.* |
| *Rarely* | *Rarely + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Rarely does he pray** in public.* |
| *Hardly / Scarcely* | *Hardly + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Hardly had he spoken** when...* |
| *No sooner... than* | *No sooner + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + than* | ***No sooner had he said it than**...* |
| *Not only... but also* | *Not only + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + but also* | ***Not only did he heal** the sick, but he also raised the dead.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con inversión:**

1. *"**Never have I heard** such teaching."* (Marcos 1:27, adaptado) – Nunca he oído tal enseñanza.
2. *"**Seldom have we witnessed** such faith."* (Lucas 7:9, adaptado) – Pocas veces hemos presenciado tal fe.
3. *"**Not only did he heal** the sick, but he also cast out demons."* (Mateo 8:16, adaptado) – No solo sanó a los enfermos, sino que también expulsó demonios.
4. *"**No sooner had he spoken** than the centurion believed."* (Mateo 8:13, adaptado) – No bien había hablado, cuando el centurión creyó.
5. *"**Rarely have we seen** such devotion."* (Hechos 2:44-45, adaptado) – Raramente hemos visto tal devoción.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Énfasis en negativas):**

- ***Never have I seen** such a beautiful church.* (Nunca he visto una iglesia tan hermosa.)
- ***Seldom have we heard** such a powerful sermon.* (Pocas veces hemos oído un sermón tan poderoso.)
- ***Rarely does he miss** a Sunday service.* (Raramente falta a un servicio dominical.)
- ***Not only did she pray** for him, but she also visited him.* (No solo oró por él, sino que también lo visitó.)
- ***No sooner had he arrived** than he started preaching.* (No bien había llegado, cuando comenzó a predicar.)
- ***Hardly had we started** praying when the power went out.* (Apenas habíamos empezado a orar cuando se fue la luz.)

**Edificación:** Jesús se maravilló de la fe del centurión. Aprendemos a usar la inversión para enfatizar la rareza y grandeza de la fe verdadera.

---

### Lección 17 – "It Was Jesus Who Healed Me"
**Gramática focal:** Cleft sentences (*It was... that/who*; *What... is/was...*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"It was Jesus who healed me."* (Adaptado de Juan 9:11 – *"The man called Jesus made mud and anointed my eyes and said to me, 'Go to Siloam and wash.' So I went and washed and received my sight."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 9:8-12, 24-25, ESV, extracto):** 
> *"The neighbors and those who had seen him before as a beggar were saying, 'Is this not the man who used to sit and beg?' Some said, 'It is he.' Others said, 'No, but he is like him.' He kept saying, 'I am the man.' So they said to him, 'Then how were your eyes opened?' He answered, 'The man called Jesus made mud and anointed my eyes and said to me, "Go to Siloam and wash." So I went and washed and received my sight.' They said to him, 'Where is he?' He said, 'I do not know.' So for the second time they called the man who had been blind and said to him, 'Give glory to God. We know that this man is a sinner.' He answered, 'Whether he is a sinner I do not know. One thing I do know, that though I was blind, now I see.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| neighbors | vecinos | beggar | mendigo |
| used to sit | solía sentarse | opened | abrió |
| mud | barro | anointed | untó |
| wash | lavar | received my sight | recibí la vista |
| sinner | pecador | blind | ciego |

**Estructuras de Cleft Sentences:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *It + be + sujeto enfatizado + that/who + cláusula* | Enfatizar el sujeto | ***It was Jesus who** healed me.* |
| *It + be + objeto enfatizado + that + cláusula* | Enfatizar el objeto | ***It was my sight that** he restored.* |
| *It + be + circunstancia + that + cláusula* | Enfatizar lugar/tiempo | ***It was at the pool that** he was healed.* |
| *What + sujeto + verbo + be + elemento enfatizado* | Enfatizar un elemento | ***What he did was** heal me.* |
| *All + sujeto + verbo + be + elemento enfatizado* | Enfatizar la única cosa | ***All I know is** that I can see.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con cleft sentences:**

1. *"**It was Abraham who** believed God."* (Génesis 15:6, adaptado) – Fue Abraham quien creyó a Dios.
2. *"**It was by faith that** they conquered kingdoms."* (Hebreos 11:33, adaptado) – Fue por fe que conquistaron reinos.
3. *"**What I desire is** mercy, not sacrifice."* (Mateo 9:13, adaptado) – Lo que deseo es misericordia, no sacrificio.
4. *"**It is the Lord who** gives wisdom."* (Proverbios 2:6) – Es el Señor quien da sabiduría.
5. *"**All I know is** that I was blind, but now I see."* (Juan 9:25) – Todo lo que sé es que era ciego, pero ahora veo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Énfasis en la fe):**
