- ***It was my grandmother who** taught me to pray.* (Fue mi abuela quien me enseñó a orar.)
- ***It was the Bible that** changed my life.* (Fue la Biblia la que cambió mi vida.)
- ***What I need is** more faith.* (Lo que necesito es más fe.)
- ***It was at the church that** I found peace.* (Fue en la iglesia donde encontré paz.)
- ***All I want is** to follow Jesus.* (Todo lo que quiero es seguir a Jesús.)
- ***What he gave me was** hope.* (Lo que me dio fue esperanza.)

**Edificación:** El ciego de nacimiento declaró: "Una cosa sé: que era ciego, y ahora veo". Aprendemos a usar cleft sentences para enfatizar lo más importante de nuestro testimonio: que Jesús nos ha transformado.

---

### Lección 18 – "Only When We Pray Do We Find Peace"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión con *only* (*only when, only after, only by, only then*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Only when we pray do we find peace."* (Adaptado de Filipenses 4:6-7 – *"Do not be anxious about anything, but in everything by prayer and supplication with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God. And the peace of God, which surpasses all understanding, will guard your hearts and your minds in Christ Jesus."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Filipenses 4:4-9, ESV):** 
> *"Rejoice in the Lord always; again I will say, rejoice. Let your reasonableness be known to everyone. The Lord is at hand; do not be anxious about anything, but in everything by prayer and supplication with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God. And the peace of God, which surpasses all understanding, will guard your hearts and your minds in Christ Jesus. Finally, brothers, whatever is true, whatever is honorable, whatever is just, whatever is pure, whatever is lovely, whatever is commendable, if there is any excellence, if there is anything worthy of praise, think about these things. What you have learned and received and heard and seen in me—practice these things, and the God of peace will be with you."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| rejoice | regocijarse | reasonableness | moderación / razón |
| at hand | cerca | anxious | ansioso |
| supplication | súplica | thanksgiving | acción de gracias |
| surpasses | sobrepasa | understanding | entendimiento |
| guard | guardar | hearts | corazones |
| minds | mentes | honorable | honorable |
| pure | puro | lovely | amable |
| commendable | digno de alabanza | excellence | excelencia |
| worthy | digno | practice | practicar |

**Inversión con *only*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Only when + cláusula, inversión + cláusula principal* | Solo cuando... | ***Only when we pray do we find** peace.* |
| *Only after + cláusula, inversión* | Solo después de... | ***Only after he died did we understand**.* |
| *Only by + -ing, inversión* | Solo por medio de... | ***Only by praying can we overcome**.* |
| *Only then + inversión* | Solo entonces... | ***Only then did I realize**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con *only* invertido:**

1. *"**Only after he had risen did they understand** the Scripture."* (Juan 20:9, adaptado) – Solo después de que resucitó entendieron la Escritura.
2. *"**Only when we confess our sins will he forgive**."* (1 Juan 1:9, adaptado) – Solo cuando confesamos nuestros pecados, él perdona.
3. *"**Only by faith can we be saved**."* (Efesios 2:8, adaptado) – Solo por fe podemos ser salvos.
4. *"**Only then will we see** him face to face."* (1 Corintios 13:12, adaptado) – Solo entonces le veremos cara a cara.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***Only when I pray do I find** peace.* (Solo cuando oro encuentro paz.)
- ***Only after he repented did he receive** forgiveness.* (Solo después de arrepentirse recibió perdón.)
- ***Only by reading the Bible can we know** God's will.* (Solo leyendo la Biblia podemos conocer la voluntad de Dios.)
- ***Only then did I understand** his love.* (Solo entonces entendí su amor.)
- ***Only when we forgive others will we be forgiven**.* (Solo cuando perdonamos a otros seremos perdonados.)

**Edificación:** Pablo nos llama a la oración como camino a la paz. Aprendemos a usar la inversión con "only" para enfatizar que la oración es el medio único para encontrar la paz de Dios.

---

### Lección 19 – "Not Only Did He Heal, but He Also Saved"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión con *not only... but also* y *neither... nor*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Not only did he heal the sick, but he also saved the lost."* (Adaptado de Lucas 19:10 – *"The Son of Man came to seek and to save the lost."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Lucas 19:1-10, ESV):** 
> *"He entered Jericho and was passing through. And behold, there was a man named Zacchaeus. He was a chief tax collector and was rich. And he was seeking to see who Jesus was, but on account of the crowd he could not, because he was small of stature. So he ran on ahead and climbed up into a sycamore tree to see him, for he was about to pass that way. And when Jesus came to the place, he looked up and said to him, 'Zacchaeus, hurry and come down, for I must stay at your house today.' So he hurried and came down and received him joyfully. And when they saw it, they all grumbled, 'He has gone in to be the guest of a man who is a sinner.' And Zacchaeus stood and said to the Lord, 'Behold, Lord, the half of my goods I give to the poor. And if I have defrauded anyone of anything, I restore it fourfold.' And Jesus said to him, 'Today salvation has come to this house, since he also is a son of Abraham. For the Son of Man came to seek and to save the lost.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| tax collector | recaudador de impuestos | rich | rico |
| crowd | multitud | small of stature | pequeño de estatura |
| sycamore | sicómoro | hurry | darse prisa |
| joyfully | gozosamente | grumbled | murmuraban |
| guest | huésped | defrauded | defraudado |
| restore | restaurar | fourfold | cuatro veces |
| salvation | salvación | seek | buscar |

**Inversión con *not only... but also*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Not only + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo, but + sujeto + also + verbo* | ***Not only did he heal** the sick, but he **also saved** the lost.* |
| *Not only + verbo + sujeto* (sin auxiliar) | ***Not only** did he come, but he **also** stayed.* |

**Inversión con *neither... nor*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Neither + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo, nor + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Neither did he come**, **nor** did he call.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Not only did he create** the heavens, but he also formed the earth."* (Isaías 45:18, adaptado) – No solo creó los cielos, sino que también formó la tierra.
2. *"**Not only were they saved**, but they were also filled with the Spirit."* (Hechos 2:38, adaptado) – No solo fueron salvos, sino que también fueron llenos del Espíritu.
3. *"**Neither did he sin**, **nor** was any deceit found in his mouth."* (1 Pedro 2:22) – Ni pecó, ni se halló engaño en su boca.
4. *"**Not only did he rise**, but he also ascended to heaven."* (Hechos 1:9, adaptado) – No solo resucitó, sino que también ascendió al cielo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***Not only did she pray** for me, but she also visited me in the hospital.* (No solo oró por mí, sino que también me visitó en el hospital.)
- ***Not only did he read** the Bible, but he also studied theology.* (No solo leyó la Biblia, sino que también estudió teología.)
- ***Neither did I know** the truth, nor did I seek it.* (Ni conocía la verdad, ni la buscaba.)
- ***Not only were they healed**, but they also were given new life.* (No solo fueron sanados, sino que también recibieron nueva vida.)
- ***Not only does he preach**, but he also lives what he preaches.* (No solo predica, sino que también vive lo que predica.)

**Edificación:** Jesús no solo sanó a Zacarías, sino que también lo salvó. Aprendemos a usar la inversión con "not only... but also" para enfatizar la plenitud de la obra de Cristo.

---

### Lección 20 – Repaso: "Never Have I Heard"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de inversión y cleft sentences.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Never have I heard such words!"* (Adaptado de Juan 7:46 – *"No one ever spoke like this man!"*)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando inversión y cleft sentences.

**Ejemplo:**
- ***Never have I seen** such faith.* (Inversión con *never*)
- ***Seldom do we hear** such preaching.* (Inversión con *seldom*)
- ***Only when we pray do we find** peace.* (Inversión con *only*)
- ***Not only did he die**, but he also rose again.* (Inversión con *not only*)
- ***It was Jesus who** saved me.* (Cleft con *it*)
- ***What I need is** more faith.* (Cleft con *what*)
- ***All I know is** that I am forgiven.* (Cleft con *all*)
- ***No sooner had I prayed** than peace came.* (Inversión con *no sooner*)
- ***Hardly had he spoken** when the crowd believed.* (Inversión con *hardly*)
- ***Only by grace can we be saved.** * (Inversión con *only by*)

---

## UNIDAD 5: GERUNDIOS E INFINITIVOS AVANZADOS Y PASIVAS
*Lecciones 21 a 25*

---

### Lección 21 – "I Enjoy Being Loved by God"
**Gramática focal:** Gerundios pasivos (*being + pp*) e infinitivos pasivos (*to be + pp*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I enjoy being loved by God."* (Adaptado de 1 Juan 4:19 – *"We love because he first loved us."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Juan 4:7-12, ESV):** 
> *"Beloved, let us love one another, for love is from God, and whoever loves has been born of God and knows God. Anyone who does not love does not know God, because God is love. In this the love of God was made manifest among us, that God sent his only Son into the world, so that we might live through him. In this is love, not that we have loved God but that he loved us and sent his Son to be the propitiation for our sins. Beloved, if God so loved us, we also ought to love one another. No one has ever seen God; if we love one another, God abides in us and his love is perfected in us."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| beloved | amados | born of God | nacido de Dios |
| manifest | manifestado | propitiation | propiciación |
| sins | pecados | abides | permanece |
| perfected | perfeccionado | | |

**Gerundios e infinitivos pasivos:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *being + pp* | Gerundio pasivo (acción pasiva en progreso) | *I enjoy **being loved** by God.* |
| *to be + pp* | Infinitivo pasivo | *I want **to be saved**.* |
| *having been + pp* | Gerundio pasivo perfectivo | ***Having been forgiven**, I forgive.* |
| *to have been + pp* | Infinitivo pasivo perfectivo | *He seems **to have been healed**.* |

**Verbos comunes seguidos de gerundio pasivo:**

| Verbo + being + pp | Significado |
|:---|:---|
| *enjoy being loved* | Disfrutar siendo amado |
| *avoid being seen* | Evitar ser visto |
| *mind being told* | Importar ser dicho |
| *remember being healed* | Recordar haber sido sanado |
| *imagine being saved* | Imaginar ser salvo |

**Verbos comunes seguidos de infinitivo pasivo:**

| Verbo + to be + pp | Significado |
|:---|:---|
| *want to be saved* | Querer ser salvo |
| *hope to be healed* | Esperar ser sanado |
| *expect to be called* | Esperar ser llamado |
| *deserve to be forgiven* | Merecer ser perdonado |
| *pretend to be saved* | Pretender ser salvo |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He did not consider equality with God a thing **to be grasped**."* (Filipenses 2:6) – No consideró el ser igual a Dios como algo a ser retenido.
2. *"We are **to be** **salt** and **light**."* (Mateo 5:13-14, adaptado) – Debemos ser sal y luz.
3. *"She was found **to be** with child."* (Mateo 1:18, adaptado) – Se encontró que estaba encinta.
4. *"He is worthy **to be praised**."* (Salmo 18:3, adaptado) – Él es digno de ser alabado.
5. *"I remember **being healed** by Jesus."* (Marcos 5:25-34, adaptado) – Recuerdo haber sido sanado por Jesús.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I enjoy **being part** of this church.* (Disfruto siendo parte de esta iglesia.)
- *He wants **to be accepted** by the community.* (Él quiere ser aceptado por la comunidad.)
- *She deserves **to be forgiven**.* (Ella merece ser perdonada.)
- *I remember **being baptized**.* (Recuerdo haber sido bautizado.)
- *We hope **to be transformed** by the Spirit.* (Esperamos ser transformados por el Espíritu.)
- *They avoid **being seen** as hypocrites.* (Ellos evitan ser vistos como hipócritas.)

**Edificación:** Juan nos invita a amar porque Dios nos amó primero. Aprendemos a usar gerundios e infinitivos pasivos para hablar de nuestra experiencia de ser amados, perdonados y transformados por Dios.

---

### Lección 22 – "I Regret Having Been Angry"
**Gramática focal:** Verbos de arrepentimiento con gerundio perfectivo (*regret having + pp, apologize for having + pp, admit having + pp*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I regret having been angry with my brother."* (Adaptado de Mateo 5:23-24 – *"If you are offering your gift at the altar and there remember that your brother has something against you, leave your gift there before the altar and go. First be reconciled to your brother, and then come and offer your gift."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 5:21-26, ESV):** 
> *"You have heard that it was said to those of old, 'You shall not murder; and whoever murders will be liable to judgment.' But I say to you that everyone who is angry with his brother will be liable to judgment; whoever insults his brother will be liable to the council; and whoever says, 'You fool!' will be liable to the hell of fire. So if you are offering your gift at the altar and there remember that your brother has something against you, leave your gift there before the altar and go. First be reconciled to your brother, and then come and offer your gift. Come to terms quickly with your accuser while you are going with him to court, lest your accuser hand you over to the judge, and the judge to the guard, and you be put in prison. Truly, I say to you, you will never get out until you have paid the last penny."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| murders | mata | liable | responsable |
| judgment | juicio | insults | insulta |
| council | concilio | fool | necio |
| hell of fire | infierno de fuego | reconciled | reconciliado |
| accuser | acusador | court | tribunal |
| guard | guardia | prison | prisión |
| penny | centavo | | |

**Verbos con gerundio perfectivo (arrepentimiento):**

| Verbo + having + pp | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *regret having + pp* | Lamentar haber hecho | *I **regret having been** angry.* |
| *apologize for having + pp* | Disculparse por haber hecho | *She **apologized for having lied**.* |
| *admit having + pp* | Admitir haber hecho | *He **admitted having sinned**.* |
| *confess having + pp* | Confesar haber hecho | *They **confessed having stolen**.* |
| *deny having + pp* | Negar haber hecho | *He **denied having seen** him.* |

**Verbos con gerundio simple (sin perfectivo):**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *regret + -ing* (arrepentimiento) | *I regret **saying** that.* |
| *admit + -ing* | *He admitted **stealing**.* |
| *deny + -ing* | *She denied **being** there.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"Peter regretted having denied Jesus."* (Mateo 26:75, adaptado) – Pedro lamentó haber negado a Jesús.
2. *"He confessed having sinned against God."* (1 Samuel 15:24, adaptado) – Confesó haber pecado contra Dios.
3. *"They admitted having been wrong."* (Hechos 19:18, adaptado) – Admitieron haber estado equivocados.
4. *"I apologize for having been impatient."* (Santiago 1:19, adaptado) – Me disculpo por haber sido impaciente.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I regret **having been** unforgiving.* (Lamento haber sido implacable.)
- *She apologized **for having** **spoken** harshly.* (Se disculpó por haber hablado con dureza.)
- *He admitted **having lied** about his past.* (Admitió haber mentido sobre su pasado.)
- *We confess **having** **neglected** our prayers.* (Confesamos haber descuidado nuestras oraciones.)
- *They denied **having seen** the miracle.* (Negaron haber visto el milagro.)
- *I regret **not having** **prayed** more.* (Lamento no haber orado más.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos llama a la reconciliación antes de ofrecer nuestro don. Aprendemos a usar gerundios perfectivos para expresar arrepentimiento y confesión, esenciales en la vida cristiana.

---

### Lección 23 – "He Is Worth Following"
**Gramática focal:** *Worth* + gerundio; *need* + gerundio (pasivo); *deserve* + infinitivo.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He is worth following."* (Adaptado de Mateo 4:19 – *"Follow me, and I will make you fishers of men."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 4:18-22, ESV):** 
> *"While walking by the Sea of Galilee, he saw two brothers, Simon (who is called Peter) and Andrew his brother, casting a net into the sea, for they were fishermen. And he said to them, 'Follow me, and I will make you fishers of men.' Immediately they left their nets and followed him. And going on from there he saw two other brothers, James the son of Zebedee and John his brother, in the boat with Zebedee their father, mending their nets, and he called them. Immediately they left the boat and their father and followed him."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| casting a net | lanzando una red | fishermen | pescadores |
| fishers of men | pescadores de hombres | immediately | inmediatamente |
| nets | redes | mending | remendando |
| boat | barca | | |

**Estructuras con *worth, need, deserve*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *worth + -ing* (activo, con significado pasivo) | Valer la pena hacer | *He **is worth following**.* |
| *need + -ing* (activo, con significado pasivo) | Necesitar ser... | *The church **needs praying** for.* |
| *need to be + pp* | Necesitar ser... | *The church **needs to be prayed** for.* |
| *deserve + to be + pp* | Merecer ser... | *He **deserves to be praised**.* |
| *deserve + -ing* (activo) | Merecer... | *He **deserves praising**.* |

**Diferencias:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *worth following* | Vale la pena seguirle | *Jesus is **worth following**.* |
| *worth to be followed* | (No se usa en inglés moderno) | - |
| *needs fixing* | Necesita ser arreglado | *The roof **needs fixing**.* |
| *needs to be fixed* | Necesita ser arreglado | *The roof **needs to be fixed**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **is worth** **worshiping**."* (Salmo 95:6, adaptado) – Él merece ser adorado.
2. *"The Lord **needs** our **prayers**."* (Efesios 6:18, adaptado) – El Señor necesita nuestras oraciones.
3. *"The gospel **deserves to be** **proclaimed**."* (Romanos 1:16, adaptado) – El evangelio merece ser proclamado.
4. *"The name of Jesus **is worth** **honoring**."* (Filipenses 2:9-11, adaptado) – El nombre de Jesús merece ser honrado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *Jesus **is worth following**.* (Jesús merece ser seguido.)
- *The Bible **is worth reading**.* (La Biblia vale la pena leerla.)
- *The church **needs** our **support**.* (La iglesia necesita nuestro apoyo.)
- *The pastor **deserves to be respected**.* (El pastor merece ser respetado.)
- *Our sins **need forgiving**.* (Nuestros pecados necesitan ser perdonados.)
- *His sacrifice **is worth remembering**.* (Su sacrificio vale la pena recordarlo.)

**Edificación:** Los discípulos dejaron todo para seguir a Jesús. Aprendemos a usar estas estructuras para expresar que Jesús y su evangelio son dignos de todo nuestro compromiso.

---

### Lección 24 – "I Look Forward to Being Healed"
**Gramática focal:** Verbos con preposición + gerundio (*look forward to, insist on, succeed in, apologize for, prevent from, thank for*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I look forward to being healed."* (Adaptado de Marcos 5:25-34 – La mujer con flujo de sangre)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Marcos 5:25-34, ESV):** 
> *"And there was a woman who had had a discharge of blood for twelve years, and who had suffered much under many physicians, and had spent all that she had, and was no better but rather grew worse. She had heard the reports about Jesus and came up behind him in the crowd and touched his garment. For she said, 'If I touch even his garments, I will be made well.' And immediately the flow of blood dried up, and she felt in her body that she was healed of her disease. And Jesus, perceiving in himself that power had gone out from him, immediately turned about in the crowd and said, 'Who touched my garments?' And his disciples said to him, 'You see the crowd pressing around you, and yet you say, "Who touched me?"' And he looked around to see who had done it. But the woman, knowing what had happened to her, came in fear and trembling and fell down before him and told him the whole truth. And he said to her, 'Daughter, your faith has made you well; go in peace, and be healed of your disease.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| discharge | flujo | physicians | médicos |
| worse | peor | reports | informes |
| garment | manto | immediately | inmediatamente |
| dried up | se secó | disease | enfermedad |
| perceiving | percibiendo | fear | miedo |
| trembling | temblor | faith | fe |

**Verbos con preposición + gerundio:**

| Verbo + Preposición + -ing | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *look forward to + -ing* | Esperar con ansias | *I **look forward to being healed**.* |
| *insist on + -ing* | Insistir en | *He **insisted on praying**.* |
| *succeed in + -ing* | Tener éxito en | *She **succeeded in overcoming**.* |
| *apologize for + -ing* | Disculparse por | *I **apologize for being late**.* |
| *prevent from + -ing* | Prevenir de | *Nothing **prevented him from** coming.* |
| *thank for + -ing* | Agradecer por | *I **thank you for praying**.* |
| *dream of + -ing* | Soñar con | *I **dream of serving** him.* |
| *believe in + -ing* | Creer en | *We **believe in praying**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"I **look forward to seeing** my Lord."* (Filipenses 1:23, adaptado) – Espero con ansias ver a mi Señor.
2. *"They **insisted on following** him."* (Marcos 10:52, adaptado) – Insistieron en seguirlo.
3. *"She **succeeded in touching** his garment."* (Marcos 5:28, adaptado) – Ella logró tocar su manto.
4. *"I **thank God for sending** his Son."* (Juan 3:16, adaptado) – Doy gracias a Dios por enviar a su Hijo.
5. *"Nothing **prevented him from preaching**."* (Hechos 28:31, adaptado) – Nada le impidió predicar.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **look forward to worshiping** with you.* (Espero con ansias adorar con vosotros.)
- *She **insisted on praying** for her enemy.* (Insistió en orar por su enemigo.)
- *We **succeeded in finishing** the project.* (Tuvimos éxito en terminar el proyecto.)
- *I **apologize for not coming** earlier.* (Me disculpo por no haber venido antes.)
- *He **thanked me for helping** him.* (Me agradeció por ayudarle.)
- *They **believed in serving** others.* (Creyeron en servir a otros.)

**Edificación:** La mujer con flujo de sangre creyó que con solo tocar el manto de Jesús sería sanada. Aprendemos a usar verbos con preposición + gerundio para expresar expectativas, insistencia y gratitud en la vida de fe.

---

### Lección 25 – Repaso: "I Look Forward to Being with Him"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de gerundios e infinitivos pasivos y con preposiciones.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I look forward to being with him forever."* (Adaptado de 1 Tesalonicenses 4:17)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes estructuras de gerundios e infinitivos.

**Ejemplo:**
- *I enjoy **being prayed** for.* (Gerundio pasivo)
- *I want **to be healed**.* (Infinitivo pasivo)
- *I remember **being baptized**.* (Gerundio pasivo perfectivo)
- *I regret **having been** angry.* (Gerundio perfectivo)
- *He admitted **having lied**.* (Gerundio perfectivo)
- *Jesus is **worth following**.* (*Worth* + gerundio)
- *The church **needs praying** for.* (*Need* + gerundio)
- *He deserves **to be praised**.* (*Deserve* + infinitivo pasivo)
- *I **look forward to meeting** him.* (Preposición + gerundio)
- *She **insisted on coming**.* (Preposición + gerundio)

---

## UNIDAD 6: DISCURSO INDIRECTO AVANZADO
*Lecciones 26 a 30*

---

### Lección 26 – "He Claimed to Have Seen the Lord"
**Gramática focal:** Reporting verbs avanzados con infinitivo (*claim to, seem to, appear to, pretend to, happen to*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He claimed to have seen the Lord."* (Adaptado de Juan 20:18 – *"Mary Magdalene went to the disciples with the news: 'I have seen the Lord!'"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 20:11-18, ESV):** 
> *"But Mary stood weeping outside the tomb, and as she wept she stooped to look into the tomb. And she saw two angels in white, sitting where the body of Jesus had lain, one at the head and one at the feet. They said to her, 'Woman, why are you weeping?' She said to them, 'They have taken away my Lord, and I do not know where they have laid him.' Having said this, she turned around and saw Jesus standing, but she did not know that it was Jesus. Jesus said to her, 'Woman, why are you weeping? Whom are you seeking?' Supposing him to be the gardener, she said to him, 'Sir, if you have carried him away, tell me where you have laid him, and I will take him away.' Jesus said to her, 'Mary.' She turned and said to him in Aramaic, 'Rabboni!' (which means Teacher). Jesus said to her, 'Do not cling to me, for I have not yet ascended to the Father; but go to my brothers and say to them, "I am ascending to my Father and your Father, to my God and your God."' Mary Magdalene went and announced to the disciples, 'I have seen the Lord'—and that he had said these things to her."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| weeping | llorando | stooped | se inclinó |
| angels | ángeles | white | blanco |
| head | cabecera | feet | pies |
| taken away | llevado | laid | puesto |
| gardener | jardinero | carried away | llevado |
| ascend | ascender | announced | anunció |

**Reporting verbs con infinitivo:**

| Verbo | Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *claim* | *claim + to + infinitivo* | Afirmar | *He **claims to have seen** the Lord.* |
| *seem* | *seem + to + infinitivo* | Parecer | *She **seems to know** the truth.* |
| *appear* | *appear + to + infinitivo* | Aparecer / parecer | *They **appear to be** believers.* |
| *pretend* | *pretend + to + infinitivo* | Fingir | *He **pretended to be** a disciple.* |
| *happen* | *happen + to + infinitivo* | Ocurrir / tener la suerte de | *I **happened to see** him.* |
| *prove* | *prove + to + infinitivo* | Resultar | *He **proved to be** faithful.* |
| *turn out* | *turn out + to + infinitivo* | Resultar | *He **turned out to be** the Messiah.* |

**Uso de los tiempos en el infinitivo:**

| Tiempo | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Presente** | *to + base form* | *He **claims to be** the Son of God.* |
| **Pasado** | *to have + pp* | *He **claims to have seen** the Lord.* |
| **Continuo** | *to be + -ing* | *He **seems to be praying**.* |
| **Pasado continuo** | *to have been + -ing* | *He **appears to have been praying**.* |
| **Pasivo** | *to be + pp* | *He **claims to be saved**.* |
| **Pasivo perfectivo** | *to have been + pp* | *He **claims to have been healed**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"Peter **claimed to have known** Jesus."* (Mateo 26:72-74, adaptado) – Pedro afirmó haber conocido a Jesús.
2. *"The disciples **seemed to be afraid**."* (Marcos 4:40, adaptado) – Los discípulos parecían tener miedo.
3. *"He **pretended to be** a stranger."* (Lucas 24:28, adaptado) – Fingió ser un extraño.
4. *"The miracle **proved to be true**."* (Juan 9:30, adaptado) – El milagro resultó ser verdad.
5. *"She **happened to be** at the tomb."* (Juan 20:1, adaptado) – Ella resultó estar en la tumba.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *She **claims to have read** the entire Bible.* (Afirma haber leído toda la Biblia.)
- *He **seems to be** a devout Christian.* (Parece ser un cristiano devoto.)
- *They **appear to have been** transformed.* (Parecen haber sido transformados.)
- *He **pretended to be** praying.* (Fingió estar orando.)
- *I **happened to meet** my pastor at the mall.* (Tuve la suerte de encontrarme con mi pastor en el centro comercial.)
- *She **turned out to be** a great leader.* (Resultó ser una gran líder.)

**Edificación:** María Magdalena anunció: "¡He visto al Señor!". Aprendemos a usar reporting verbs con infinitivo para reportar afirmaciones sobre la fe, con matices de certeza, duda y apariencia.

---

### Lección 27 – "She Suggested That They Pray"
**Gramática focal:** Reporting verbs con subjuntivo (*suggest, recommend, insist, demand, propose*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"She suggested that they pray together."* (Adaptado de Hechos 1:14 – *"They all joined together constantly in prayer."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 1:12-14, ESV):** 
> *"Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mount called Olivet, which is near Jerusalem, a Sabbath day's journey away. And when they had entered, they went up to the upper room, where they were staying, Peter and John and James and Andrew, Philip and Thomas, Bartholomew and Matthew, James the son of Alphaeus and Simon the Zealot and Judas the son of James. All these with one accord were devoting themselves to prayer, together with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus, and his brothers."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| returned | regresaron | Mount Olivet | Monte de los Olivos |
| upper room | aposento alto | staying | quedándose |
| one accord | unánimemente | devoting | dedicándose |
| prayer | oración | together | juntos |

**Verbos que requieren subjuntivo (en inglés formal, base form):**

| Verbo | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *suggest* | *suggest that + sujeto + base form* | *She **suggested that they pray**.* |
| *recommend* | *recommend that + sujeto + base form* | *He **recommended that we read**.* |
| *insist* | *insist that + sujeto + base form* | *She **insisted that he come**.* |
| *demand* | *demand that + sujeto + base form* | *They **demanded that he leave**.* |
| *propose* | *propose that + sujeto + base form* | *He **proposed that they meet**.* |

**También se pueden usar:**
- *suggest + -ing*: *She suggested praying.*
- *recommend + -ing*: *He recommended reading the Bible.*

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"She **suggested that they worship** the Lord."* (Hechos 13:2, adaptado) – Ella sugirió que adoraran al Señor.
2. *"He **insisted that we believe**."* (Marcos 9:24, adaptado) – Insistió en que creyéramos.
3. *"They **demanded that he heal** the sick."* (Mateo 12:38, adaptado) – Exigieron que sanara a los enfermos.
4. *"He **recommended that they pray** without ceasing."* (1 Tesalonicenses 5:17, adaptado) – Recomendó que oraran sin cesar.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **suggest that we pray** together.* (Sugiero que oremos juntos.)
- *He **recommended that I read** the book of John.* (Recomendó que leyera el libro de Juan.)
- *She **insisted that he come** to the service.* (Insistió en que él viniera al servicio.)
- *They **demanded that the pastor stay**.* (Exigieron que el pastor se quedara.)
- *We **propose that the church help** the poor.* (Proponemos que la iglesia ayude a los pobres.)
- *The apostle **urged that they love** one another.* (El apóstol instó a que se amaran unos a otros.)

**Edificación:** Los discípulos se dedicaban a la oración. Aprendemos a usar verbs de sugerencia e insistencia para proponer acciones espirituales en la comunidad cristiana.

---

### Lección 28 – "She Asked if He Had Believed"
**Gramática focal:** Discurso indirecto con preguntas complejas (WH- + backshifting).

**Versículo Clave (directo):** 
> *"She asked, 'Do you believe in the Son of God?'"* → *She asked if he had believed.* (Adaptado de Juan 9:35)

**Texto Extendido (directo – Juan 9:35-38, ESV):** 
> *"Jesus heard that they had cast him out, and having found him he said, 'Do you believe in the Son of Man?' He answered, 'And who is he, sir, that I may believe in him?' Jesus said to him, 'You have seen him, and it is he who is speaking to you.' He said, 'Lord, I believe,' and he worshiped him."*

**Texto Extendido (indirecto):**
> *"Jesus asked the man if he believed in the Son of Man. The man asked who he was so that he might believe. Jesus told him that he had seen him and that he was speaking to him. The man said that he believed and worshiped him."*

**Backshifting en preguntas WH-:**

| Tiempo | Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|:---|
| Present Simple | *"What do you see?"* | *He asked what I **saw**.* |
| Present Continuous | *"What are you doing?"* | *He asked what I **was doing**.* |
| Past Simple | *"What did you see?"* | *He asked what I **had seen**.* |
| Past Continuous | *"What were you doing?"* | *He asked what I **had been doing**.* |
| Present Perfect | *"What have you seen?"* | *He asked what I **had seen**.* |
| Future (will) | *"What will you do?"* | *He asked what I **would do**.* |
| Future (going to) | *"What are you going to do?"* | *He asked what I **was going to do**.* |

**Preguntas con *if / whether*:**

| Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|
| *"Do you believe?"* | *He asked **if** I believed.* |
| *"Are you a Christian?"* | *He asked **whether** I was a Christian.* |
| *"Have you been saved?"* | *He asked **if** I had been saved.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos en discurso indirecto:**

1. *"He asked, 'Who touched me?'"* → *He asked who **had touched** him.* (Marcos 5:30)
2. *"She asked, 'Where have you put him?'"* → *She asked where they **had put** him.* (Juan 20:13)
3. *"They asked, 'Are you the King of the Jews?'"* → *They asked whether he was the King of the Jews.* (Mateo 27:11)
4. *"Peter asked, 'Lord, how often will my brother sin against me, and I forgive him?'"* → *Peter asked how often he should forgive his brother.* (Mateo 18:21)

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He asked **what I believed**.* (Preguntó qué creía.)
- *She asked **whether I had read** the Bible.* (Preguntó si había leído la Biblia.)
- *They asked **where I worshiped**.* (Preguntaron dónde adoraba.)
- *The pastor asked **why I had come**.* (El pastor preguntó por qué había venido.)
- *She asked **how often I prayed**.* (Preguntó con qué frecuencia oraba.)
- *He asked **when I would be baptized**.* (Preguntó cuándo sería bautizado.)

**Edificación:** Jesús pregunta al ciego: "¿Crees en el Hijo de Dios?". Aprendemos a reportar preguntas profundas sobre la fe usando el discurso indirecto con backshifting preciso.

---

### Lección 29 – "He Warned Them Not to Sin"
**Gramática focal:** Reporting verbs con infinitivo y objeto (*advise, warn, persuade, convince, remind, encourage*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He warned them not to sin."* (Adaptado de Mateo 5:29-30)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 5:27-32, ESV):** 
> *"You have heard that it was said, 'You shall not commit adultery.' But I say to you that everyone who looks at a woman with lustful intent has already committed adultery with her in his heart. If your right eye causes you to sin, tear it out and throw it away. For it is better that you lose one of your members than that your whole body be thrown into hell. And if your right hand causes you to sin, cut it off and throw it away. For it is better that you lose one of your members than that your whole body go into hell. It was also said, 'Whoever divorces his wife, let him give her a certificate of divorce.' But I say to you that everyone who divorces his wife, except on the ground of sexual immorality, makes her commit adultery, and whoever marries a divorced woman commits adultery."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| commit adultery | cometer adulterio | looks | mira |
| lustful | lujurioso | intent | intención |
| heart | corazón | causes | causa |
| tear out | arrancar | throw away | tirar |
| member | miembro | hell | infierno |
| divorce | divorciar | certificate | certificado |
| sexual immorality | inmoralidad sexual | marries | se casa |

**Reporting verbs con objeto + infinitivo:**

| Verbo | Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *advise* | *advise someone to do* | Aconsejar | *He **advised them to pray**.* |
| *warn* | *warn someone not to do* | Advertir | *He **warned them not to sin**.* |
| *persuade* | *persuade someone to do* | Persuadir | *She **persuaded him to stay**.* |
| *convince* | *convince someone to do* | Convencer | *They **convinced me to go**.* |
| *remind* | *remind someone to do* | Recordar | *He **reminded me to pray**.* |
| *encourage* | *encourage someone to do* | Animar | *She **encouraged him to preach**.* |
| *command* | *command someone to do* | Mandar | *He **commanded them to follow**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **warned them not to be** afraid."* (Mateo 28:5, adaptado) – Les advirtió que no tuvieran miedo.
2. *"She **encouraged him to believe**."* (Juan 4:39-42, adaptado) – Ella le animó a creer.
3. *"The apostle **commanded them to love** one another."* (Juan 15:17, adaptado) – El apóstol les mandó amarse unos a otros.
4. *"He **reminded them to pray**."* (Lucas 18:1, adaptado) – Les recordó que oraran.
5. *"They **persuaded him to stay** longer."* (Hechos 18:20, adaptado) – Le persuadieron para que se quedara más tiempo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *The pastor **advised me to read** the Bible daily.* (El pastor me aconsejó leer la Biblia diariamente.)
- *He **warned us not to** give up.* (Nos advirtió que no nos rindiéramos.)
- *She **encouraged me to pray** more.* (Ella me animó a orar más.)
- *They **reminded us to forgive** others.* (Nos recordaron que perdonáramos a otros.)
- *I **persuaded him to come** to church.* (Le persuadí para que viniera a la iglesia.)
- *She **convinced me to believe**.* (Me convenció para creer.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos advierte contra el pecado y nos anima a la santidad. Aprendemos a usar reporting verbs para transmitir consejos, advertencias y exhortaciones basadas en la Palabra.

---

### Lección 30 – Repaso: "They Claimed to Have Believed"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de discurso indirecto avanzado.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"They claimed to have believed in him."* (Adaptado de Juan 8:31 – *"So Jesus said to the Jews who had believed him..."*)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante transforma 10 oraciones directas en discurso indirecto y viceversa.

**Ejemplo:**
1. *"I have seen the Lord!"* → *She claimed to have seen the Lord.*
2. *"Do you believe?"* → *He asked if I believed.*
3. *"Let us pray."* → *She suggested that they pray.*
4. *"Don't sin."* → *He warned them not to sin.*
5. *"Read the Bible."* → *He encouraged me to read the Bible.*

---

## UNIDAD 7: CONECTORES AVANZADOS Y ESTILO FORMAL
*Lecciones 31 a 35*

---

### Lección 31 – "Moreover, He Rose from the Dead"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de adición (*moreover, furthermore, in addition, besides, not only... but also*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Moreover, he rose from the dead, just as he said."* (Adaptado de Mateo 28:6)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Corintios 15:1-8, ESV):** 
> *"Now I would remind you, brothers, of the gospel I preached to you, which you received, in which you stand, and by which you are being saved, if you hold fast to the word I preached to you—unless you believed in vain. For I delivered to you as of first importance what I also received: that Christ died for our sins in accordance with the Scriptures, that he was buried, that he was raised on the third day in accordance with the Scriptures, and that he appeared to Cephas, then to the twelve. Then he appeared to more than five hundred brothers at one time, most of whom are still alive, though some have fallen asleep. Then he appeared to James, then to all the apostles. Last of all, as to one untimely born, he appeared also to me."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| remind | recordar | hold fast | retener |
| in vain | en vano | delivered | entregué |
| received | recibí | accordance | conformidad |
| raised | resucitado | appeared | apareció |
| alive | vivos | fallen asleep | han muerto |
| untimely | fuera de tiempo | | |

**Conectores de adición:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *moreover* | Además (formal) | *Christ died for us. **Moreover**, he rose again.* |
| *furthermore* | Además (formal) | *He was buried. **Furthermore**, he appeared to many.* |
| *in addition* | Además | *He died for our sins. **In addition**, he conquered death.* |
| *besides* | Además (informal) | *He was crucified. **Besides**, he rose.* |
| *not only... but also* | No solo... sino también | ***Not only** did he die, **but also** he rose.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Moreover**, God gave us his Spirit."* (1 Juan 3:24, adaptado) – Además, Dios nos dio su Espíritu.
2. *"**Furthermore**, he is the head of the church."* (Efesios 1:22, adaptado) – Además, él es la cabeza de la iglesia.
3. *"**In addition**, we have peace with God."* (Romanos 5:1, adaptado) – Además, tenemos paz con Dios.
4. *"**Not only** were they saved, **but also** they were filled with the Spirit."* (Hechos 2:38, adaptado) – No solo fueron salvos, sino que también fueron llenos del Espíritu.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *Jesus died for us. **Moreover**, he rose from the dead.* (Jesús murió por nosotros. Además, resucitó de entre los muertos.)
- *The Bible is inspired. **Furthermore**, it is useful for teaching.* (La Biblia es inspirada. Además, es útil para enseñar.)
- *He prayed for me. **In addition**, he visited me.* (Él oró por mí. Además, me visitó.)
- *She is a great preacher. **Besides**, she is a wonderful teacher.* (Es una gran predicadora. Además, es una maravillosa maestra.)
- ***Not only** did he read the Bible, **but also** he obeyed it.* (No solo leyó la Biblia, sino que también la obedeció.)

**Edificación:** Pablo enumera las evidencias de la resurrección: Cristo murió, fue sepultado, resucitó y apareció a muchos. Aprendemos a usar conectores de adición para construir argumentos y declaraciones teológicas.

---

### Lección 32 – "Nevertheless, God Was with Him"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de contraste avanzados (*nevertheless, nonetheless, whereas, while, yet, albeit*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Nevertheless, God was with him."* (Adaptado de Hechos 7:9 – *"God was with him"* en el contexto de José)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 7:9-10, ESV):** 
> *"And the patriarchs, jealous of Joseph, sold him into Egypt; but God was with him and rescued him out of all his afflictions and gave him favor and wisdom before Pharaoh, king of Egypt, who made him ruler over Egypt and over all his household."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| patriarchs | patriarcas | jealous | celosos |
| sold | vendieron | rescued | rescató |
| afflictions | aflicciones | favor | favor |
| wisdom | sabiduría | ruler | gobernante |
| household | casa | | |

**Conectores de contraste:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *nevertheless* | Sin embargo (formal) | *They persecuted him. **Nevertheless**, God was with him.* |
| *nonetheless* | No obstante (formal) | *He suffered. **Nonetheless**, he trusted God.* |
| *whereas* | Mientras que (contraste directo) | *Joseph was sold **whereas** his brothers prospered.* |
| *while* | Mientras que (contraste) | *He was a slave **while** God was with him.* |
| *yet* | Sin embargo | *He was poor, **yet** he was rich in faith.* |
| *albeit* | Aunque (formal, + adjetivo/frase) | *He was weak, **albeit** determined.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Nevertheless**, they did not believe the prophets."* (Hechos 7:39, adaptado) – Sin embargo, no creyeron a los profetas.
2. *"**Whereas** David was a man after God's own heart, Saul was rejected."* (Hechos 13:22, adaptado) – Mientras que David fue un hombre conforme al corazón de Dios, Saúl fue rechazado.
3. *"He was crucified in weakness, **yet** he lives by God's power."* (2 Corintios 13:4) – Fue crucificado en debilidad, pero vive por el poder de Dios.
4. *"**Nevertheless**, I am not ashamed."* (2 Timoteo 1:12) – Sin embargo, no me avergüenzo.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *Life is hard. **Nevertheless**, God is faithful.* (La vida es difícil. Sin embargo, Dios es fiel.)
- *He was persecuted. **Nonetheless**, he continued preaching.* (Fue perseguido. No obstante, continuó predicando.)
- ***Whereas** his brother doubted, he believed.* (Mientras que su hermano dudaba, él creía.)
- *She is young, **yet** she has great faith.* (Es joven, pero tiene gran fe.)
- *He is humble, **albeit** highly gifted.* (Es humilde, aunque muy talentoso.)
- *The church is small, **nevertheless**, it is growing.* (La iglesia es pequeña; sin embargo, está creciendo.)

**Edificación:** José fue vendido por sus hermanos, pero Dios estaba con él. Aprendemos a usar conectores de contraste para expresar cómo, a pesar de las dificultades, Dios permanece fiel.

---

### Lección 33 – "Consequently, We Are Saved"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de causa y consecuencia avanzados (*consequently, as a result, owing to, due to, hence, thus*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Consequently, we are saved by grace through faith."* (Adaptado de Efesios 2:8)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Efesios 2:1-10, ESV):** 
> *"And you were dead in the trespasses and sins in which you once walked, following the course of this world, following the prince of the power of the air, the spirit that is now at work in the sons of disobedience—among whom we all once lived in the passions of our flesh, carrying out the desires of the body and the mind, and were by nature children of wrath, like the rest of mankind. But God, being rich in mercy, because of the great love with which he loved us, even when we were dead in our trespasses, made us alive together with Christ—by grace you have been saved—and raised us up with him and seated us with him in the heavenly places in Christ Jesus, so that in the coming ages he might show the immeasurable riches of his grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus. For by grace you have been saved through faith. And this is not your own doing; it is the gift of God, not a result of works, so that no one may boast. For we are his workmanship, created in Christ Jesus for good works, which God prepared beforehand, that we should walk in them."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| trespasses | transgresiones | sins | pecados |
| prince | príncipe | power of the air | poder del aire |
| disobedience | desobediencia | passions | pasiones |
| flesh | carne | desires | deseos |
| children of wrath | hijos de ira | rich | rico |
| mercy | misericordia | raised up | resucitado |
| seated | sentado | heavenly places | lugares celestiales |
| immeasurable | inconmensurable | kindness | bondad |
| gift | regalo | workmanship | obra maestra |

**Conectores de causa y consecuencia:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *consequently* | Por consiguiente | *He died for us. **Consequently**, we are saved.* |
| *as a result* | Como resultado | *He rose again. **As a result**, we have hope.* |
| *owing to* | Debido a (+ sustantivo) | ***Owing to** his grace, we are saved.* |
| *due to* | Debido a (+ sustantivo) | ***Due to** his love, he gave his Son.* |
| *hence* | Por lo tanto (formal) | *He overcame death; **hence**, we have life.* |
| *thus* | Así que (formal) | *He died and rose; **thus**, salvation is available.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Consequently**, faith comes from hearing the message."* (Romanos 10:17, adaptado) – Por consiguiente, la fe viene del oír el mensaje.
2. *"**As a result**, they were filled with the Spirit."* (Hechos 2:4, adaptado) – Como resultado, fueron llenos del Espíritu.
3. *"**Owing to** his great mercy, he saved us."* (Tito 3:5, adaptado) – Debido a su gran misericordia, nos salvó.
4. *"**Thus**, death has been swallowed up in victory."* (1 Corintios 15:54, adaptado) – Así, la muerte ha sido devorada en victoria.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He prayed faithfully. **Consequently**, God answered.* (Oró fielmente. Por consiguiente, Dios respondió.)
- *She read the Bible daily. **As a result**, she grew in faith.* (Leía la Biblia diariamente. Como resultado, creció en fe.)
- ***Owing to** God's grace, we are forgiven.* (Debido a la gracia de Dios, somos perdonados.)
- ***Due to** his faithfulness, he was blessed.* (Debido a su fidelidad, fue bendecido.)
- *He repented. **Hence**, he was forgiven.* (Se arrepintió. Por lo tanto, fue perdonado.)
- *She trusted God; **thus**, she found peace.* (Confiaba en Dios; así que encontró paz.)

**Edificación:** Pablo explica que por gracia somos salvos mediante la fe. Aprendemos a usar conectores de causa y consecuencia para articular la lógica de la salvación.

---

### Lección 34 – "In Order That We Might Believe"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de propósito avanzados (*so that, in order that, with a view to, for the purpose of, lest*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"These are written in order that you may believe."* (Adaptado de Juan 20:31)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 20:30-31, ESV):** 
> *"Now Jesus did many other signs in the presence of the disciples, which are not written in this book; but these are written so that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God, and that by believing you may have life in his name."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| signs | señales | presence | presencia |
| written | escrito | believe | creer |
| Christ | Cristo | Son of God | Hijo de Dios |
| life | vida | | |

**Conectores de propósito:**

| Conector | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *so that* | + cláusula (con *may/might/will*) | *These are written **so that** you **may** believe.* |
| *in order that* | + cláusula (formal) | *He came **in order that** we **might** have life.* |
| *with a view to* | + -ing | *He preached **with a view to** saving souls.* |
| *for the purpose of* | + -ing | *The Bible was given **for the purpose of** teaching.* |
| *lest* | + subjuntivo (formal, para evitar) | *He warned them **lest** they **should** fall.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He sent his Son **so that** we might live through him."* (1 Juan 4:9, adaptado) – Envió a su Hijo para que vivamos por medio de él.
2. *"They prayed **in order that** they might receive the Spirit."* (Hechos 8:15) – Oración para que recibieran el Espíritu.
3. *"He gave the law **with a view to** revealing sin."* (Romanos 7:7, adaptado) – Dio la ley con miras a revelar el pecado.
4. *"Do not be deceived, **lest** you fall."* (1 Corintios 10:12, adaptado) – No te engañes, no sea que caigas.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I read the Bible **so that** I may grow in faith.* (Leo la Biblia para que crezca en fe.)
- *He prays every day **in order that** he might stay close to God.* (Ora cada día para que pueda permanecer cerca de Dios.)
- *She serves in the church **with a view to** helping others.* (Sirve en la iglesia con miras a ayudar a otros.)
- *The lesson was designed **for the purpose of** teaching the gospel.* (La lección fue diseñada con el propósito de enseñar el evangelio.)
- *Be watchful, **lest** you should fall into temptation.* (Velad, no sea que caigáis en tentación.)

**Edificación:** El Evangelio de Juan fue escrito con un propósito claro: que creamos. Aprendemos a usar conectores de propósito para expresar la intención detrás de las acciones bíblicas y nuestras propias acciones de fe.

---

### Lección 35 – Repaso: "Nevertheless, I Have Hope"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de conectores avanzados.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Nevertheless, I have hope in God."* (Adaptado de Hechos 24:15)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes conectores.

**Ejemplo:**
- *Christ died for us. **Moreover**, he rose from the dead.* (Adición)
- *He was crucified. **However**, he is alive.* (Contraste)
- ***Not only** did he suffer, **but also** he conquered death.* (Adición)
- *We have hope **because** Christ rose.* (Causa)
- *He was persecuted. **Nevertheless**, he rejoiced.* (Contraste)
- *We are saved **so that** we may serve.* (Propósito)
- ***Whereas** we were enemies, we are now friends.* (Contraste)
- *He died **so that** we might live.* (Propósito)
- *They preached boldly **with a view to** converting souls.* (Propósito)
- ***Due to** his great love, he gave his Son.* (Causa)

---

## UNIDAD 8: SUBJUNTIVO Y EXPRESIONES IDIOMÁTICAS AVANZADAS
*Lecciones 36 a 40*

---

### Lección 36 – "I Wish I Were There"
**Gramática focal:** Subjuntivo en expresiones de deseo (*I wish I were, if only I were, would that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I wish I were there with you."* (Adaptado de Romanos 1:11 – *"I long to see you"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 1:8-12, ESV):** 
> *"First, I thank my God through Jesus Christ for all of you, because your faith is proclaimed in all the world. For God is my witness, whom I serve with my spirit in the gospel of his Son, that without ceasing I mention you always in my prayers, asking that somehow by God's will I may now at last succeed in coming to you. For I long to see you, that I may impart to you some spiritual gift to strengthen you—that is, that we may be mutually encouraged by each other's faith, both yours and mine."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| proclaimed | proclamado | witness | testigo |
| without ceasing | sin cesar | mention | mencionar |
| somehow | de alguna manera | at last | por fin |
| succeed | tener éxito | long to | anhelar |
| impart | impartir | spiritual gift | don espiritual |
| strengthen | fortalecer | mutually | mutuamente |
| encouraged | animados | | |

**Subjuntivo en expresiones de deseo:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *I wish + past simple* | Deseo presente (situación irreal) | *I wish I **were** there.* |
| *I wish + past perfect* | Deseo pasado (arrepentimiento) | *I wish I **had known**.* |
| *I wish + would + infinitive* | Deseo futuro (queja/esperanza) | *I wish he **would come**.* |
| *If only + past simple* | Deseo enfático presente | *If only I **were** stronger.* |
| *If only + past perfect* | Deseo enfático pasado | *If only I **had prayed**.* |
| *Would that + past simple* | Deseo formal (arcaico) | ***Would that** we **were** there.* |
| *It is time + past simple* | Es hora de que... | *It is time we **prayed**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"I wish you **were** one of them."* (Gálatas 4:20, adaptado) – Ojalá fuerais uno de ellos.
2. *"If only we **had been** there!"* (Hechos 2:1, adaptado) – ¡Ojalá hubiéramos estado allí!
3. *"Would that they **were** wise!"* (Deuteronomio 32:29) – ¡Ojalá fueran sabios!
4. *"I wish he **would** return."* (Apocalipsis 22:20, adaptado) – Ojalá regresara.
5. *"It is time we **turned** to the Lord."* (Oseas 5:4, adaptado) – Es hora de que nos volvamos al Señor.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I wish I **were** more faithful.* (Ojalá fuera más fiel.)
- *I wish I **had prayed** before making that decision.* (Ojalá hubiera orado antes de tomar esa decisión.)
- *I wish she **would come** to church.* (Ojalá ella viniera a la iglesia.)
- *If only we **had known** the truth.* (¡Ojalá hubiéramos conocido la verdad!)
- *It is time we **repented**.* (Es hora de que nos arrepintamos.)
- *Would that we **were** all united!* (¡Ojalá estuviéramos todos unidos!)

**Edificación:** Pablo anhelaba ver a los romanos. Aprendemos a usar el subjuntivo en expresiones de deseo para articular nuestro anhelo espiritual y nuestro arrepentimiento.

---

### Lección 37 – "It Is Necessary That He Be Born Again"
**Gramática focal:** Subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad y juicio (*it is necessary that, it is essential that, I demand that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"It is necessary that he be born again."* (Adaptado de Juan 3:7 – *"You must be born again."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 3:1-8, ESV):** 
> *"Now there was a man of the Pharisees named Nicodemus, a ruler of the Jews. This man came to Jesus by night and said to him, 'Rabbi, we know that you are a teacher come from God, for no one can do these signs that you do unless God is with him.' Jesus answered him, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, unless one is born again he cannot see the kingdom of God.' Nicodemus said to him, 'How can a man be born when he is old? Can he enter a second time into his mother's womb and be born?' Jesus answered, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, unless one is born of water and the Spirit, he cannot enter the kingdom of God. That which is born of the flesh is flesh, and that which is born of the Spirit is spirit. Do not marvel that I said to you, "You must be born again." The wind blows where it wishes, and you hear its sound, but you do not know where it comes from or where it goes. So it is with everyone who is born of the Spirit.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| Pharisees | fariseos | ruler | gobernante |
| Nicodemus | Nicodemo | signs | señales |
| kingdom | reino | born again | nacido de nuevo |
| water | agua | Spirit | Espíritu |
| flesh | carne | marvel | maravillarse |
| wind | viento | sound | sonido |
| goes | va | | |

**Subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad y juicio:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *It is necessary that + sujeto + base form* | Necesidad | *It is necessary that he **be** born again.* |
| *It is essential that + sujeto + base form* | Esencial | *It is essential that we **believe**.* |
| *It is important that + sujeto + base form* | Importante | *It is important that he **repent**.* |
| *I demand that + sujeto + base form* | Exigencia | *I demand that he **leave**.* |
| *They recommended that + sujeto + base form* | Recomendación | *They recommended that we **pray**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"It is necessary that he **increase** and I **decrease**."* (Juan 3:30, adaptado) – Es necesario que él crezca y yo mengüe.
2. *"It is essential that we **love** one another."* (1 Juan 4:7, adaptado) – Es esencial que nos amemos unos a otros.
3. *"He commanded that they **go** and **preach**."* (Mateo 28:19, adaptado) – Mandó que fueran y predicaran.
4. *"They insisted that he **stay** with them."* (Lucas 24:29, adaptado) – Insistieron en que se quedara con ellos.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *It is necessary that we **pray** without ceasing.* (Es necesario que oremos sin cesar.)
- *It is essential that the church **serve** the community.* (Es esencial que la iglesia sirva a la comunidad.)
- *The pastor recommended that we **read** the Bible daily.* (El pastor recomendó que leyéramos la Biblia diariamente.)
- *The apostles commanded that they **believe** in Jesus.* (Los apóstoles mandaron que creyeran en Jesús.)
- *I demand that he **apologize** for his behavior.* (Exijo que se disculpe por su comportamiento.)

**Edificación:** Jesús le dice a Nicodemo: "Es necesario que nazcas de nuevo". Aprendemos a usar el subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad para expresar las exigencias esenciales de la fe cristiana.

---

### Lección 38 – "I Suggest That We Pray Without Ceasing"
**Gramática focal:** Subjuntivo en cláusulas de sugerencia, insistencia y recomendación (con *that* + base form).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"I suggest that we pray without ceasing."* (Adaptado de 1 Tesalonicenses 5:17)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Tesalonicenses 5:12-22, ESV):** 
> *"We ask you, brothers, to respect those who labor among you and are over you in the Lord and admonish you, and to esteem them very highly in love because of their work. Be at peace among yourselves. And we urge you, brothers, admonish the idle, encourage the fainthearted, help the weak, be patient with them all. See that no one repays anyone evil for evil, but always seek to do good to one another and to everyone. Rejoice always, pray without ceasing, give thanks in all circumstances; for this is the will of God in Christ Jesus for you. Do not quench the Spirit. Do not despise prophecies, but test everything; hold fast what is good. Abstain from every form of evil."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| respect | respetar | labor | trabajan |
| admonish | amonestar | esteem | estimar |
| at peace | en paz | urge | instar |
| idle | perezosos | fainthearted | de poco ánimo |
| weak | débiles | patient | paciente |
| repay | devolver | seek | buscar |
| rejoice | regocijarse | give thanks | dar gracias |
| circumstances | circunstancias | quench | apagar |
| despise | despreciar | test | probar |
| hold fast | retener | abstain | abstenerse |

**Subjuntivo con verbos de sugerencia e insistencia:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *suggest that + sujeto + base form* | *I **suggest that we pray**.* |
| *recommend that + sujeto + base form* | *I **recommend that he read**.* |
| *insist that + sujeto + base form* | *She **insists that he come**.* |
| *urge that + sujeto + base form* | *He **urged that they pray**.* |
| *propose that + sujeto + base form* | *They **proposed that we meet**.* |

**También se puede usar *should* (más común en inglés británico):**
- *I suggest that we **should** pray.*

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **suggested that they wait** for the Spirit."* (Hechos 1:4, adaptado) – Sugirió que esperaran el Espíritu.
2. *"They **insisted that he stay** with them."* (Lucas 24:29) – Insistieron en que se quedara con ellos.
3. *"He **urged that they repent**."* (Hechos 2:38, adaptado) – Instó a que se arrepintieran.
4. *"The apostle **recommended that they love** one another."* (Juan 15:12, adaptado) – El apóstol recomendó que se amaran unos a otros.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **suggest that we pray** together.* (Sugiero que oremos juntos.)
- *The pastor **recommends that we read** the book of Romans.* (El pastor recomienda que leamos el libro de Romanos.)
- *She **insists that he come** to the meeting.* (Ella insiste en que él venga a la reunión.)
- *They **urge that we be** more generous.* (Nos instan a que seamos más generosos.)
- *I **propose that the church help** the needy.* (Propongo que la iglesia ayude a los necesitados.)

**Edificación:** Pablo nos exhorta a orar sin cesar. Aprendemos a usar el subjuntivo en cláusulas de sugerencia e insistencia para proponer acciones de fe en la comunidad.

---

### Lección 39 – "He Acts As If He Had Never Sinned"
**Gramática focal:** Subjuntivo con *as if / as though* + past perfect; *it is high time* + past.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He acts as if he had never sinned."* (Adaptado de 1 Juan 1:9 – *"If we confess our sins, he is faithful and just to forgive us our sins."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Juan 1:5-10, ESV):** 
> *"This is the message we have heard from him and proclaim to you, that God is light, and in him is no darkness at all. If we say we have fellowship with him while we walk in darkness, we lie and do not practice the truth. But if we walk in the light, as he is in the light, we have fellowship with one another, and the blood of Jesus his Son cleanses us from all sin. If we say we have no sin, we deceive ourselves, and the truth is not in us. If we confess our sins, he is faithful and just to forgive us our sins and to cleanse us from all unrighteousness. If we say we have not sinned, we make him a liar, and his word is not in us."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| message | mensaje | proclaim | proclamar |
| light | luz | darkness | oscuridad |
| fellowship | comunión | lie | mentir |
| practice | practicar | blood | sangre |
| cleanses | limpia | deceive | engañar |
| confess | confesar | faithful | fiel |
| just | justo | forgive | perdonar |
| unrighteousness | injusticia | liar | mentiroso |

**Subjuntivo con *as if* y *as though*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *as if + past simple* | Situación irreal presente | *He acts **as if he were** a saint.* |
| *as if + past perfect* | Situación irreal pasada | *He acts **as if he had never sinned**.* |
| *as though + past simple* | Situación irreal presente | *She speaks **as though she knew** everything.* |
| *as though + past perfect* | Situación irreal pasada | *They looked **as though they had seen** a ghost.* |

**Uso de *it is high time*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *It is high time + past simple* | Ya es hora de que (énfasis) | *It is high time we **repented**.* |
| *It is about time + past simple* | Ya es hora de que | *It is about time we **prayed**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He spoke **as if he were** the Messiah."* (Juan 4:25-26, adaptado) – Habló como si fuera el Mesías.
2. *"She looked **as though she had seen** an angel."* (Hechos 12:13-15, adaptado) – Parecía como si hubiera visto un ángel.
3. *"They acted **as if they had never known** God."* (Romanos 1:21, adaptado) – Actuaron como si nunca hubieran conocido a Dios.
4. *"It is high time we **turned** to the Lord."* (Oseas 5:4, adaptado) – Ya es hora de que nos volvamos al Señor.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He preaches **as if he were** an apostle.* (Predica como si fuera un apóstol.)
- *She prays **as though she had known** God for years.* (Ora como si conociera a Dios por años.)
- *They act **as if they had never sinned**.* (Actúan como si nunca hubieran pecado.)
- *It is high time we **confessed** our sins.* (Ya es hora de que confesemos nuestros pecados.)
- *He spoke **as though he were** a prophet.* (Habló como si fuera un profeta.)
- *She lives **as if she had been** saved.* (Vive como si hubiera sido salva.)

**Edificación:** Juan nos llama a confesar nuestros pecados. Aprendemos a usar "as if" para expresar la realidad de la transformación que Dios produce en nosotros, y "it is high time" para urgir a la acción espiritual.

---

### Lección 40 – Repaso Final: "I Am the Resurrection and the Life"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de todos los temas del nivel B2.

**Versículo Clave (Texto de Cierre):** 
> *"I am the resurrection and the life. Whoever believes in me, though he die, yet shall he live, and everyone who lives and believes in me shall never die. Do you believe this?"* — **Juan 11:25-26**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 11:17-27, ESV):** 
> *"Now when Jesus came, he found that Lazarus had already been in the tomb four days. Bethany was near Jerusalem, about two miles off, and many of the Jews had come to Martha and Mary to console them concerning their brother. So when Martha heard that Jesus was coming, she went and met him, but Mary remained seated in the house. Martha said to Jesus, 'Lord, if you had been here, my brother would not have died. But even now I know that whatever you ask from God, God will give you.' Jesus said to her, 'Your brother will rise again.' Martha said to him, 'I know that he will rise again in the resurrection on the last day.' Jesus said to her, 'I am the resurrection and the life. Whoever believes in me, though he die, yet shall he live, and everyone who lives and believes in me shall never die. Do you believe this?' She said to him, 'Yes, Lord; I believe that you are the Christ, the Son of God, who is coming into the world.'"*

**Vocabulario final:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| resurrection | resurrección | life | vida |
| believes | cree | die | morir |
| shall live | vivirá | never die | nunca morirá |
| tomb | tumba | Bethany | Betania |
| Jerusalem | Jerusalén | consoled | consolado |
| Martha | Marta | Mary | María |
| Christ | Cristo | Son of God | Hijo de Dios |

---

## Actividad Final de Evaluación – Nivel B2

El estudiante debe escribir un **ensayo teológico-personal** de **300-400 palabras** sobre el siguiente tema:

**"¿Qué significa para ti que Jesús es la resurrección y la vida?"**

Debe incluir al menos **15** de las siguientes estructuras avanzadas del nivel B2 (marcar claramente cada una):

1. **Future Perfect** (*will have + pp*)
2. **Future Perfect Continuous** (*will have been + -ing*)
3. **Past Perfect Continuous** (*had been + -ing*)
4. **Voz pasiva con modales en pasado** (*must have been done*)
5. **Voz pasiva con reporting verbs** (*is said to have*)
6. **Pasiva con verbos ditransitivos** (*was given*)
7. **Gerundio pasivo** (*being loved*)
8. **Infinitivo pasivo** (*to be saved*)
9. **Tercer condicional** (*If + past perfect, would have + pp*)
10. **Condicional mixto** (*If + past perfect, would + infinitive*)
11. **I wish / If only** (expresando arrepentimiento o deseo)
12. **As if / as though** (con subjuntivo)
13. **It is time** (con pasado)
14. **Inversión con adverbios negativos** (*Never have I...*)
15. **Cleft sentence** (*It was... who/that*)
16. **Inversión con *only*** (*Only when... do I...*)
17. **Discurso indirecto** (con reporting verb + infinitivo)
18. **Reporting verb con subjuntivo** (*suggest that he pray*)
19. **Conector de adición** (*moreover, furthermore*)
20. **Conector de contraste** (*nevertheless, whereas*)
21. **Conector de consecuencia** (*consequently, hence*)
22. **Conector de propósito** (*so that, in order that*)
23. **Subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad** (*It is necessary that he be*)

---

## Ejemplo de Ensayo Final (para guía del estudiante):

> *"I am the resurrection and the life." These words, spoken by Jesus to Martha, have profoundly shaped my faith. **Never have I heard** such a powerful declaration about the hope we have in Christ. **It was Jesus who** spoke these words, and **what they mean to me** is everything.*

> *Before I believed, I **had been living** without hope. **If I had known** the truth earlier, I **would have changed** my life sooner. I **wish I had understood** the gospel when I was younger. **If only I had read** the Bible before! However, God **is said to have** been patient with me, and He **has given me** a new life. I **have been saved** by grace through faith.*

> *I **look forward to being with** Christ forever. **Not only did he die** for my sins, **but also he rose** from the dead. **Consequently**, I have eternal life. **Moreover**, he promised that I **will have been** with him in glory. I **suggest that we all believe** in him, for **it is necessary that we be** born again.*

> *The Bible **was written** so that we may believe. **As if I had never known** such peace, now I live in hope. **It is high time we all turned** to the Lord. **Only when we believe** do we receive eternal life. I **wish you would also believe** in him, for **he is the resurrection and the life**. **Nevertheless**, the choice is ours. **Consequently**, I choose to follow him.*

---

## Apéndice 1: Verbos de Reporte Avanzados

| Verbo | Estructura | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *claim* | *claim to do / that* | afirmar |
| *deny* | *deny -ing / that* | negar |
| *admit* | *admit -ing / that* | admitir |
| *insist* | *insist on -ing / that* | insistir |
| *suggest* | *suggest -ing / that* | sugerir |
| *recommend* | *recommend -ing / that* | recomendar |
| *urge* | *urge someone to do / that* | instar |
| *persuade* | *persuade someone to do* | persuadir |
| *convince* | *convince someone to do* | convencer |
| *warn* | *warn someone not to do* | advertir |
| *advise* | *advise someone to do* | aconsejar |
| *encourage* | *encourage someone to do* | animar |
| *remind* | *remind someone to do* | recordar |
| *command* | *command someone to do* | mandar |
| *propose* | *propose -ing / that* | proponer |
| *demand* | *demand that* | exigir |

---

## Apéndice 2: Verbos Frasales Avanzados

| Verbo Frasal | Significado | Ejemplo Bíblico |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *hold fast* | retener | *Hold fast what is good.* |
| *give up* | rendirse | *Do not give up.* |
| *turn away* | apartarse | *Turn away from evil.* |
| *look forward to* | esperar con ansias | *I look forward to seeing him.* |
| *come forward* | presentarse | *A centurion came forward.* |
| *go through* | pasar por | *He went through suffering.* |
| *stand by* | mantenerse fiel | *He stood by his faith.* |
| *put up with* | soportar | *He put up with persecution.* |

---

## Apéndice 3: Conectores Avanzados

| Categoría | Conectores |
|:---|:---|
| **Adición** | *moreover, furthermore, in addition, besides, not only... but also* |
| **Contraste** | *nevertheless, nonetheless, whereas, while, yet, albeit, although, though, even though, despite, in spite of* |
| **Causa** | *because, since, as, for, owing to, due to* |
| **Consecuencia** | *consequently, as a result, hence, thus, therefore, so* |
| **Propósito** | *so that, in order that, with a view to, for the purpose of, lest* |
| **Condición** | *if, unless, provided that, as long as, in case* |

---

## Conclusión del Curso

Al completar este nivel B2, el estudiante será capaz de:

- Comprender las ideas principales de textos complejos que tratan temas concretos y abstractos, incluyendo la Escritura en versiones estándar (ESV, NIV).
- Interactuar con hablantes nativos con un grado suficiente de fluidez y naturalidad.
- Producir textos claros y detallados sobre una amplia gama de temas, incluyendo la teología y la vida cristiana.
- Expresar opiniones, argumentos y puntos de vista con precisión y matices.

**Edificación Final:**

> *"Y conoceréis la verdad, y la verdad os hará libres."* — Juan 8:32

El estudiante ha recorrido un camino desde el nivel A1 hasta el B2. Ahora puede leer la Biblia en inglés en versiones estándar (ESV, NIV) con comprensión profunda, puede discutir su fe con otros en inglés con fluidez y precisión, y puede seguir creciendo en el conocimiento de la Palabra. Este curso ha sido un instrumento para que la Palabra de Dios more abundantemente en su corazón en el idioma inglés.

**"Toda la Escritura es inspirada por Dios y útil para enseñar, para redargüir, para corregir, para instruir en justicia, a fin de que el hombre de Dios sea perfecto, enteramente preparado para toda buena obra."** – 2 Timoteo 3:16-17

---

**¡Gloria a Dios por su Palabra!**

# CURSO DE INGLÉS BÍBLICO – NIVEL C1 (MCER)

## Documento Maestro del Estudiante

---

## Introducción

Este curso es la continuación natural del **Nivel B2** y está diseñado para llevar al estudiante desde un nivel intermedio superior (B2) hasta un **nivel avanzado (C1)** del Marco Común Europeo de Referencia (MCER). En este nivel, el estudiante pasa de ser un "usuario independiente avanzado" a un "usuario competente" que puede comprender una amplia gama de textos exigentes y expresarse con fluidez, espontaneidad y precisión.

**Versiones de la Biblia recomendadas:**
- **English Standard Version (ESV)** – para precisión teológica y riqueza literaria, con un estilo formal que refleja el inglés académico.
- **New American Standard Bible (NASB)** – para estudio detallado con traducción literal.
- **King James Version (KJV)** – para apreciación de la lengua inglesa clásica (opcional, para análisis literario).
- **New International Version (NIV)** – para claridad y equilibrio.
- **New Living Translation (NLT)** – para pasajes narrativos y poéticos.
- **The Message (MSG)** – para comparación de estilos y expresiones idiomáticas contemporáneas.

**Metodología:**
> *"Leemos la Biblia para aprender inglés, y no al revés."*

Cada lección se centra en **un pasaje bíblico extenso (5-15 versículos)** que contiene la estructura gramatical objetivo. La dinámica es:
1. **Lectura extensiva y análisis textual** – identificar vocabulario avanzado, estructuras gramaticales complejas, figuras retóricas y estilo literario.
2. **Análisis gramatical profundo** – el estudiante descubre y analiza las reglas a través del texto.
3. **Aplicación al contexto cotidiano y académico** – el estudiante utiliza las estructuras para escribir ensayos, dar discursos y participar en debates.
4. **Producción escrita y oral avanzada** – el estudiante expresa su fe usando estructuras sofisticadas y matices lingüísticos.
5. **Discusión teológica y exegética** – el estudiante utiliza el inglés para profundizar en la comprensión de la Escritura y articular argumentos teológicos.
6. **Análisis literario y retórico** – el estudiante aprecia la belleza y el poder del lenguaje bíblico.

---

## Estructura del Curso

**Total de lecciones:** 40 lecciones

**Unidades:** 8 unidades de 5 lecciones cada una

**Duración estimada por lección:** 3.5 - 4 horas de instrucción + 4-5 horas de trabajo autónomo

**Duración total estimada:** 140-160 horas de instrucción + 160-200 horas de trabajo autónomo

---

## Contenido Gramatical del Nivel C1

| Categoría | Estructuras C1 |
|:---|:---|
| **Tiempos Verbales** | Future Perfect (profundización); Future Perfect Continuous; Past Perfect Continuous con énfasis en duración; Secuencia de tiempos compleja |
| **Voz Pasiva** | Pasiva con verbos de percepción (*He was seen to leave*); Pasiva impersonal (*It is understood that...*); Pasiva con verbos causativos (*have/get something done*); Pasiva en discurso indirecto complejo |
| **Condicionales** | Condicionales mixtos avanzados (todos los tiempos); Inversión en condicionales (*Had I known...*); *Were I to...*; *If it were not for...*; *But for...* |
| **Subjuntivo** | Subjuntivo en cláusulas de deseo; Subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad (profundización); Subjuntivo en cláusulas de concesión (*be that as it may*); *Whether* + subjuntivo |
| **Inversión y Énfasis** | Inversión con adverbios negativos (profundización); Inversión con *only* (profundización); Inversión con *so/such... that*; Inversión con *not until*; Inversión en condicionales; Inversión con *neither/nor*; Inversión con *as* (*As do I*) |
| **Gerundios e Infinitivos** | Gerundios e infinitivos pasivos y perfectivos (profundización); Verbos con cambio de significado (profundización); Construcciones complejas (*It is worth considering*); Verbos con preposición + gerundio (profundización); Construcciones con *to be* + infinitivo perfectivo |
| **Discurso Indirecto** | Backshifting avanzado con todos los tiempos; Reporting verbs con diferentes patrones (*claim to have, deny having*); Discurso indirecto con modales (*would, could, should, might*); Preguntas indirectas complejas; Estilo indirecto libre (narrativa literaria) |
| **Conectores** | Conectores de adición, contraste, causa, consecuencia, propósito, concesión, condición (profundización); Conectores formales (*notwithstanding, inasmuch as, insofar as, whereas, albeit, whilst*); Conectores de reformulación (*that is to say, namely, in other words*); Conectores de ejemplificación (*for instance, to illustrate*); Conectores de conclusión (*in conclusion, to sum up*) |
| **Cláusulas** | Cláusulas de relativo (profundización); Cláusulas de concesión (*Although, even though, whilst, albeit*); Cláusulas de modo (*as, just as, as if, as though*); Cláusulas de propósito (*lest, for fear that*); Cláusulas de resultado (*so... that, such... that*); Cláusulas de tiempo avanzadas (*the moment, no sooner... than, scarcely... when*) |
