| **Nominalización** | Transformación de verbos en sustantivos (*belief, salvation, redemption*); Estilo formal y académico |
| **Énfasis y Estilo** | Cleft sentences (profundización); Pseudo-cleft sentences; Inversión (profundización); Fronting; *It is... that* (estructuras enfáticas); *What... is/was* (estructuras enfáticas) |
| **Participios** | Participios presentes y pasados en frases absolutas; Participios como adjetivos (profundización); Construcciones de participio en estilo literario |
| **Modales** | Modales de deducción en pasado (profundización); Modales de obligación y necesidad (*needn't have, didn't need to*); Modales de crítica (*might have, could have, would have*); Modales en condicionales; Modales en discurso indirecto |
| **Puntuación y Estilo** | Uso de punto y coma, dos puntos, guiones; Estilo formal e informal; Registro y tono; Figuras retóricas en el texto bíblico |

---

## UNIDAD 1: INVERSIÓN Y ESTRUCTURAS ENFÁTICAS AVANZADAS
*Lecciones 1 a 5*

---

### Lección 1 – "Had I Known, I Would Have Acted Differently"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión en condicionales (*Had I known, Were I to go, Should you need*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Had I known that this would be the last time I would see him, I would have acted differently."* (Adaptado de 2 Reyes 2:9-10 – *"Let me inherit a double portion of your spirit"* y el contexto de la despedida de Elías)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 2 Reyes 2:1-12, ESV):** 
> *"Now when the Lord was about to take Elijah up to heaven by a whirlwind, Elijah and Elisha were on their way from Gilgal. And Elijah said to Elisha, 'Please stay here, for the Lord has sent me as far as Bethel.' But Elisha said, 'As the Lord lives, and as you yourself live, I will not leave you.' So they went down to Bethel. And the sons of the prophets who were in Bethel came out to Elisha and said to him, 'Do you know that today the Lord will take away your master from over you?' And he said, 'Yes, I know it; keep quiet.' Elijah said to him, 'Elisha, please stay here, for the Lord has sent me to Jericho.' But he said, 'As the Lord lives, and as you yourself live, I will not leave you.' So they came to Jericho. The sons of the prophets who were at Jericho drew near to Elisha and said to him, 'Do you know that today the Lord will take away your master from over you?' And he answered, 'Yes, I know it; keep quiet.' Then Elijah said to him, 'Please stay here, for the Lord has sent me to the Jordan.' But he said, 'As the Lord lives, and as you yourself live, I will not leave you.' So the two of them went on. Fifty men of the sons of the prophets also went and stood at some distance from them, as they both were standing by the Jordan. Then Elijah took his cloak and rolled it up and struck the water, and the water was parted to the one side and to the other, till the two of them could go over on dry ground. When they had crossed, Elijah said to Elisha, 'Ask what I shall do for you, before I am taken from you.' And Elisha said, 'Please let there be a double portion of your spirit on me.' And he said, 'You have asked a hard thing; yet, if you see me as I am being taken from you, it shall be so for you, but if you do not, it shall not be so.' And as they still went on and talked, behold, chariots of fire and horses of fire separated the two of them. And Elijah went up by a whirlwind into heaven. And Elisha saw it and he cried, 'My father, my father! The chariots of Israel and its horsemen!' And he saw him no more."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| whirlwind | torbellino | master | amo / señor |
| keep quiet | guardar silencio | double portion | doble porción |
| cloak | manto | rolled it up | lo enrolló |
| struck | golpeó | parted | se dividió |
| dry ground | tierra seca | chariots | carros |
| horsemen | jinetes | | |

**Inversión en condicionales (estructuras formales):**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Had + sujeto + pp, + sujeto + would have + pp* | Si hubiera... (tercer condicional invertido) | ***Had I known**, I would have acted differently.* |
| *Were + sujeto + to + infinitivo, + sujeto + would + infinitivo* | Si fuera a... (segundo condicional invertido) | ***Were I to go**, I would see him.* |
| *Should + sujeto + base form, + sujeto + will/would + infinitivo* | Si llegara a... (primer condicional invertido) | ***Should you need** help, I will be there.* |
| *Had it not been for + sustantivo, + sujeto + would have + pp* | Si no hubiera sido por... | ***Had it not been for** his faith, he would have given up.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con inversión condicional:**

1. *"**Had** you **believed** in Moses, you **would have believed** in me."* (Juan 5:46, adaptado) – Si hubierais creído en Moisés, me habríais creído a mí.
2. *"**Had** they **known** the Lord, they **would not have** crucified him."* (1 Corintios 2:8, adaptado) – Si hubieran conocido al Señor, no lo habrían crucificado.
3. *"**Were** I **to** boast, I **would** not be foolish."* (2 Corintios 11:16, adaptado) – Si fuera a jactarme, no sería insensato.
4. *"**Should** anyone **ask** you, tell them the Lord needs it."* (Marcos 11:3, adaptado) – Si alguien os preguntara, decidle que el Señor lo necesita.
5. *"**Had it not been for** the Lord's mercy, we **would have been** consumed."* (Lamentaciones 3:22, adaptado) – Si no hubiera sido por la misericordia del Señor, habríamos sido consumidos.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Arrepentimiento y reflexión formal):**

- ***Had I prayed** more, I **would have experienced** greater peace.* (Si hubiera orado más, habría experimentado mayor paz.)
- ***Had she listened** to the wisdom of her elders, she **would not have made** that mistake.* (Si hubiera escuchado la sabiduría de sus mayores, no habría cometido ese error.)
- ***Were I to give** you advice, I **would** tell you to trust in God.* (Si fuera a darte un consejo, te diría que confíes en Dios.)
- ***Should you feel** lost, remember that God is with you.* (Si llegaras a sentirte perdido, recuerda que Dios está contigo.)
- ***Had it not been for** my faith, I **would have lost** all hope.* (Si no hubiera sido por mi fe, habría perdido toda esperanza.)
- ***Were we to have** more faith, we **would see** more miracles.* (Si tuviéramos más fe, veríamos más milagros.)

**Edificación:** Elisha pidió una doble porción del espíritu de Elías. Aprendemos a usar la inversión condicional para expresar arrepentimiento, reflexión y consejos formales, como los que encontramos en la literatura sapiencial.

---

### Lección 2 – "Never Have I Seen Such Righteousness"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión con adverbios negativos y restrictivos (profundización): *never, seldom, rarely, hardly, scarcely, no sooner, not only, not until, only, neither/nor*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Never have I seen such righteousness."* (Adaptado de Mateo 5:20 – *"Unless your righteousness exceeds that of the scribes and Pharisees..."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 5:17-20, ESV):** 
> *"Do not think that I have come to abolish the Law or the Prophets; I have not come to abolish them but to fulfill them. For truly, I say to you, until heaven and earth pass away, not an iota, not a dot, will pass from the Law until all is accomplished. Therefore whoever relaxes one of the least of these commandments and teaches others to do the same will be called least in the kingdom of heaven, but whoever does them and teaches them will be called great in the kingdom of heaven. For I tell you, unless your righteousness exceeds that of the scribes and Pharisees, you will never enter the kingdom of heaven."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| abolish | abolir | fulfill | cumplir |
| iota | jota (letra más pequeña) | dot | tilde |
| accomplished | cumplido | relaxes | relaja |
| least | más pequeño | exceeds | sobrepasa |
| scribes | escribas | Pharisees | fariseos |

**Inversión con adverbios negativos/restrictivos:**

| Adverbio | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Never* | *Never + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Never have I seen** such righteousness.* |
| *Seldom* | *Seldom + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Seldom do we witness** such faith.* |
| *Rarely* | *Rarely + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Rarely does he speak** of his suffering.* |
| *Hardly / Scarcely* | *Hardly + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Hardly had he spoken** when the crowd fell silent.* |
| *No sooner... than* | *No sooner + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + than* | ***No sooner had he arrived** than he began to preach.* |
| *Not only... but also* | *Not only + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + but also* | ***Not only did he heal** the sick, but also he raised the dead.* |
| *Not until* | *Not until + cláusula + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Not until the Spirit came** did they understand.* |
| *Only* | *Only + adverbio + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Only when we pray** do we find peace.* |
| *Neither / Nor* | *Neither/Nor + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Neither did he sin**, nor did he betray his faith.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Never have I heard** such teaching!"* (Marcos 1:27, adaptado) – ¡Nunca he oído tal enseñanza!
2. *"**Seldom have we witnessed** such devotion."* (Hechos 2:44-45, adaptado) – Rara vez hemos presenciado tal devoción.
3. *"**Not until he had risen** did they understand the Scriptures."* (Lucas 24:45, adaptado) – No fue hasta que resucitó que entendieron las Escrituras.
4. *"**Not only did he come** to save, but also to serve."* (Marcos 10:45, adaptado) – No solo vino a salvar, sino también a servir.
5. *"**Nor did he** consider equality with God as something to be grasped."* (Filipenses 2:6, adaptado) – Ni consideró el ser igual a Dios como algo a qué aferrarse.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Énfasis y estilo formal):**

- ***Never have I experienced** such peace as I have in Christ.* (Nunca he experimentado tanta paz como la que tengo en Cristo.)
- ***Seldom do we reflect** on the depth of God's love.* (Rara vez reflexionamos sobre la profundidad del amor de Dios.)
- ***Rarely does he miss** a Sunday service.* (Raramente falta a un servicio dominical.)
- ***No sooner had I prayed** than I felt God's presence.* (Apenas había orado cuando sentí la presencia de Dios.)
- ***Not only did she forgive** him, but she also prayed for him.* (No solo le perdonó, sino que también oró por él.)
- ***Not until I read** the Bible did I understand the truth.* (No fue hasta que leí la Biblia que entendí la verdad.)
- ***Only by faith can we be saved.** * (Solo por fe podemos ser salvos.)
- ***Neither did he abandon** his faith, nor did he compromise his values.* (Ni abandonó su fe ni comprometió sus valores.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos llama a una justicia que supere la de los fariseos. Aprendemos a usar la inversión con adverbios negativos para enfatizar la rareza de la verdadera fe y la grandeza de la obra de Cristo.

---

### Lección 3 – "Such Was His Faith That He Believed"
**Gramática focal:** Inversión con *so... that* y *such... that*; *so* y *such* con inversión.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Such was his faith that he believed God."* (Adaptado de Romanos 4:20-21 – *"No unbelief made him waver concerning the promise of God, but he grew strong in his faith as he gave glory to God, fully convinced that God was able to do what he had promised."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 4:18-25, ESV):** 
> *"In hope he believed against hope, that he should become the father of many nations, as he had been told, 'So shall your offspring be.' He did not weaken in faith when he considered his own body, which was as good as dead (since he was about a hundred years old), or when he considered the barrenness of Sarah's womb. No unbelief made him waver concerning the promise of God, but he grew strong in his faith as he gave glory to God, fully convinced that God was able to do what he had promised. That is why his faith was 'counted to him as righteousness.' But the words 'it was counted to him' were not written for his sake alone, but for ours also. It will be counted to us who believe in him who raised from the dead Jesus our Lord, who was delivered up for our trespasses and raised for our justification."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| against hope | contra toda esperanza | offspring | descendencia |
| weaken | debilitar | considered | consideró |
| barrenness | esterilidad | waver | vacilar |
| promise | promesa | fully convinced | plenamente convencido |
| counted | contado / imputado | righteousness | justicia |
| trespasses | transgresiones | justification | justificación |

**Inversión con *so... that* y *such... that*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *So + adjetivo/adverbio + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + that...* | ***So great was his faith** that he believed God.* |
| *Such + be + sujeto + that...* | ***Such was his faith** that he believed God.* |
| *Such + sustantivo + be + sujeto + that...* | ***Such a man was he** that all respected him.* |
| *To such an extent + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + that...* | ***To such an extent did he trust** God that he never wavered.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**So great was** the love of God that he gave his only Son."* (Juan 3:16, adaptado) – Tan grande fue el amor de Dios que dio a su único Hijo.
2. *"**Such was** the faith of the centurion that Jesus marveled."* (Mateo 8:10, adaptado) – Tal fue la fe del centurión que Jesús se maravilló.
3. *"**So many were** the miracles that they could not all be recorded."* (Juan 21:25, adaptado) – Tan numerosos fueron los milagros que no pudieron ser registrados todos.
4. *"**Such was** the power of the Holy Spirit that thousands believed."* (Hechos 2:41, adaptado) – Tal fue el poder del Espíritu Santo que miles creyeron.
5. *"**So clearly did** he speak that everyone understood."* (Marcos 7:37, adaptado) – Tan claramente habló que todos entendieron.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Énfasis en cualidades y resultados):**

- ***So great is** God's mercy that he forgives all who repent.* (Tan grande es la misericordia de Dios que perdona a todos los que se arrepienten.)
- ***Such was** her devotion that she prayed without ceasing.* (Tal era su devoción que oraba sin cesar.)
- ***So powerfully did** he preach that the whole congregation was moved.* (Tan poderosamente predicó que toda la congregación fue conmovida.)
- ***Such was** the miracle that no one could deny it.* (Tal fue el milagro que nadie pudo negarlo.)
- ***So deep is** God's love that it surpasses all understanding.* (Tan profundo es el amor de Dios que sobrepasa todo entendimiento.)
- ***To such an extent did** he trust God that he never doubted.* (Hasta tal punto confió en Dios que nunca dudó.)

**Edificación:** Pablo describe la fe de Abraham: tan grande era su fe que creyó contra toda esperanza. Aprendemos a usar la inversión con *so... that* y *such... that* para enfatizar la grandeza de la fe, el amor y el poder de Dios.

---

### Lección 4 – "What God Has Joined Together, Let No One Separate"
**Gramática focal:** Fronting (colocar elementos al principio para énfasis); *What* y *All* con inversión.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"What therefore God has joined together, let not man separate."* — **Mateo 19:6**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 19:1-9, ESV):** 
> *"Now when Jesus had finished these sayings, he went away from Galilee and entered the region of Judea beyond the Jordan. And large crowds followed him, and he healed them there. And Pharisees came up to him and tested him by asking, 'Is it lawful to divorce one's wife for any cause?' He answered, 'Have you not read that he who created them from the beginning made them male and female, and said, "Therefore a man shall leave his father and his mother and hold fast to his wife, and the two shall become one flesh"? So they are no longer two but one flesh. What therefore God has joined together, let not man separate.' They said to him, 'Why then did Moses command one to give a certificate of divorce and to send her away?' He said to them, 'Because of your hardness of heart Moses allowed you to divorce your wives, but from the beginning it was not so. And I say to you: whoever divorces his wife, except for sexual immorality, and marries another, commits adultery.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| sayings | enseñanzas / dichos | region | región |
| Pharisees | fariseos | lawful | lícito |
| divorce | divorciar | cause | causa |
| male | varón | female | hembra |
| hold fast | aferrarse | one flesh | una sola carne |
| certificate | certificado | hardness of heart | dureza de corazón |
| allowed | permitió | sexual immorality | inmoralidad sexual |
| commits adultery | comete adulterio | | |

**Fronting (colocar elementos al principio para énfasis):**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Objeto + verbo + sujeto* | ***What God has joined together**, let not man separate.* |
| *Complemento + verbo + sujeto* | ***In him** we have redemption.* |
| *Adverbio + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Truly** I say to you.* |
| *What + sujeto + verbo + be + complemento* | ***What I desire** is mercy, not sacrifice.* |
| *All + sujeto + verbo + be + complemento* | ***All I know** is that I was blind, but now I see.* |

**Estructuras con *What* y *All* (pseudo-cleft sentences):**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *What + sujeto + verbo + be + complemento* | Enfatizar un elemento | ***What I believe** is the gospel.* |
| *All + sujeto + verbo + be + complemento* | Enfatizar la única cosa | ***All I want** is to follow Jesus.* |
| *The one who + verbo + be + complemento* | Enfatizar el sujeto | ***The one who believes** will be saved.* |
| *It be + sujeto/objeto + that/who + cláusula* | Cleft sentence | ***It was Jesus who** saved me.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con fronting:**

1. *"**In him** we live and move and have our being."* (Hechos 17:28) – En él vivimos, nos movemos y existimos.
2. *"**The truth** I tell you."* (Juan 16:7, adaptado) – La verdad os digo.
3. *"**Mercy** I desire, not sacrifice."* (Mateo 9:13) – Misericordia deseo, no sacrificio.
4. *"**What I fear** is that I may have labored in vain."* (Gálatas 4:11, adaptado) – Lo que temo es que haya trabajado en vano.
5. *"**All we like sheep** have gone astray."* (Isaías 53:6) – Todos nosotros, como ovejas, nos hemos descarriado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Énfasis y estilo formal):**

- ***What I believe** is that Jesus is the Son of God.* (Lo que creo es que Jesús es el Hijo de Dios.)
- ***All I need** is your love.* (Todo lo que necesito es tu amor.)
- ***In God** we trust.* (En Dios confiamos.)
- ***What he taught** was revolutionary.* (Lo que enseñó fue revolucionario.)
- ***The one who perseveres** will receive the crown of life.* (El que persevera recibirá la corona de vida.)
- ***Mercy** and **grace** I have received from the Lord.* (Misericordia y gracia he recibido del Señor.)
- ***What I desire most** is to know Christ.* (Lo que más deseo es conocer a Cristo.)

**Edificación:** Jesús declara que lo que Dios ha unido, el hombre no lo separe. Aprendemos a usar el fronting para enfatizar las verdades fundamentales de la fe, colocando el objeto o complemento al principio de la oración.

---

### Lección 5 – Repaso: "Never Have I Heard Such Words"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de inversión, fronting y estructuras enfáticas.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Never have I heard such words!"* (Adaptado de Juan 7:46 – *"No one ever spoke like this man!"*)

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 12 oraciones usando diferentes estructuras de inversión y fronting.

**Ejemplo:**
1. ***Never have I seen** such faith.** (Inversión con *never*)
2. ***Seldom do we witness** such devotion.** (Inversión con *seldom*)
3. ***No sooner had he spoken** than the crowd fell silent.** (Inversión con *no sooner*)
4. ***Not only did he heal**, but also he raised the dead.** (Inversión con *not only*)
5. ***Not until I prayed** did I find peace.** (Inversión con *not until*)
6. ***Only by faith can we be saved.** * (Inversión con *only*)
7. ***So great was his faith** that he believed God.** (Inversión con *so... that*)
8. ***Such was the miracle** that all were amazed.** (Inversión con *such... that*)
9. ***Had I known** the truth, I would have acted differently.** (Inversión condicional)
10. ***Were I to speak** of his love, I would never finish.** (Inversión condicional)
11. ***What I believe** is the gospel.** (Pseudo-cleft)
12. ***All I want** is to follow Jesus.** (Pseudo-cleft)

---

## UNIDAD 2: CLAUSULAS COMPLEJAS Y MODALES AVANZADOS
*Lecciones 6 a 10*

---

### Lección 6 – "Notwithstanding, I Have Hope"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de concesión avanzados (*notwithstanding, albeit, whereas, whilst, in spite of the fact that, despite the fact that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Notwithstanding, I have hope in God."* (Adaptado de Hechos 24:15 – *"I have hope in God"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 24:10-16, ESV):** 
> *"And when the governor had nodded to him to speak, Paul replied: 'Knowing that for many years you have been a judge over this nation, I cheerfully make my defense. You can verify that it is not more than twelve days since I went up to worship in Jerusalem, and they did not find me disputing with anyone or stirring up a crowd in the temple, nor in the synagogues nor in the city. Neither can they prove to you what they now bring up against me. But this I confess to you, that according to the Way, which they call a sect, I worship the God of our fathers, believing everything laid down by the Law and written in the Prophets, having a hope in God, which these men themselves accept, that there will be a resurrection of both the just and the unjust. So I always take pains to have a clear conscience toward both God and man.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| governor | gobernador | nodded | asintió |
| cheerfully | alegremente | defense | defensa |
| verify | verificar | disputing | discutiendo |
| stirring up | alborotando | synagogues | sinagogas |
| prove | probar | confess | confesar |
| sect | secta | laid down | establecido |
| just | justo | unjust | injusto |
| take pains | esforzarse | conscience | conciencia |

**Conectores de concesión avanzados:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *notwithstanding* | Sin embargo (formal) | ***Notwithstanding**, I have hope.* |
| *albeit* | Aunque (+ adjetivo/frase) | *He was weak, **albeit** determined.* |
| *whereas* | Mientras que (contraste) | *He suffered, **whereas** others prospered.* |
| *whilst* | Mientras que (formal) | *He prayed, **whilst** others slept.* |
| *in spite of the fact that* | A pesar de que (+ cláusula) | ***In spite of the fact that** he was persecuted, he rejoiced.* |
| *despite the fact that* | A pesar de que (+ cláusula) | ***Despite the fact that** he was weak, he was strong.* |
| *for all that* | A pesar de todo | *He suffered; **for all that**, he trusted God.* |
| *be that as it may* | Sea como sea | ***Be that as it may**, I believe in God.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Notwithstanding**, the Lord was with me."* (Génesis 39:21, adaptado) – Sin embargo, el Señor estaba conmigo.
2. *"He was crucified in weakness, **albeit** he lives by God's power."* (2 Corintios 13:4, adaptado) – Fue crucificado en debilidad, aunque vive por el poder de Dios.
3. *"**Whereas** the world persecutes, God protects."* (Juan 15:18-19, adaptado) – Mientras que el mundo persigue, Dios protege.
4. *"**In spite of the fact that** he was a sinner, God forgave him."* (Lucas 15:22, adaptado) – A pesar de que era un pecador, Dios le perdonó.
5. *"**Be that as it may**, I will serve the Lord."* (Josué 24:15, adaptado) – Sea como sea, serviré al Señor.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Expresar concesión y contraste):**

- ***Notwithstanding** the difficulties, I will continue to pray.* (Sin embargo, a pesar de las dificultades, continuaré orando.)
- *He was a great preacher, **albeit** a humble man.* (Era un gran predicador, aunque un hombre humilde.)
- ***Whereas** his brother doubted, he believed firmly.* (Mientras que su hermano dudaba, él creía firmemente.)
- *The church grew, **whilst** the world grew more hostile.* (La iglesia creció, mientras que el mundo se volvía más hostil.)
- ***In spite of the fact that** he suffered greatly, he never lost his faith.* (A pesar de que sufrió mucho, nunca perdió su fe.)
- ***Despite the fact that** the situation seemed hopeless, he trusted God.* (A pesar de que la situación parecía desesperada, confió en Dios.)
- *He faced persecution; **for all that**, he remained joyful.* (Enfrentó persecución; a pesar de todo, permaneció gozoso.)
- ***Be that as it may**, I have peace in my heart.* (Sea como sea, tengo paz en mi corazón.)

**Edificación:** Pablo testifica que tiene esperanza en Dios, a pesar de las acusaciones. Aprendemos a usar conectores de concesión avanzados para expresar nuestra fe en medio de las dificultades.

---

### Lección 7 – "Inasmuch as He Loved Us"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores causales y condicionales avanzados (*inasmuch as, insofar as, in that, given that, provided that, on condition that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Inasmuch as he loved us, we ought to love one another."* (Adaptado de 1 Juan 4:11)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Juan 4:7-12, ESV):** 
> *"Beloved, let us love one another, for love is from God, and whoever loves has been born of God and knows God. Anyone who does not love does not know God, because God is love. In this the love of God was made manifest among us, that God sent his only Son into the world, so that we might live through him. In this is love, not that we have loved God but that he loved us and sent his Son to be the propitiation for our sins. Beloved, if God so loved us, we also ought to love one another. No one has ever seen God; if we love one another, God abides in us and his love is perfected in us."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| beloved | amados | manifest | manifestado |
| propitiation | propiciación | abides | permanece |
| perfected | perfeccionado | | |

**Conectores causales y condicionales avanzados:**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *inasmuch as* | En cuanto / debido a que | ***Inasmuch as** he loved us, we ought to love.* |
| *insofar as* | En la medida en que | ***Insofar as** we love, we reflect God.* |
| *in that* | En que (causal) | *Love is from God, **in that** God is love.* |
| *given that* | Dado que | ***Given that** God loved us first, we should love.* |
| *provided that* | Siempre que (condición) | *He will forgive, **provided that** we repent.* |
| *on condition that* | Con la condición de que | *He will save us, **on condition that** we believe.* |
| *forasmuch as* | Por cuanto (formal) | ***Forasmuch as** he died, we live.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Inasmuch as** you did it to the least of these, you did it to me."* (Mateo 25:40) – En cuanto lo hicisteis a uno de estos más pequeños, a mí lo hicisteis.
2. *"**Insofar as** we are in Christ, we are a new creation."* (2 Corintios 5:17, adaptado) – En la medida en que estamos en Cristo, somos nueva creación.
3. *"**Given that** God is faithful, we can trust him."* (1 Corintios 10:13, adaptado) – Dado que Dios es fiel, podemos confiar en él.
4. *"He will answer, **provided that** we ask according to his will."* (1 Juan 5:14, adaptado) – Él responderá, siempre que pidamos conforme a su voluntad.
5. *"**On condition that** we confess, he will forgive."* (1 Juan 1:9, adaptado) – Con la condición de que confesemos, él perdonará.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Expresar causa y condición):**

- ***Inasmuch as** God loved us, we should love others.* (En cuanto Dios nos amó, debemos amar a otros.)
- ***Insofar as** we follow Christ, we are his disciples.* (En la medida en que seguimos a Cristo, somos sus discípulos.)
- *He is trustworthy, **in that** he has never broken a promise.* (Es digno de confianza, en que nunca ha roto una promesa.)
- ***Given that** the Bible is inspired, it is our authority.* (Dado que la Biblia es inspirada, es nuestra autoridad.)
- *I will pray for you, **provided that** you also pray for me.* (Oraré por ti, siempre que tú también ores por mí.)
- *He will forgive us, **on condition that** we forgive others.* (Él nos perdonará, con la condición de que perdonemos a otros.)
- ***Forasmuch as** Christ died for us, we should live for him.* (Por cuanto Cristo murió por nosotros, debemos vivir para él.)

**Edificación:** Juan nos llama a amar porque Dios nos amó primero. Aprendemos a usar conectores causales y condicionales avanzados para articular la lógica de la fe y la ética cristiana.

---

### Lección 8 – "He Was Seen to Enter the Temple"
**Gramática focal:** Voz pasiva con verbos de percepción (*He was seen to leave, She was heard to sing*); Voz pasiva con verbos causativos (*have/get something done*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He was seen to enter the temple."* (Adaptado de Hechos 21:26 – *"Paul went into the temple"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 21:26-30, ESV):** 
> *"Then Paul took the men, and the next day he purified himself along with them and went into the temple, giving notice when the days of purification would be fulfilled and the offering presented for each one of them. When the seven days were almost completed, the Jews from Asia, seeing him in the temple, stirred up the whole crowd and laid hands on him, crying out, 'Men of Israel, help! This is the man who is teaching everyone everywhere against the people and the law and this place. Moreover, he even brought Greeks into the temple and has defiled this holy place.' For they had previously seen Trophimus the Ephesian with him in the city, and they supposed that Paul had brought him into the temple. Then all the city was stirred up, and the people ran together. They seized Paul and dragged him out of the temple, and at once the gates were shut."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| purified | se purificó | giving notice | avisando |
| fulfilled | cumplido | offering | ofrenda |
| presented | presentada | stirred up | alborotaron |
| laid hands on | echaron mano | defiled | profanado |
| supposed | supusieron | seized | apresaron |
| dragged | arrastraron | gates | puertas |

**Voz pasiva con verbos de percepción:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Sujeto + be + visto/escuchado + to + infinitivo* | *He **was seen to enter** the temple.* |
| *Sujeto + be + visto/escuchado + -ing* | *He **was seen entering** the temple.* |
| *Sujeto + be + oído + to + infinitivo* | *She **was heard to pray**.* |
| *Sujeto + be + oído + -ing* | *She **was heard praying**.* |

**Voz pasiva con verbos causativos:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *have + objeto + pp* | *I **had** my Bible **bound**.* |
| *get + objeto + pp* | *I **got** my watch **repaired**.* |
| *have + objeto + base form* (activo) | *I **had** him **pray** with me.* |
| *get + objeto + to + infinitivo* (activo) | *I **got** him **to pray**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **was heard to say**, 'It is finished.'"* (Juan 19:30, adaptado) – Se le oyó decir: "Consumado es".
2. *"The angels **were seen to appear** to the shepherds."* (Lucas 2:13, adaptado) – Se vio a los ángeles aparecer a los pastores.
3. *"She **was seen to touch** his garment."* (Marcos 5:28, adaptado) – Se la vio tocar su manto.
4. *"They **had** the temple **rebuilt**."* (Esdras 6:14, adaptado) – Hicieron reconstruir el templo.
5. *"He **got** his disciples **to wait** in Jerusalem."* (Hechos 1:4, adaptado) – Logró que sus discípulos esperaran en Jerusalén.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **was seen to leave** the church early.* (Se le vio salir de la iglesia temprano.)
- *She **was heard to pray** in the garden.* (Se la oyó orar en el jardín.)
- *The apostles **were seen to heal** the sick.* (Se vio a los apóstoles sanar a los enfermos.)
- *I **had** my Bible **repaired**.* (Hice reparar mi Biblia.)
- *She **got** her prayer group **to meet** every week.* (Logró que su grupo de oración se reuniera cada semana.)
- *He **had** the church **renovated**.* (Hizo renovar la iglesia.)

**Edificación:** Pablo fue visto en el templo. Aprendemos a usar la voz pasiva con verbos de percepción para narrar eventos bíblicos desde una perspectiva objetiva, y con verbos causativos para expresar acciones realizadas a través de otros.

---

### Lección 9 – "He Need Not Have Worried"
**Gramática focal:** Modales de obligación y necesidad en pasado (*needn't have, didn't need to, didn't have to*); Modales de crítica (*might have, could have, would have*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He need not have worried; God was with him."* (Adaptado de Isaías 41:10 – *"Fear not, for I am with you"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Isaías 41:8-13, ESV):** 
> *"But you, Israel, my servant, Jacob, whom I have chosen, the offspring of Abraham, my friend; you whom I took from the ends of the earth, and called from its farthest corners, saying to you, 'You are my servant, I have chosen you and not cast you off'; fear not, for I am with you; be not dismayed, for I am your God; I will strengthen you, I will help you, I will uphold you with my righteous right hand. Behold, all who are incensed against you shall be put to shame and confounded; those who strive against you shall be as nothing and shall perish. You shall seek those who contend with you, but you shall not find them; those who war against you shall be as nothing at all. For I, the Lord your God, hold your right hand; it is I who say to you, 'Fear not, I am the one who helps you.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| chosen | escogido | cast off | desechar |
| fear not | no temas | dismayed | desanimado |
| strengthen | fortalecer | uphold | sostener |
| incensed | airados | ashamed | avergonzados |
| confounded | confundidos | strive | luchar |
| contend | contender | war | hacer guerra |

**Modales de obligación y necesidad en pasado:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *needn't have + pp* | No era necesario hacerlo (pero se hizo) | *He **needn't have worried**.* |
| *didn't need to + infinitivo* | No era necesario (y no se hizo) | *He **didn't need to worry**.* |
| *didn't have to + infinitivo* | No tenía que (y no se hizo) | *He **didn't have to fear**.* |

**Modales de crítica:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *might have + pp* | Podría haber (pero no) | *He **might have trusted** God.* |
| *could have + pp* | Podría haber (pero no) | *He **could have prayed** more.* |
| *would have + pp* | Habría (condición) | *He **would have been** saved.* |
| *should have + pp* | Debería haber (pero no) | *He **should have believed**.* |
| *ought to have + pp* | Debería haber (pero no) | *He **ought to have repented**.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"You **need not have** **been** afraid."* (Mateo 14:27, adaptado) – No habríais debido tener miedo.
2. *"She **didn't need to** go to the tomb; she had already seen the Lord."* (Juan 20:17-18, adaptado) – No necesitaba ir a la tumba; ya había visto al Señor.
3. *"They **might have** **believed** if they had seen the miracles."* (Juan 6:2, adaptado) – Podrían haber creído si hubieran visto los milagros.
4. *"You **could have** **prayed** for me."* (Marcos 14:37-38, adaptado) – Podrías haber orado por mí.
5. *"They **should have listened**."* (Marcos 12:24, adaptado) – Deberían haber escuchado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **needn't have worried** about the exam; God gave me peace.* (No habría debido preocuparme por el examen; Dios me dio paz.)
- *She **didn't need to** ask for help; it was given to her.* (No necesitaba pedir ayuda; se le fue dada.)
- *He **might have trusted** God more.* (Podría haber confiado más en Dios.)
- *They **could have prayed** more diligently.* (Podrían haber orado más diligentemente.)
- *We **should have believed** the prophecy.* (Deberíamos haber creído la profecía.)
- *You **ought to have repented** earlier.* (Deberías haberte arrepentido antes.)

**Edificación:** Dios dice: "No temas, porque yo estoy contigo". Aprendemos a usar modales de necesidad y crítica para reflexionar sobre la innecesaria preocupación del pueblo de Israel y la fidelidad de Dios.

---

### Lección 10 – Repaso: "He Need Not Have Feared"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de conectores de concesión, voz pasiva con percepción, modales en pasado.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando las estructuras de esta unidad.

**Ejemplo:**
1. ***Notwithstanding** the persecution, the church grew.* (Concesión)
2. ***Inasmuch as** he loved us, we love him.** (Causal)
3. ***Provided that** we repent, God forgives.** (Condicional)
4. *He **was heard to preach** in the temple.** (Voz pasiva con percepción)
5. *She **had** her Bible **translated**.** (Causativo)
6. *They **needn't have worried**; God was with them.* (Modal de necesidad)
7. *We **should have believed** the prophets.* (Modal de crítica)
8. *He **might have doubted**, but he didn't.* (Modal de crítica)
9. *They **could have helped** the poor.* (Modal de crítica)
10. *He **didn't need to** prove his faith; it was evident.* (Modal de necesidad)

---

## UNIDAD 3: DISCURSO INDIRECTO AVANZADO Y ESTILO LITERARIO
*Lecciones 11 a 15*

---

### Lección 11 – "He Is Believed to Have Written the Letter"
**Gramática focal:** Discurso indirecto con reporting verbs avanzados e infinitivos perfectivos (*claim to have, deny having, admit having, insist on having*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He is believed to have written the letter to the Hebrews."* (Tradición sobre Pablo)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hebreos 1:1-4, ESV):** 
> *"Long ago, at many times and in many ways, God spoke to our fathers by the prophets, but in these last days he has spoken to us by his Son, whom he appointed the heir of all things, through whom also he created the world. He is the radiance of the glory of God and the exact imprint of his nature, and he upholds the universe by the word of his power. After making purification for sins, he sat down at the right hand of the Majesty on high, having become as much superior to angels as the name he has inherited is more excellent than theirs."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| appointed | designado | heir | heredero |
| radiance | resplandor | glory | gloria |
| exact imprint | imagen exacta | nature | naturaleza |
| upholds | sostiene | universe | universo |
| purification | purificación | Majesty | Majestad |
| superior | superior | inherited | heredado |
| excellent | excelente | | |

**Reporting verbs con infinitivo perfectivo:**

| Verbo | Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *believe* | *believe to have + pp* | Creer que... | *He **is believed to have written** it.* |
| *claim* | *claim to have + pp* | Afirmar que... | *They **claim to have seen** him.* |
| *deny* | *deny having + pp* | Negar que... | *He **denied having seen** him.* |
| *admit* | *admit having + pp* | Admitir que... | *She **admitted having lied**.* |
| *insist* | *insist on having + pp* | Insistir en que... | *They **insisted on having** seen him.* |
| *report* | *report to have + pp* | Reportar que... | *He **is reported to have** died.* |
| *say* | *say to have + pp* | Decir que... | *He **is said to have** risen.* |

**Discurso indirecto con infinitivos perfectivos:**

| Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|
| *"I wrote the letter."* | *He **claimed to have written** the letter.* |
| *"I have seen the Lord."* | *She **claimed to have seen** the Lord.* |
| *"I did not steal."* | *He **denied having stolen**.* |
| *"I made a mistake."* | *She **admitted having made** a mistake.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **is believed to have been** the author of the Gospel."* (Lucas 1:1-4, adaptado) – Se cree que fue el autor del Evangelio.
2. *"They **claimed to have seen** the risen Lord."* (1 Corintios 15:5-8, adaptado) – Afirmaron haber visto al Señor resucitado.
3. *"She **denied having known** him."* (Mateo 26:72, adaptado) – Negó haberle conocido.
4. *"He **admitted having sinned** against God."* (1 Samuel 15:24, adaptado) – Admitió haber pecado contra Dios.
5. *"Paul **is reported to have** been shipwrecked."* (2 Corintios 11:25, adaptado) – Se reporta que Pablo naufragó.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *The apostle **is believed to have written** several letters.* (Se cree que el apóstol escribió varias cartas.)
- *She **claims to have read** the entire Bible.* (Afirma haber leído toda la Biblia.)
- *He **denied having seen** the miracle.* (Negó haber visto el milagro.)
- *They **admitted having made** a mistake.* (Admitieron haber cometido un error.)
- *The disciples **insisted on having seen** the risen Lord.* (Los discípulos insistieron en haber visto al Señor resucitado.)
- *The church **is reported to have** grown rapidly.* (Se reporta que la iglesia creció rápidamente.)

**Edificación:** La carta a los Hebreos nos habla de la superioridad de Cristo. Aprendemos a usar reporting verbs con infinitivos perfectivos para transmitir afirmaciones sobre la autoría y la veracidad de los textos bíblicos.

---

### Lección 12 – "He Suggested That They Wait"
**Gramática focal:** Discurso indirecto con subjuntivo (*suggest that, recommend that, insist that, demand that, propose that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He suggested that they wait in Jerusalem."* (Adaptado de Hechos 1:4 – *"He ordered them not to depart from Jerusalem"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 1:1-8, ESV):** 
> *"In the first book, O Theophilus, I have dealt with all that Jesus began to do and teach, until the day when he was taken up, after he had given commands through the Holy Spirit to the apostles whom he had chosen. He presented himself alive to them after his suffering by many proofs, appearing to them during forty days and speaking about the kingdom of God. And while staying with them he ordered them not to depart from Jerusalem, but to wait for the promise of the Father, which, he said, 'you heard from me; for John baptized with water, but you will be baptized with the Holy Spirit not many days from now.' So when they had come together, they asked him, 'Lord, will you at this time restore the kingdom to Israel?' He said to them, 'It is not for you to know times or seasons that the Father has fixed by his own authority. But you will receive power when the Holy Spirit has come upon you, and you will be my witnesses in Jerusalem and in all Judea and Samaria, and to the end of the earth.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| dealt | tratado | commands | mandatos |
| presented | presentó | proofs | pruebas |
| appearing | apareciendo | staying with | permaneciendo con |
| depart | salir | wait | esperar |
| promise | promesa | restore | restaurar |
| fixed | fijado | authority | autoridad |
| power | poder | witnesses | testigos |

**Verbos de sugerencia e insistencia + subjuntivo (en inglés formal):**

| Verbo | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *suggest* | *suggest that + sujeto + base form* | *He **suggested that they wait**.* |
| *recommend* | *recommend that + sujeto + base form* | *He **recommended that they pray**.* |
| *insist* | *insist that + sujeto + base form* | *He **insisted that they stay**.* |
| *demand* | *demand that + sujeto + base form* | *He **demanded that they believe**.* |
| *propose* | *propose that + sujeto + base form* | *He **proposed that they meet**.* |
| *urge* | *urge that + sujeto + base form* | *He **urged that they repent**.* |

**También se puede usar *should*:**
- *He suggested that they should wait.*

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **commanded that they go** into all the world."* (Mateo 28:19, adaptado) – Mandó que fueran por todo el mundo.
2. *"She **insisted that he stay** with them."* (Lucas 24:29, adaptado) – Insistió en que se quedara con ellos.
3. *"They **proposed that we pray** together."* (Hechos 4:23-24, adaptado) – Propusieron que oráramos juntos.
4. *"The apostle **urged that they love** one another."* (Juan 15:12, adaptado) – El apóstol instó a que se amaran unos a otros.
5. *"He **demanded that they believe** in the Son of God."* (Juan 6:29, adaptado) – Exigió que creyeran en el Hijo de Dios.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *The pastor **suggested that we pray** without ceasing.* (El pastor sugirió que oráramos sin cesar.)
- *The Bible **recommends that we love** our enemies.* (La Biblia recomienda que amemos a nuestros enemigos.)
- *Jesus **insisted that they wait** for the Holy Spirit.* (Jesús insistió en que esperaran el Espíritu Santo.)
- *The church **proposed that we help** the poor.* (La iglesia propuso que ayudáramos a los pobres.)
- *The apostle **urged that they be** reconciled.* (El apóstol instó a que se reconciliaran.)

**Edificación:** Jesús ordenó a sus discípulos que esperaran en Jerusalén. Aprendemos a usar el subjuntivo en el discurso indirecto para transmitir mandatos, sugerencias e insistencias de la Escritura.

---

### Lección 13 – "She Asked Where He Had Gone"
**Gramática focal:** Discurso indirecto con preguntas complejas y backshifting avanzado.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"She asked where he had gone."* (Adaptado de Juan 20:13 – *"Woman, why are you weeping? Whom are you seeking?"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 20:11-18, ESV):** 
> *"But Mary stood weeping outside the tomb, and as she wept she stooped to look into the tomb. And she saw two angels in white, sitting where the body of Jesus had lain, one at the head and one at the feet. They said to her, 'Woman, why are you weeping?' She said to them, 'They have taken away my Lord, and I do not know where they have laid him.' Having said this, she turned around and saw Jesus standing, but she did not know that it was Jesus. Jesus said to her, 'Woman, why are you weeping? Whom are you seeking?' Supposing him to be the gardener, she said to him, 'Sir, if you have carried him away, tell me where you have laid him, and I will take him away.' Jesus said to her, 'Mary.' She turned and said to him in Aramaic, 'Rabboni!' (which means Teacher). Jesus said to her, 'Do not cling to me, for I have not yet ascended to the Father; but go to my brothers and say to them, "I am ascending to my Father and your Father, to my God and your God."' Mary Magdalene went and announced to the disciples, 'I have seen the Lord'—and that he had said these things to her."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| weeping | llorando | stooped | se inclinó |
| angels | ángeles | head | cabecera |
| feet | pies | laid | puesto |
| gardener | jardinero | carried away | llevado |
| ascended | ascendió | cling | aferrarse |
| announced | anunció | | |

**Backshifting avanzado en preguntas:**

| Tiempo | Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|:---|
| Present Simple | *"Where do you live?"* | *He asked where I **lived**.* |
| Present Continuous | *"What are you doing?"* | *He asked what I **was doing**.* |
| Past Simple | *"What did you see?"* | *He asked what I **had seen**.* |
| Past Continuous | *"What were you doing?"* | *He asked what I **had been doing**.* |
| Present Perfect | *"Where have you been?"* | *He asked where I **had been**.* |
| Past Perfect | *"What had you done?"* | *He asked what I **had done**.* |
| Future (will) | *"What will you do?"* | *He asked what I **would do**.* |
| Future (going to) | *"What are you going to do?"* | *He asked what I **was going to do**.* |
| Modal (can) | *"What can you see?"* | *He asked what I **could see**.* |
| Modal (may) | *"What may I do?"* | *He asked what he **might do**.* |
| Modal (must) | *"What must I do?"* | *He asked what he **must do** (o **had to do**).* |

**Preguntas indirectas con *if/whether*:**

| Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|
| *"Do you believe?"* | *He asked **if** I believed.* |
| *"Are you a Christian?"* | *He asked **whether** I was a Christian.* |
| *"Have you been saved?"* | *He asked **if** I had been saved.* |
| *"Will you come?"* | *He asked **whether** I would come.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He asked, 'Who touched me?'"* → *He asked who **had touched** him.* (Marcos 5:30)
2. *"She asked, 'Where have you put him?'"* → *She asked where they **had put** him.* (Juan 20:13)
3. *"They asked, 'Are you the King of the Jews?'"* → *They asked whether he **was** the King of the Jews.* (Mateo 27:11)
4. *"Peter asked, 'Lord, how often will my brother sin against me, and I forgive him?'"* → *Peter asked how often he **should** forgive his brother.* (Mateo 18:21)
5. *"The rich young man asked, 'What must I do to inherit eternal life?'"* → *The rich young man asked what he **must do** to inherit eternal life.* (Marcos 10:17)

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *She asked **where I lived**.* (Preguntó dónde vivía.)
- *He asked **what I was doing**.* (Preguntó qué estaba haciendo.)
- *They asked **if I had read** the Bible.* (Preguntaron si había leído la Biblia.)
- *The pastor asked **whether I had been baptized**.* (El pastor preguntó si había sido bautizado.)
- *He asked **what I would do** if I were in his shoes.* (Preguntó qué haría si estuviera en su lugar.)
- *She asked **how often I prayed**.* (Preguntó con qué frecuencia oraba.)
- *He asked **why I had come** to church.* (Preguntó por qué había venido a la iglesia.)

**Edificación:** María Magdalena preguntó dónde habían puesto al Señor. Aprendemos a reportar preguntas complejas con precisión, manteniendo los matices de los tiempos verbales y los modales.

---

### Lección 14 – "She Claimed That He Would Return"
**Gramática focal:** Discurso indirecto con modales y condicionales; discurso indirecto libre (estilo literario).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"She claimed that he would return."* (Adaptado de Hechos 1:11 – *"This same Jesus, who has been taken from you into heaven, will come back in the same way you have seen him go into heaven."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 1:9-11, ESV):** 
> *"And when he had said these things, as they were looking on, he was lifted up, and a cloud took him out of their sight. And while they were gazing into heaven as he went, behold, two men stood by them in white robes, and said, 'Men of Galilee, why do you stand looking into heaven? This Jesus, who was taken up from you into heaven, will come in the same way as you saw him go into heaven.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| looking on | mirando | lifted up | levantado |
| cloud | nube | sight | vista |
| gazing | mirando fijamente | robes | túnicas |
| taken up | llevado | come back | regresará |

**Discurso indirecto con modales:**

| Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|
| *"He **will** return."* | *She claimed that he **would** return.* |
| *"He **can** save."* | *He said that he **could** save.* |
| *"He **may** come."* | *She said that he **might** come.* |
| *"He **must** go."* | *He said that he **must** go (o **had to** go).* |
| *"He **should** pray."* | *She said that he **should** pray.* |
| *"He **might have** left."* | *He said that he **might have** left.* |

**Discurso indirecto con condicionales:**

| Directo | Indirecto |
|:---|:---|
| *"If he comes, I will go."* | *He said that if he came, he would go.* |
| *"If I were you, I would pray."* | *He said that if he were me, he would pray.* |
| *"If I had known, I would have come."* | *He said that if he had known, he would have come.* |

**Estilo indirecto libre (Free Indirect Speech):**

El estilo indirecto libre es una técnica literaria donde los pensamientos de un personaje se presentan sin verbos de reporte explícitos, en tercera persona. Se utiliza en narrativa bíblica para dar acceso a los pensamientos de los personajes.

**Ejemplo bíblico (estilo indirecto libre):**
> *"The woman said to herself, 'If I only touch his garment, I will be made well.'"* (Marcos 5:28) → Se puede presentar como: *If she only touched his garment, she would be made well.*

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **claimed that he would** return.* (Afirmó que regresaría.)
- *She **said that she could** heal the sick.* (Dijo que podía sanar a los enfermos.)
- *They **announced that he might** come.* (Anunciaron que podría venir.)
- *He **insisted that he must** go.* (Insistió en que debía irse.)
- *The prophet **declared that if** the people repented, God **would** forgive them.* (El profeta declaró que si el pueblo se arrepentía, Dios los perdonaría.)
- *She **thought that if** she prayed more, she **would** find peace.* (Pensó que si oraba más, encontraría paz.)

**Edificación:** Los ángeles proclamaron que Jesús volvería de la misma manera que ascendió. Aprendemos a reportar promesas y declaraciones proféticas con precisión, manteniendo el sentido de certeza y esperanza.

---

### Lección 15 – Repaso: "He Claimed to Have Risen"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de discurso indirecto avanzado y estilo literario.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante transforma 10 oraciones directas en discurso indirecto usando diferentes estructuras.

**Ejemplo:**
1. *"I have seen the Lord!"* → *She claimed to have seen the Lord.*
2. *"Do you believe?"* → *He asked if I believed.*
3. *"Where have you been?"* → *She asked where I had been.*
4. *"Let us pray."* → *He suggested that they pray.*
5. *"He will return."* → *They declared that he would return.*
6. *"I must go."* → *He said that he must go.*
7. *"If you believe, you will be saved."* → *He said that if I believed, I would be saved.*
8. *"I did not steal."* → *He denied having stolen.*
9. *"Wait for me."* → *He urged them to wait.*
10. *"What must I do?"* → *He asked what he must do.*

---

## UNIDAD 4: NOMINALIZACIÓN Y ESTILO FORMAL ACADÉMICO
*Lecciones 16 a 20*

---

### Lección 16 – "The Salvation of the Lord Is Near"
**Gramática focal:** Nominalización (transformación de verbos y adjetivos en sustantivos).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The salvation of the Lord is near."* (Adaptado de Isaías 51:5)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Isaías 51:1-6, ESV):** 
> *"Listen to me, you who pursue righteousness, you who seek the Lord: look to the rock from which you were hewn, and to the quarry from which you were dug. Look to Abraham your father and to Sarah who bore you; for he was but one when I called him, that I might bless him and multiply him. For the Lord comforts Zion; he comforts all her waste places and makes her wilderness like Eden, her desert like the garden of the Lord; joy and gladness will be found in her, thanksgiving and the voice of song. Give attention to me, my people, and give ear to me, my nation; for a law will go out from me, and I will set my justice for a light to the peoples. My righteousness draws near, my salvation has gone out, and my arms will judge the peoples; the coastlands hope for me, and for my arm they wait. Lift up your eyes to the heavens, and look at the earth beneath; for the heavens vanish like smoke, the earth will wear out like a garment, and they who dwell in it will die in like manner; but my salvation will be forever, and my righteousness will never be dismayed."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| pursue | buscar / perseguir | righteousness | justicia |
| hewn | tallado | quarry | cantera |
| bore | dio a luz | multiply | multiplicar |
| comforts | consuela | waste places | lugares desolados |
| wilderness | desierto | gladness | alegría |
| thanksgiving | acción de gracias | attention | atención |
| justice | justicia | peoples | pueblos |
| coastlands | costas | vanish | desaparecen |
| wear out | gastar | garment | vestidura |
| dwell | habitar | dismayed | desanimado |

**Nominalización (transformación de verbos en sustantivos):**

| Verbo | Sustantivo | Ejemplo (verbo) | Ejemplo (sustantivo) |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *save* | *salvation* | *God saves us.* | *The **salvation** of the Lord is near.* |
| *believe* | *belief* | *I believe in God.* | *My **belief** in God is strong.* |
| *forgive* | *forgiveness* | *God forgives us.* | *We receive **forgiveness**.* |
| *redeem* | *redemption* | *Christ redeems us.* | *Our **redemption** is through him.* |
| *justify* | *justification* | *God justifies us.* | *We receive **justification**.* |
| *sanctify* | *sanctification* | *God sanctifies us.* | *Our **sanctification** is in Christ.* |
| *glorify* | *glory* | *We glorify God.* | *All **glory** to God.* |

**Nominalización (transformación de adjetivos en sustantivos):**

| Adjetivo | Sustantivo | Ejemplo (adjetivo) | Ejemplo (sustantivo) |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *righteous* | *righteousness* | *He is righteous.* | *His **righteousness** is perfect.* |
| *holy* | *holiness* | *God is holy.* | *His **holiness** is awesome.* |
| *faithful* | *faithfulness* | *God is faithful.* | *His **faithfulness** endures.* |
| *just* | *justice* | *God is just.* | *His **justice** prevails.* |
| *merciful* | *mercy* | *He is merciful.* | *His **mercy** is great.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con nominalización:**

1. *"The **salvation** of the righteous is from the Lord."* (Salmo 37:39) – La salvación de los justos viene del Señor.
2. *"The **forgiveness** of sins is through his blood."* (Efesios 1:7, adaptado) – El perdón de pecados es por medio de su sangre.
3. *"We await our **redemption**."* (Romanos 8:23, adaptado) – Esperamos nuestra redención.
4. *"His **faithfulness** is a shield."* (Salmo 91:4, adaptado) – Su fidelidad es un escudo.
5. *"The **justice** of God will prevail."* (Salmo 37:6, adaptado) – La justicia de Dios prevalecerá.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal académico):**

- *The **salvation** of mankind is through Christ alone.* (La salvación de la humanidad es solo por medio de Cristo.)
- *The **belief** in God gives us hope.* (La creencia en Dios nos da esperanza.)
- *The **forgiveness** of our sins is a gift of grace.* (El perdón de nuestros pecados es un don de gracia.)
- *Our **redemption** was accomplished on the cross.* (Nuestra redención fue cumplida en la cruz.)
- *The **justification** of the sinner is by faith.* (La justificación del pecador es por fe.)
- *His **holiness** is beyond our comprehension.* (Su santidad está más allá de nuestra comprensión.)
- *The **faithfulness** of God is unwavering.* (La fidelidad de Dios es inquebrantable.)
- *We appeal to the **mercy** of the Lord.* (Apelamos a la misericordia del Señor.)

**Edificación:** Isaías proclama que la salvación del Señor está cerca. Aprendemos a usar la nominalización para expresar conceptos teológicos en un estilo formal y académico, apropiado para la predicación, la enseñanza y la escritura teológica.

---

### Lección 17 – "The Belief in God Leads to Salvation"
**Gramática focal:** Nominalización con verbos causativos y de opinión (*belief leads to, knowledge of, understanding of*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The belief in God leads to salvation."* (Adaptado de Romanos 10:9-10)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 10:8-13, ESV):** 
> *"But what does it say? 'The word is near you, in your mouth and in your heart' (that is, the word of faith that we proclaim); because, if you confess with your mouth that Jesus is Lord and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead, you will be saved. For with the heart one believes and is justified, and with the mouth one confesses and is saved. For the Scripture says, 'Everyone who believes in him will not be put to shame.' For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek; for the same Lord is Lord of all, bestowing his riches on all who call on him. For 'everyone who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| proclaim | proclamar | confess | confesar |
| believes | cree | justified | justificado |
| saved | salvo | Scripture | Escritura |
| shame | vergüenza | distinction | distinción |
| bestowing | otorgando | riches | riquezas |

**Nominalización con verbos causativos:**

| Verbo | Sustantivo | Ejemplo (verbo) | Ejemplo (sustantivo) |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *believe* | *belief* | *We believe in God.* | ***Belief** in God leads to salvation.* |
| *confess* | *confession* | *We confess our sins.* | ***Confession** brings forgiveness.* |
| *obey* | *obedience* | *We obey God.* | ***Obedience** is better than sacrifice.* |
| *trust* | *trust* | *We trust in God.* | ***Trust** in God brings peace.* |

**Estructuras nominalizadas comunes:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *The + sustantivo + of + complemento + verbo* | *The **salvation** of the Lord is near.* |
| *The + sustantivo + that + cláusula* | *The **belief** that God is love is central.* |
| *His/Her/Their + sustantivo* | *His **faithfulness** endures forever.* |
| *The + sustantivo + is + complemento* | *The **knowledge** of God is eternal life.* |

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal):**

- *The **belief** in Jesus Christ leads to eternal life.* (La creencia en Jesucristo conduce a la vida eterna.)
- *The **confession** of our sins is necessary for forgiveness.* (La confesión de nuestros pecados es necesaria para el perdón.)
- *The **obedience** to God's commands brings blessing.* (La obediencia a los mandamientos de Dios trae bendición.)
- *The **knowledge** of the truth sets us free.* (El conocimiento de la verdad nos hace libres.)
- *The **understanding** of Scripture is a gift of the Spirit.* (El entendimiento de la Escritura es un don del Espíritu.)
- *The **hope** of eternal life sustains us.* (La esperanza de la vida eterna nos sostiene.)
- *The **love** of God is the greatest commandment.* (El amor de Dios es el mandamiento más grande.)

**Edificación:** Pablo declara que la fe en Dios lleva a la salvación. Aprendemos a usar la nominalización para expresar las creencias fundamentales de la fe cristiana en un lenguaje formal y teológico.

---

### Lección 18 – "The Justification of the Sinner Is by Faith"
**Gramática focal:** Nominalización de verbos teológicos clave (*salvation, redemption, justification, sanctification, glorification*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The justification of the sinner is by faith."* (Adaptado de Romanos 3:28)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 3:21-26, ESV):** 
> *"But now the righteousness of God has been manifested apart from the law, although the Law and the Prophets bear witness to it—the righteousness of God through faith in Jesus Christ for all who believe. For there is no distinction: for all have sinned and fall short of the glory of God, and are justified by his grace as a gift, through the redemption that is in Christ Jesus, whom God put forward as a propitiation by his blood, to be received by faith. This was to show God's righteousness, because in his divine forbearance he had passed over former sins. It was to show his righteousness at the present time, so that he might be just and the justifier of the one who has faith in Jesus."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| manifested | manifestado | bear witness | dan testimonio |
| distinction | distinción | sinned | pecado |
| fall short | no alcanzan | glory | gloria |
| justified | justificados | grace | gracia |
| gift | don | redemption | redención |
| propitiation | propiciación | forbearance | paciencia |
| justifier | el que justifica | | |

**Nominalización de verbos teológicos:**

| Verbo | Sustantivo | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *save* | *salvation* | salvación | *The **salvation** of the Lord is near.* |
| *redeem* | *redemption* | redención | *Our **redemption** is through his blood.* |
| *justify* | *justification* | justificación | *The **justification** of the sinner is by faith.* |
| *sanctify* | *sanctification* | santificación | *Our **sanctification** is in Christ.* |
| *glorify* | *glorification* | glorificación | *The **glorification** of the saints awaits.* |
| *believe* | *belief* | creencia | *The **belief** in God is essential.* |
| *confess* | *confession* | confesión | *The **confession** of faith is public.* |
| *obey* | *obedience* | obediencia | *Obedience is better than sacrifice.* |

**Uso de nominalizaciones en oraciones complejas:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *The + sustantivo + of + complemento + is + complemento* | *The **salvation** of the believer is through faith.* |
| *His/Her/Their + sustantivo + is + complemento* | *His **faithfulness** is a shield.* |
| *The + sustantivo + that + cláusula* | *The **faith** that saves us is a gift from God.* |

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Teología formal):**

- *The **salvation** of the believer is by grace through faith.* (La salvación del creyente es por gracia mediante la fe.)
- *The **redemption** of mankind was accomplished on the cross.* (La redención de la humanidad fue cumplida en la cruz.)
- *The **justification** of the sinner is a gift of God's grace.* (La justificación del pecador es un don de la gracia de Dios.)
- *The **sanctification** of the believer is a work of the Holy Spirit.* (La santificación del creyente es una obra del Espíritu Santo.)
- *The **glorification** of the saints will occur at the last day.* (La glorificación de los santos ocurrirá en el último día.)
- *The **knowledge** of God is eternal life.* (El conocimiento de Dios es vida eterna.)
- *The **forgiveness** of our sins is through his blood.* (El perdón de nuestros pecados es por medio de su sangre.)

**Edificación:** Pablo explica que la justificación del pecador es por fe, sin las obras de la ley. Aprendemos a usar la nominalización de términos teológicos para articular las doctrinas fundamentales de la fe cristiana con precisión y claridad.

---

### Lección 19 – "The Knowledge of God Is Eternal Life"
**Gramática focal:** Nominalización de adjetivos en sustantivos abstractos (*holiness, righteousness, faithfulness, mercy, grace*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The knowledge of God is eternal life."* (Adaptado de Juan 17:3)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 17:1-5, ESV):** 
> *"When Jesus had spoken these words, he lifted up his eyes to heaven, and said, 'Father, the hour has come; glorify your Son that the Son may glorify you, since you have given him authority over all flesh, to give eternal life to all whom you have given him. And this is eternal life, that they know you the only true God, and Jesus Christ whom you have sent. I glorified you on earth, having accomplished the work that you gave me to do. And now, Father, glorify me in your own presence with the glory that I had with you before the world existed.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| glorify | glorificar | authority | autoridad |
| flesh | carne | eternal life | vida eterna |
| accomplished | cumplido | presence | presencia |
| existed | existió | | |

**Nominalización de adjetivos en sustantivos abstractos:**

| Adjetivo | Sustantivo | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| *righteous* | *righteousness* | justicia | *The **righteousness** of God is revealed.* |
| *holy* | *holiness* | santidad | *His **holiness** is awesome.* |
| *faithful* | *faithfulness* | fidelidad | *His **faithfulness** endures.* |
| *just* | *justice* | justicia | *The **justice** of God prevails.* |
| *merciful* | *mercy* | misericordia | *His **mercy** is great.* |
| *gracious* | *grace* | gracia | *His **grace** sustains us.* |
| *good* | *goodness* | bondad | *The **goodness** of the Lord is seen.* |
| *great* | *greatness* | grandeza | *His **greatness** is unsearchable.* |

**Estructuras con adjetivos nominalizados:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *The + sustantivo + of + complemento* | *The **faithfulness** of God is eternal.* |
| *His/Her/Their + sustantivo* | *His **mercy** is new every morning.* |
| *Sustantivo + be + complemento* | *His **grace** is sufficient.* |

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *The **righteousness** of God is revealed in the gospel.* (La justicia de Dios es revelada en el evangelio.)
- *The **holiness** of God is beyond our comprehension.* (La santidad de Dios está más allá de nuestra comprensión.)
- *His **faithfulness** is a refuge for us.* (Su fidelidad es un refugio para nosotros.)
- *The **justice** of God will be done.* (La justicia de Dios se hará.)
- *His **mercy** is new every morning.* (Su misericordia es nueva cada mañana.)
- *His **grace** is sufficient for us.* (Su gracia es suficiente para nosotros.)
- *The **goodness** of the Lord leads to repentance.* (La bondad del Señor lleva al arrepentimiento.)
- *His **greatness** is beyond all praise.* (Su grandeza está más allá de toda alabanza.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos da vida eterna al conocernos a Dios. Aprendemos a usar la nominalización de adjetivos para expresar los atributos de Dios de manera formal y teológica.

---

### Lección 20 – Repaso: "The Salvation of the Lord"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de nominalización y estilo formal.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe un párrafo formal sobre la salvación usando al menos 10 nominalizaciones.

**Ejemplo:**
> *The **salvation** of the Lord is the central message of the Bible. The **knowledge** of God leads to eternal life. The **faith** of the believer is a gift of God's grace. The **justification** of the sinner is by faith, not by works. The **redemption** of mankind was accomplished through the sacrifice of Christ. His **righteousness** is imputed to us. His **faithfulness** and **mercy** endure forever. The **obedience** of Christ is our example. The **hope** of eternal life is our anchor. The **sanctification** of the Spirit is our assurance. The **glorification** of the saints is our ultimate hope.*

---

## UNIDAD 5: PARTICIPIOS Y CLAUSULAS ABSOLUTAS
*Lecciones 21 a 25*

---

### Lección 21 – "Having Loved His Own, He Loved Them to the End"
**Gramática focal:** Participios presentes y pasados en frases absolutas (estilo literario).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Having loved his own who were in the world, he loved them to the end."* — **Juan 13:1**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 13:1-5, ESV):** 
> *"Now before the Feast of the Passover, when Jesus knew that his hour had come to depart out of this world to the Father, having loved his own who were in the world, he loved them to the end. During supper, when the devil had already put it into the heart of Judas Iscariot, Simon's son, to betray him, Jesus, knowing that the Father had given all things into his hands, and that he had come from God and was going back to God, rose from supper. He laid aside his outer garments, and taking a towel, tied it around his waist. Then he poured water into a basin and began to wash the disciples' feet and to wipe them with the towel that was wrapped around him."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| Feast | Fiesta | Passover | Pascua |
| depart | partir | betray | traicionar |
| laid aside | dejó a un lado | outer garments | ropa exterior |
| towel | toalla | waist | cintura |
| basin | lebrillo | wash | lavar |
| wipe | secar | wrapped | envuelto |

**Frases de participio (Participial Phrases):**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Having + pp + (complemento)* | Acción completada antes de otra | ***Having loved** his own, he loved them to the end.* |
| *Present participle (-ing) + (complemento)* | Acción simultánea | ***Knowing** that the Father had given all things, he rose.* |
| *Past participle (pp) + (complemento)* | Acción pasiva | ***Given** authority, he acted with power.* |
| *Having been + pp + (complemento)* | Pasiva perfectiva | ***Having been sent** by the Father, he came.* |

**Frases absolutas (Absolute Phrases):**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Sustantivo + participio (+ complemento)* | Descripción independiente | *His **heart filled** with love, he served them.* |
| *Sustantivo + adjetivo (+ complemento)* | Descripción de estado | *His **face shining** with glory, he prayed.* |
| *Sustantivo + preposición + complemento* | Descripción de ubicación | *His **hands on the table**, he taught.* |
| *With + sustantivo + participio* | Construcción con *with* | ***With** his **feet washed**, he was clean.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos con participios:**

1. *"**Being filled** with the Holy Spirit, they spoke boldly."* (Hechos 4:31) – Estando llenos del Espíritu Santo, hablaron con valentía.
2. *"**Having been** justified by faith, we have peace with God."* (Romanos 5:1) – Habiendo sido justificados por la fe, tenemos paz con Dios.
3. *"**Seeing** the crowds, he had compassion on them."* (Mateo 9:36) – Viendo a las multitudes, tuvo compasión de ellas.
4. *"**Taking** the child, he set him in the midst of them."* (Marcos 9:36) – Tomando al niño, lo puso en medio de ellos.
5. *"**He has delivered us** from the domain of darkness."* (Colosenses 1:13, adaptado) – Habiéndonos librado del dominio de las tinieblas.

**Frases absolutas en la Biblia:**

1. *"His **heart burning** within him, he explained the Scriptures."* (Lucas 24:32, adaptado) – Ardiendo su corazón dentro de él, explicó las Escrituras.
2. *"His **eyes opened**, he saw the Lord."* (Juan 9:11, adaptado) – Abiertos sus ojos, vio al Señor.
3. *"His **hands filled** with authority, he healed the sick."* (Marcos 1:31, adaptado) – Llenas sus manos de autoridad, sanó a los enfermos.
4. *"With **his face shining** like the sun, he was transfigured."* (Mateo 17:2) – Con su rostro resplandeciendo como el sol, fue transfigurado.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo literario):**

- ***Having prayed** all night, Jesus had the strength to face the cross.* (Habiendo orado toda la noche, Jesús tuvo la fuerza para enfrentar la cruz.)
- ***Knowing** that God is faithful, we can trust him in all circumstances.* (Sabiendo que Dios es fiel, podemos confiar en él en todas las circunstancias.)
- ***Being filled** with the Spirit, the disciples preached with power.* (Estando llenos del Espíritu, los discípulos predicaron con poder.)
- ***Having been** forgiven, we should forgive others.* (Habiendo sido perdonados, debemos perdonar a otros.)
- ***Seeking** first the kingdom of God, we will find everything we need.* (Buscando primeramente el reino de Dios, encontraremos todo lo que necesitamos.)
- *His **heart filled** with compassion, he reached out to the sick.* (Su corazón lleno de compasión, extendió la mano a los enfermos.)
- *With **his faith unshaken**, he stood firm.* (Con su fe inquebrantable, se mantuvo firme.)

**Edificación:** Jesús, habiendo amado a los suyos, los amó hasta el fin. Aprendemos a usar participios y frases absolutas para crear un estilo literario rico y narrativo, como el que encontramos en el Evangelio de Juan.

---

### Lección 22 – "He Who Believed Was Saved" (Uso de *he who* y *the one who*)
**Gramática focal:** Construcciones con *he who*, *the one who*, *those who*, *whoever*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He who believed was saved."* (Adaptado de Juan 3:16)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 3:16-21, ESV):** 
> *"For God so loved the world, that he gave his only Son, that whoever believes in him should not perish but have eternal life. For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world, but in order that the world might be saved through him. Whoever believes in him is not condemned, but whoever does not believe is condemned already, because he has not believed in the name of the only Son of God. And this is the judgment: the light has come into the world, and people loved the darkness rather than the light because their works were evil. For everyone who does wicked things hates the light and does not come to the light, lest his works should be exposed. But whoever does what is true comes to the light, so that it may be clearly seen that his works have been carried out in God."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| perish | perecer | condemn | condenar |
| judgment | juicio | darkness | oscuridad |
| wicked | malvados | exposed | expuestos |

**Construcciones con *he who*, *the one who*, *those who*, *whoever*:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *He who + verbo* | La persona que (sujeto) | ***He who believed** was saved.* |
| *The one who + verbo* | La persona que | ***The one who believes** will be saved.* |
| *Those who + verbo* | Aquellos que | ***Those who love** God obey his commands.* |
| *Whoever + verbo* | Cualquiera que | ***Whoever believes** will not perish.* |
| *The + adjetivo + verbo* | Los que son... | ***The righteous** will live by faith.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**He who** has ears to hear, let him hear."* (Mateo 11:15) – El que tiene oídos para oír, oiga.
2. *"**Whoever** believes in him will not perish."* (Juan 3:16) – Todo aquel que cree en él, no perecerá.
3. *"**The one who** does not love does not know God."* (1 Juan 4:8) – El que no ama, no conoce a Dios.
4. *"**Those who** worship him must worship in spirit and truth."* (Juan 4:24) – Los que le adoran, en espíritu y en verdad es necesario que adoren.
5. *"**The righteous** shall live by faith."* (Romanos 1:17) – El justo vivirá por la fe.
6. *"**All who** believe are justified."* (Hechos 13:39, adaptado) – Todos los que creen son justificados.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***He who** trusts in the Lord will be saved.* (El que confía en el Señor será salvo.)
- ***The one who** prays without ceasing will find peace.* (El que ora sin cesar encontrará paz.)
- ***Those who** love God will obey his commands.* (Aquellos que aman a Dios obedecerán sus mandamientos.)
- ***Whoever** seeks him will find him.* (Cualquiera que lo busque, lo encontrará.)
- ***The faithful** will be rewarded.* (Los fieles serán recompensados.)
- ***All who** call on the name of the Lord will be saved.* (Todos los que invoquen el nombre del Señor serán salvos.)

**Edificación:** Jesús declara que todo aquel que cree en él no perecerá. Aprendemos a usar las construcciones con *he who*, *the one who*, *those who* y *whoever* para referirnos a los que creen y los que no, en un estilo formal y teológico.

---

### Lección 23 – "His Faith, Being Tested, Proved Genuine"
**Gramática focal:** Construcciones de participio como adjetivos; participios que modifican sustantivos.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"His faith, being tested, proved genuine."* (Adaptado de 1 Pedro 1:7)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Pedro 1:3-9, ESV):** 
> *"Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ! According to his great mercy, he has caused us to be born again to a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead, to an inheritance that is imperishable, undefiled, and unfading, kept in heaven for you, who by God's power are being guarded through faith for a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time.
