In this you rejoice, though now for a little while, if necessary, you have been grieved by various trials, so that the tested genuineness of your faith—more precious than gold that perishes though it is tested by fire—may be found to result in praise and glory and honor at the revelation of Jesus Christ. Though you have not seen him, you love him. Though you do not now see him, you believe in him and rejoice with joy that is inexpressible and filled with glory, obtaining the outcome of your faith, the salvation of your souls."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| blessed | bendito | inheritance | herencia |
| imperishable | imperecedero | undefiled | incontaminado |
| unfading | inmarchitable | guarded | guardados |
| grieved | afligidos | trials | pruebas |
| genuineness | autenticidad | precious | precioso |
| perishes | perece | inexpressible | inexpresable |
| outcome | resultado | | |

**Participios como adjetivos:**

| Participio | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *-ing* (presente activo) | Descripción activa | *The **running** water is refreshing.* |
| *-ed* (pasado pasivo) | Descripción pasiva | *The **tested** faith proved genuine.* |
| *-ing* (causativo) | Causa un efecto | *The **frightening** sight was overwhelming.* |
| *-ed* (estado) | Estado resultante | *He was **surrounded** by his disciples.* |

**Participios en frases absolutas (profundización):**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Sustantivo + participio + complemento* | *His **faith**, being tested, proved genuine.* |
| *Participio + complemento, sujeto + verbo* | ***Tested** by fire, his faith proved genuine.* |
| *Sujeto + verbo, participio + complemento* | *He prayed, **kneeling** on the ground.* |
| *With + sujeto + participio + complemento* | ***With** his **heart burning**, he spoke.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Blessed** is the one who reads aloud the words of this prophecy."* (Apocalipsis 1:3) – Bienaventurado el que lee...
2. *"The **crucified** Jesus is the Messiah."* (1 Corintios 1:23, adaptado) – El Jesús crucificado es el Mesías.
3. *"**Surrounded** by so great a cloud of witnesses, let us run with endurance."* (Hebreos 12:1) – Rodeados por tan grande nube de testigos...
4. *"The **living** God is greater than the dead idols."* (Hechos 14:15, adaptado) – El Dios vivo es mayor que los ídolos muertos.
5. *"His **heart burning** within him, he explained the Scriptures."* (Lucas 24:32) – Su corazón ardiendo dentro de él...

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo literario):**

- *His **faith**, being tested, proved genuine.* (Su fe, siendo probada, resultó genuina.)
- ***Tested** by trials, his character was refined.* (Probado por las pruebas, su carácter fue refinado.)
- *The **living** water satisfies the thirsty soul.* (El agua viva satisface el alma sedienta.)
- ***Crucified** for our sins, he was raised for our justification.* (Crucificado por nuestros pecados, fue resucitado para nuestra justificación.)
- *His **heart filled** with compassion, he healed the sick.* (Su corazón lleno de compasión, sanó a los enfermos.)
- *The **grieving** disciples were comforted by the Spirit.* (Los discípulos afligidos fueron consolados por el Espíritu.)
- *With **his faith unshaken**, he faced the lions.* (Con su fe inquebrantable, enfrentó a los leones.)

**Edificación:** La fe probada resulta genuina. Aprendemos a usar participios como adjetivos y en frases absolutas para describir la condición espiritual de los creyentes y los atributos de Dios.

---

### Lección 24 – "The Apostle, Having Been Sent, Preached Boldly"
**Gramática focal:** Participios perfectivos (*having + pp*) y pasivos perfectivos (*having been + pp*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The apostle, having been sent, preached boldly."* (Adaptado de Hechos 13:1-4)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hechos 13:1-4, ESV):** 
> *"Now there were in the church at Antioch prophets and teachers, Barnabas, Simeon who was called Niger, Lucius of Cyrene, Manaen a lifelong friend of Herod the tetrarch, and Saul. While they were worshiping the Lord and fasting, the Holy Spirit said, 'Set apart for me Barnabas and Saul for the work to which I have called them.' Then after fasting and praying they laid their hands on them and sent them off. So, being sent out by the Holy Spirit, they went down to Seleucia, and from there they sailed to Cyprus."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| prophets | profetas | teachers | maestros |
| lifelong | de toda la vida | tetrarch | tetrarca |
| set apart | apartar | laid their hands | impusieron las manos |
| sent out | enviados | sailed | navegaron |

**Participios perfectivos:**

| Estructura | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Having + pp* | Acción completada antes de otra | ***Having prayed**, he went to the disciples.* |
| *Having been + pp* | Pasiva completada antes de otra | ***Having been sent**, they preached.* |
| *Not having + pp* | Negativa perfectiva | ***Not having seen** him, they doubted.* |
| *Not having been + pp* | Negativa pasiva perfectiva | ***Not having been taught**, they were confused.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Having been** filled with the Spirit, they spoke boldly."* (Hechos 2:4) – Habiendo sido llenos del Espíritu, hablaron con valentía.
2. *"**Having** seen the empty tomb, the disciples believed."* (Juan 20:8, adaptado) – Habiendo visto la tumba vacía, los discípulos creyeron.
3. *"**Having been** forgiven, we forgive others."* (Colosenses 3:13, adaptado) – Habiendo sido perdonados, perdonamos a otros.
4. *"**Not having** heard the gospel, they were lost."* (Romanos 10:14, adaptado) – No habiendo oído el evangelio, estaban perdidos.
5. *"**Having been** justified by faith, we have peace."* (Romanos 5:1) – Habiendo sido justificados por la fe, tenemos paz.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***Having prayed** all night, Jesus had strength for the day.* (Habiendo orado toda la noche, Jesús tuvo fuerza para el día.)
- ***Having been** called by God, he left everything to follow Christ.* (Habiendo sido llamado por Dios, dejó todo para seguir a Cristo.)
- ***Having seen** the miracle, the people believed.* (Habiendo visto el milagro, la gente creyó.)
- ***Having been** healed, she gave thanks to God.* (Habiendo sido sanada, dio gracias a Dios.)
- ***Not having** repented, they faced judgment.* (No habiéndose arrepentido, enfrentaron el juicio.)
- ***Having been** taught by the Spirit, they understood the truth.* (Habiendo sido enseñados por el Espíritu, entendieron la verdad.)

**Edificación:** Los apóstoles, habiendo sido enviados por el Espíritu Santo, predicaron con valentía. Aprendemos a usar participios perfectivos para expresar que la acción ha sido completada antes de la acción principal.

---

### Lección 25 – Repaso: "Having Been Saved, We Live for Him"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de participios, frases absolutas y construcciones participiales.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes estructuras participiales.

**Ejemplo:**
1. ***Having loved** his own, he loved them to the end.** (Perfectivo)
2. ***Being filled** with the Spirit, they spoke boldly.** (Pasivo presente)
3. ***Having been** justified, we have peace.** (Pasivo perfectivo)
4. ***Seeing** the crowds, he had compassion.** (Presente activo)
5. ***Tested** by fire, his faith proved genuine.** (Pasivo adjetivo)
6. *His **heart burning** within him, he explained the Scriptures.** (Absoluta)
7. ***Having prayed**, he went to his disciples.** (Perfectivo)
8. ***Being led** by the Spirit, he went to the wilderness.** (Pasivo)
9. ***Not having known** the truth, they were lost.** (Negativa perfectiva)
10. ***Having been** sent by God, he preached the gospel.** (Pasivo perfectivo)

---

## UNIDAD 6: MODALES DE DEDUCCIÓN Y OBLIGACIÓN AVANZADOS
*Lecciones 26 a 30*

---

### Lección 26 – "He Must Have Been the Messiah"
**Gramática focal:** Modales de deducción en pasado (profundización) – *must have been, might have been, could have been, can't have been*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He must have been the Messiah."* (Adaptado de Juan 4:29 – *"Could this be the Messiah?"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 4:28-30, 39-42, ESV):** 
> *"So the woman left her water jar and went away into town and said to the people, 'Come, see a man who told me all that I ever did. Can this be the Christ?' They went out of the town and were coming to him. Many Samaritans from that town believed in him because of the woman's testimony, 'He told me all that I ever did.' So when the Samaritans came to him, they asked him to stay with them, and he stayed there two days. And many more believed because of his word. They said to the woman, 'It is no longer because of what you said that we believe, for we have heard for ourselves, and we know that this is indeed the Savior of the world.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| water jar | cántaro | testimony | testimonio |
| Samaritans | samaritanos | believed | creyeron |
| stay | quedarse | indeed | ciertamente |
| Savior | Salvador | | |

**Modales de deducción en pasado (profundización):**

| Modal | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *must have + pp* | Certeza (95%) | *He **must have been** the Messiah.* |
| *might have + pp* | Posibilidad (40-60%) | *He **might have been** a prophet.* |
| *may have + pp* | Posibilidad (50%) | *He **may have known** the truth.* |
| *could have + pp* | Posibilidad/Capacidad (70%) | *He **could have saved** himself.* |
| *would have + pp* | Condición hipotética | *He **would have been** killed.* |
| *should have + pp* | Obligación no cumplida | *He **should have believed**.* |
| *can't have + pp* | Certeza negativa (95%) | *He **can't have been** the one.* |
| *couldn't have + pp* | Certeza negativa (95%) | *He **couldn't have known**.* |

**Modales con grados de certeza:**

| Grado | Modal | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **100%** | *He definitely* | *He definitely was the Messiah.* |
| **95%** | *He must have been* | *He **must have been** the Messiah.* |
| **70%** | *He could have been* | *He **could have been** the Messiah.* |
| **50%** | *He may have been* | *He **may have been** the Messiah.* |
| **40%** | *He might have been* | *He **might have been** the Messiah.* |
| **5%** | *He can't have been* | *He **can't have been** the Messiah.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He **must have seen** a miracle."* (Juan 9:33, adaptado) – Debe haber visto un milagro.
2. *"They **might have heard** the prophecy."* (Lucas 24:25-27, adaptado) – Puede que hayan oído la profecía.
3. *"She **could have been** Mary Magdalene."* (Juan 20:16, adaptado) – Podría haber sido María Magdalena.
4. *"He **can't have known** the plan."* (Juan 13:18, adaptado) – No puede haber conocido el plan.
5. *"They **must have believed** in him."* (Juan 2:23, adaptado) – Deben haber creído en él.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **must have been** a man of great faith.* (Debe haber sido un hombre de gran fe.)
- *She **might have prayed** for us.* (Puede que haya orado por nosotros.)
- *They **could have been** the disciples.* (Podrían haber sido los discípulos.)
- *He **can't have done** such a thing.* (No puede haber hecho tal cosa.)
- *We **should have believed** the prophecy.* (Deberíamos haber creído la profecía.)
- *They **must have known** the truth.* (Deben haber sabido la verdad.)

**Edificación:** La mujer samaritana preguntó: "¿Será este el Mesías?". Aprendemos a usar modales de deducción en pasado para expresar los diferentes grados de certeza con los que la gente respondió a la obra de Jesús.

---

### Lección 27 – "Had It Not Been for God's Grace"
**Gramática focal:** Modales de deducción en pasado con *had it not been for, but for, without*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Had it not been for God's grace, we would have been lost."* (Adaptado de Lamentaciones 3:22 – *"The steadfast love of the Lord never ceases; his mercies never come to an end"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Lamentaciones 3:22-26, ESV):** 
> *"The steadfast love of the Lord never ceases; his mercies never come to an end; they are new every morning; great is your faithfulness. 'The Lord is my portion,' says my soul, 'therefore I will hope in him.' The Lord is good to those who wait for him, to the soul who seeks him. It is good that one should wait quietly for the salvation of the Lord."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| steadfast | firme / constante | ceases | cesa |
| mercies | misericordias | portion | porción |
| wait | esperar | seeks | busca |
| quietly | en silencio | | |

**Estructuras condicionales de deducción:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Had it not been for + sustantivo* | Si no hubiera sido por... | ***Had it not been for** God's grace, we would have been lost.* |
| *But for + sustantivo* | Si no fuera por... | ***But for** his mercy, we would have perished.* |
| *Without + sustantivo* | Sin... | ***Without** God's love, we would have no hope.* |
| *If it had not been for + sustantivo* | Si no hubiera sido por... | ***If it had not been for** the Lord, we would have failed.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Had it not been for** the Lord, we would have been consumed."* (Salmo 124:1-3, adaptado) – Si no hubiera sido por el Señor, habríamos sido consumidos.
2. *"**But for** his grace, we would still be in our sins."* (Efesios 2:8, adaptado) – Si no fuera por su gracia, aún estaríamos en nuestros pecados.
3. *"**Without** the Spirit, we can do nothing."* (Juan 15:5, adaptado) – Sin el Espíritu, nada podemos hacer.
4. *"**If it had not been for** the prophets, they would not have known."* (Romanos 10:14, adaptado) – Si no hubiera sido por los profetas, no habrían conocido.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- ***Had it not been for** my faith, I would have given up.* (Si no hubiera sido por mi fe, me habría rendido.)
- ***But for** his prayers, I would not have found peace.* (Si no fuera por sus oraciones, no habría encontrado paz.)
- ***Without** the Bible, we would not know the truth.* (Sin la Biblia, no conoceríamos la verdad.)
- ***Had it not been for** the church, I would have been lost.* (Si no hubiera sido por la iglesia, me habría perdido.)
- ***But for** God's mercy, we would be condemned.* (Si no fuera por la misericordia de Dios, estaríamos condenados.)
- ***Without** Christ, we have no hope.* (Sin Cristo, no tenemos esperanza.)

**Edificación:** El profeta declara que la misericordia del Señor nunca se acaba. Aprendemos a usar estructuras de deducción condicional para expresar nuestra dependencia de la gracia de Dios.

---

### Lección 28 – "He Must Have Known the Truth"
**Gramática focal:** Modales de deducción en presente y pasado con *must, might, could, can't*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He must have known the truth."* (Adaptado de Juan 8:32 – *"You will know the truth, and the truth will set you free."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 8:31-36, ESV):** 
> *"So Jesus said to the Jews who had believed him, 'If you abide in my word, you are truly my disciples, and you will know the truth, and the truth will set you free.' They answered him, 'We are offspring of Abraham and have never been enslaved to anyone. How is it that you say, "You will become free"?' Jesus answered them, 'Truly, truly, I say to you, everyone who practices sin is a slave to sin. The slave does not remain in the house forever; the son remains forever. So if the Son sets you free, you will be free indeed.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| abide | permanecer | offspring | descendencia |
| enslaved | esclavizado | practices | practica |
| slave | esclavo | remain | permanecer |
| indeed | ciertamente | | |

**Modales de deducción en presente y pasado:**

| Tiempo | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Presente** | *He must know* | *He **must know** the truth.* |
| **Presente** | *He might know* | *He **might know** the truth.* |
| **Presente** | *He could know* | *He **could know** the truth.* |
| **Presente** | *He can't know* | *He **can't know** the truth.* |
| **Pasado** | *He must have known* | *He **must have known** the truth.* |
| **Pasado** | *He might have known* | *He **might have known** the truth.* |
| **Pasado** | *He could have known* | *He **could have known** the truth.* |
| **Pasado** | *He can't have known* | *He **can't have known** the truth.* |

**Uso con verbos de estado:**

| Verbo de estado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *believe* | *He **must believe** in God.* |
| *know* | *She **might know** the answer.* |
| *understand* | *They **can't understand** the Scriptures.* |
| *love* | *He **must love** his enemies.* |
| *trust* | *We **must trust** in God.* |

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *He **must know** the truth; he has read the Bible many times.* (Debe saber la verdad; ha leído la Biblia muchas veces.)
- *She **might understand** the prophecy.* (Puede que entienda la profecía.)
- *They **can't believe** in God without faith.* (No pueden creer en Dios sin fe.)
- *He **must have believed** in Jesus.* (Debe haber creído en Jesús.)
- *She **might have heard** the gospel.* (Puede que haya oído el evangelio.)
- *They **could have known** the truth.* (Podrían haber conocido la verdad.)

**Edificación:** Jesús nos dice que la verdad nos hace libres. Aprendemos a usar modales de deducción para expresar cómo las personas responden a la verdad y cómo nosotros mismos conocemos la verdad.

---

### Lección 29 – "He Needn't Have Done That"
**Gramática focal:** Modales de necesidad y obligación en pasado con *needn't have, didn't need to, didn't have to*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"He needn't have done that."* (Adaptado de Mateo 26:8-9 – *"Why this waste?"*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Mateo 26:6-13, ESV):** 
> *"Now when Jesus was at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper, a woman came up to him with an alabaster flask of very expensive ointment, and she poured it on his head as he reclined at table. And when the disciples saw it, they were indignant, saying, 'Why this waste? For this could have been sold for a large sum and given to the poor.' But Jesus, aware of this, said to them, 'Why do you trouble the woman? For she has done a beautiful thing to me. For you always have the poor with you, but you will not always have me. In pouring this ointment on my body, she has done it to prepare me for burial. Truly, I say to you, wherever this gospel is proclaimed in the whole world, what she has done will also be told in memory of her.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| leper | leproso | alabaster | alabastro |
| flask | frasco | expensive | caro |
| ointment | ungüento | poured | derramó |
| reclined | recostado | indignant | indignados |
| waste | desperdicio | sold | vendido |
| aware | consciente | trouble | molestar |
| prepare | preparar | burial | sepultura |
| memory | memoria | | |

**Modales de necesidad en pasado:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *needn't have + pp* | No era necesario (pero se hizo) | *He **needn't have done** that.* |
| *didn't need to + infinitivo* | No era necesario (y no se hizo) | *He **didn't need to** worry.* |
| *didn't have to + infinitivo* | No tenía que (y no se hizo) | *He **didn't have to** go.* |

**Modales de obligación en pasado:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *should have + pp* | Debería haber (pero no se hizo) | *He **should have** given to the poor.* |
| *ought to have + pp* | Debería haber (pero no se hizo) | *He **ought to have** helped.* |
| *could have + pp* | Podría haber (pero no se hizo) | *He **could have** done more.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"She **needn't have** **worried**; God was with her."* (Isaías 41:10, adaptado) – No habría debido preocuparse; Dios estaba con ella.
2. *"They **didn't need to** **build** the tower; God gave them the land."* (Génesis 11:4, adaptado) – No necesitaban construir la torre; Dios les dio la tierra.
3. *"He **should have** **repented**."* (Lucas 13:3, adaptado) – Debería haberse arrepentido.
4. *"They **could have** **believed**."* (Juan 12:37, adaptado) – Podrían haber creído.

**Aplicación Cotidiana:**

- *I **needn't have worried** about the exam; God gave me peace.* (No habría debido preocuparme por el examen; Dios me dio paz.)
- *She **didn't need to** prove herself; her faith was evident.* (No necesitaba demostrarse a sí misma; su fe era evidente.)
- *We **didn't have to** go through all that trouble.* (No teníamos que pasar por todo ese problema.)
- *He **should have listened** to the prophets.* (Debería haber escuchado a los profetas.)
- *They **ought to have** helped the poor.* (Deberían haber ayudado a los pobres.)
- *You **could have prayed** instead of worrying.* (Podrías haber orado en lugar de preocuparte.)

**Edificación:** Jesús defendió la acción de la mujer que derramó ungüento sobre él. Aprendemos a usar modales de necesidad y obligación en pasado para reflexionar sobre lo que es realmente necesario en nuestra vida espiritual.

---

### Lección 30 – Repaso: "He Must Have Believed"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de modales de deducción y necesidad.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 10 oraciones usando diferentes modales en pasado.

**Ejemplo:**
1. *He **must have been** a prophet.** (Certeza)
2. *She **might have known** the truth.** (Posibilidad)
3. *They **could have believed**.** (Capacidad)
4. *He **can't have done** that.** (Certeza negativa)
5. *We **should have prayed** more.** (Obligación no cumplida)
6. *They **ought to have repented**.** (Obligación no cumplida)
7. *I **needn't have worried**.** (Necesidad innecesaria)
8. *She **didn't need to ask**.** (Necesidad no utilizada)
9. *He **could have been** the Messiah.** (Posibilidad)
10. *They **must have seen** the miracles.** (Certeza)

---

## UNIDAD 7: CONECTORES AVANZADOS Y ESTILO RETÓRICO
*Lecciones 31 a 35*

---

### Lección 31 – "Notwithstanding, He Trusted in God"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de concesión y contraste avanzados (*notwithstanding, albeit, nevertheless, nonetheless, whereas, whilst, for all that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Notwithstanding, he trusted in God."* (Adaptado de Job 13:15 – *"Though he slay me, I will hope in him."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Job 13:13-16, ESV):** 
> *"Let me have silence, and I will speak, and let come on me what may. Why should I take my flesh in my teeth and put my life in my hand? Though he slay me, I will hope in him; yet I will argue my ways to his face. This will be my salvation, that the godless shall not come before him."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| silence | silencio | slay | matar |
| argue | discutir / argumentar | salvation | salvación |
| godless | impíos | | |

**Conectores de concesión avanzados (profundización):**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *notwithstanding* | Sin embargo (formal) | ***Notwithstanding**, he trusted in God.* |
| *albeit* | Aunque (+ adjetivo/frase) | *He was weak, **albeit** determined.* |
| *nevertheless* | Sin embargo | *He suffered; **nevertheless**, he hoped.* |
| *nonetheless* | No obstante | *He was persecuted; **nonetheless**, he trusted.* |
| *whereas* | Mientras que (contraste) | *He suffered, **whereas** others prospered.* |
| *whilst* | Mientras que (formal) | *He prayed, **whilst** others slept.* |
| *for all that* | A pesar de todo | *He lost everything; **for all that**, he trusted.* |
| *be that as it may* | Sea como sea | ***Be that as it may**, I will believe.* |
| *even supposing* | Aun suponiendo que | ***Even supposing** he was wrong, he was forgiven.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Notwithstanding**, God was with Joseph."* (Génesis 39:21, adaptado) – Sin embargo, Dios estaba con José.
2. *"**Nevertheless**, I am not ashamed of the gospel."* (Romanos 1:16) – Sin embargo, no me avergüenzo del evangelio.
3. *"**Whereas** the world hated them, God loved them."* (Juan 15:18-19, adaptado) – Mientras que el mundo los odiaba, Dios los amaba.
4. *"**For all that**, he did not lose his faith."* (Job 1:22, adaptado) – A pesar de todo, no perdió su fe.
5. *"**Be that as it may**, I will serve the Lord."* (Josué 24:15, adaptado) – Sea como sea, serviré al Señor.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo retórico):**

- ***Notwithstanding** the challenges, I will continue to follow Christ.* (Sin embargo, a pesar de los desafíos, continuaré siguiendo a Cristo.)
- *He was a humble leader, **albeit** a powerful preacher.* (Era un líder humilde, aunque un predicador poderoso.)
- ***Nevertheless**, we have hope in God.* (Sin embargo, tenemos esperanza en Dios.)
- ***Whereas** the world seeks power, Christians seek humility.* (Mientras que el mundo busca poder, los cristianos buscan humildad.)
- ***For all that** he suffered, he never doubted God's goodness.* (A pesar de todo lo que sufrió, nunca dudó de la bondad de Dios.)
- ***Be that as it may**, I will trust in the Lord.* (Sea como sea, confiaré en el Señor.)
- ***Even supposing** that all seems lost, God is with us.* (Aun suponiendo que todo parezca perdido, Dios está con nosotros.)

**Edificación:** Job declaró: "Aunque me mate, en él esperaré". Aprendemos a usar conectores de concesión para expresar la fe inquebrantable en medio de la adversidad.

---

### Lección 32 – "Inasmuch as He Suffered, He Learned Obedience"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores causales y condicionales avanzados (*inasmuch as, insofar as, in that, given that, provided that, on condition that, forasmuch as*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Inasmuch as he suffered, he learned obedience."* (Adaptado de Hebreos 5:8)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Hebreos 5:1-10, ESV):** 
> *"For every high priest chosen from among men is appointed to act on behalf of men in relation to God, to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins. He can deal gently with the ignorant and wayward, since he himself is beset with weakness. Because of this he is obligated to offer sacrifice for his own sins just as he does for those of the people. And no one takes this honor for himself, but only when called by God, just as Aaron was. So also Christ did not exalt himself to be made a high priest, but was appointed by him who said to him, 'You are my Son, today I have begotten you'; as he says also in another place, 'You are a priest forever, after the order of Melchizedek.' In the days of his flesh, Jesus offered up prayers and supplications, with loud cries and tears, to him who was able to save him from death, and he was heard because of his reverence. Although he was a son, he learned obedience through what he suffered. And being made perfect, he became the source of eternal salvation to all who obey him, being designated by God a high priest after the order of Melchizedek."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| high priest | sumo sacerdote | appointed | designado |
| on behalf of | en nombre de | gifts | ofrendas |
| sacrifices | sacrificios | gentle | bondadoso |
| ignorant | ignorante | wayward | extraviado |
| beset | asediado | weakness | debilidad |
| obligated | obligado | exalt | exaltarse |
| begotten | engendrado | Melchizedek | Melquisedec |
| supplications | súplicas | loud cries | fuertes clamores |
| reverence | reverencia | source | fuente |
| designated | designado | | |

**Conectores causales y condicionales avanzados (profundización):**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *inasmuch as* | En cuanto / debido a que | ***Inasmuch as** he suffered, he learned obedience.* |
| *insofar as* | En la medida en que | ***Insofar as** we love, we reflect God.* |
| *in that* | En que (causal) | *He suffered, **in that** he was human.* |
| *given that* | Dado que | ***Given that** God is faithful, we can trust him.* |
| *provided that* | Siempre que (condición) | *He will hear, **provided that** we ask.* |
| *on condition that* | Con la condición de que | *He will forgive, **on condition that** we repent.* |
| *forasmuch as* | Por cuanto (formal) | ***Forasmuch as** he died, we live.* |
| *seeing that* | Visto que | ***Seeing that** God loved us, we should love.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Inasmuch as** you did it to the least of these, you did it to me."* (Mateo 25:40) – En cuanto lo hicisteis a uno de estos más pequeños, a mí lo hicisteis.
2. *"**Insofar as** we are in Christ, we are a new creation."* (2 Corintios 5:17) – En la medida en que estamos en Cristo, somos nueva creación.
3. *"**Given that** God is faithful, he will not let us be tempted beyond our ability."* (1 Corintios 10:13) – Dado que Dios es fiel, no nos dejará ser tentados más allá de nuestra capacidad.
4. *"**Forasmuch as** Christ suffered for us, we should follow his example."* (1 Pedro 2:21, adaptado) – Por cuanto Cristo sufrió por nosotros, debemos seguir su ejemplo.
5. *"**Seeing that** we have a great high priest, let us draw near with confidence."* (Hebreos 4:14-16, adaptado) – Visto que tenemos un gran sumo sacerdote, acerquémonos con confianza.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal):**

- ***Inasmuch as** Christ suffered for us, we should be willing to suffer for him.* (En cuanto Cristo sufrió por nosotros, debemos estar dispuestos a sufrir por él.)
- ***Insofar as** we are guided by the Spirit, we are children of God.* (En la medida en que somos guiados por el Espíritu, somos hijos de Dios.)
- ***Given that** the Bible is inspired, it is our ultimate authority.* (Dado que la Biblia es inspirada, es nuestra autoridad suprema.)
- *He will answer our prayers, **provided that** we ask according to his will.* (Él responderá nuestras oraciones, siempre que pidamos conforme a su voluntad.)
- ***Forasmuch as** the Lord is faithful, we can trust him completely.* (Por cuanto el Señor es fiel, podemos confiar en él completamente.)
- ***Seeing that** we have been justified by faith, we have peace with God.* (Visto que hemos sido justificados por la fe, tenemos paz con Dios.)

**Edificación:** Cristo aprendió obediencia por lo que sufrió. Aprendemos a usar conectores causales y condicionales avanzados para articular la teología del sufrimiento y la obediencia.

---

### Lección 33 – "Consequently, We Have Peace with God"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de consecuencia y resultado avanzados (*consequently, as a result, hence, thus, therefore, accordingly, for this reason*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Consequently, we have peace with God."* (Adaptado de Romanos 5:1)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 5:1-5, ESV):** 
> *"Therefore, since we have been justified by faith, we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ. Through him we have also obtained access by faith into this grace in which we stand, and we rejoice in hope of the glory of God. Not only that, but we rejoice in our sufferings, knowing that suffering produces endurance, and endurance produces character, and character produces hope, and hope does not put us to shame, because God's love has been poured into our hearts through the Holy Spirit who has been given to us."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| justified | justificados | peace | paz |
| obtained | obtenido | access | acceso |
| grace | gracia | stand | estar |
| rejoice | regocijarse | sufferings | sufrimientos |
| endurance | perseverancia | character | carácter |
| hope | esperanza | shame | vergüenza |
| poured | derramado | hearts | corazones |

**Conectores de consecuencia y resultado (profundización):**

| Conector | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *consequently* | Por consiguiente | ***Consequently**, we have peace with God.* |
| *as a result* | Como resultado | *He rose from the dead; **as a result**, we have hope.* |
| *hence* | Por lo tanto (formal) | *He overcame death; **hence**, we have life.* |
| *thus* | Así que (formal) | *He died and rose; **thus**, salvation is available.* |
| *therefore* | Por lo tanto | *He loved us; **therefore**, we love him.* |
| *accordingly* | En consecuencia | *He commanded; **accordingly**, they obeyed.* |
| *for this reason* | Por esta razón | ***For this reason**, he came to save us.* |
| *wherefore* | Por lo cual (formal) | ***Wherefore**, let us draw near with confidence.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"**Therefore**, since we have been justified by faith, we have peace with God."* (Romanos 5:1) – Por tanto, ya que hemos sido justificados por la fe, tenemos paz con Dios.
2. *"**Consequently**, faith comes from hearing the message."* (Romanos 10:17) – Por consiguiente, la fe viene del oír el mensaje.
3. *"**As a result**, they were filled with the Spirit."* (Hechos 2:4) – Como resultado, fueron llenos del Espíritu.
4. *"**Hence**, we should not be afraid."* (Hebreos 13:6, adaptado) – Por lo tanto, no debemos tener miedo.
5. *"**Thus**, death has been swallowed up in victory."* (1 Corintios 15:54) – Así, la muerte ha sido devorada en victoria.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal):**

- ***Consequently**, we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ.* (Por consiguiente, tenemos paz con Dios por medio de nuestro Señor Jesucristo.)
- ***As a result** of his sacrifice, we are forgiven.* (Como resultado de su sacrificio, somos perdonados.)
- ***Hence**, we should live for him.* (Por lo tanto, debemos vivir para él.)
- ***Therefore**, let us draw near to the throne of grace with confidence.* (Por tanto, acerquémonos con confianza al trono de la gracia.)
- ***For this reason**, he was sent into the world.* (Por esta razón, fue enviado al mundo.)
- ***Wherefore**, let us hold fast our confession.* (Por lo cual, retengamos nuestra confesión.)

**Edificación:** Pablo declara que, como resultado de la justificación por la fe, tenemos paz con Dios. Aprendemos a usar conectores de consecuencia para articular la lógica de la salvación y la esperanza.

---

### Lección 34 – "In Order That We Might Be Saved"
**Gramática focal:** Conectores de propósito avanzados (*so that, in order that, with a view to, for the purpose of, lest, for fear that*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"These are written in order that you may believe."* (Adaptado de Juan 20:31)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 20:30-31, ESV):** 
> *"Now Jesus did many other signs in the presence of the disciples, which are not written in this book; but these are written so that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God, and that by believing you may have life in his name."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| signs | señales | written | escrito |
| believe | creer | Christ | Cristo |
| Son of God | Hijo de Dios | life | vida |

**Conectores de propósito avanzados (profundización):**

| Conector | Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *so that* | + cláusula (con *may/might/will*) | *These are written **so that** you **may** believe.* |
| *in order that* | + cláusula (formal) | *He came **in order that** we **might** have life.* |
| *with a view to* | + -ing | *He preached **with a view to** saving souls.* |
| *for the purpose of* | + -ing | *The Bible was given **for the purpose of** teaching.* |
| *lest* | + subjuntivo (formal, para evitar) | *He warned them **lest** they **should** fall.* |
| *for fear that* | + cláusula (temor) | *They hid **for fear that** they **would** be seen.* |
| *to the end that* | + cláusula (formal) | *He taught **to the end that** we **might** know.* |

**Más ejemplos bíblicos:**

1. *"He sent his Son **so that** we might live through him."* (1 Juan 4:9) – Envió a su Hijo para que vivamos por medio de él.
2. *"They prayed **in order that** they might receive the Spirit."* (Hechos 8:15) – Oraron para que recibieran el Espíritu.
3. *"He gave the law **with a view to** revealing sin."* (Romanos 7:7, adaptado) – Dio la ley con miras a revelar el pecado.
4. *"Do not be deceived, **lest** you fall."* (1 Corintios 10:12) – No te engañes, no sea que caigas.
5. *"They feared **for fear that** they would be discovered."* (Mateo 2:13, adaptado) – Temían no fueran a ser descubiertos.

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal):**

- *I read the Bible **so that** I may grow in faith.* (Leo la Biblia para que crezca en fe.)
- *He prays every day **in order that** he might stay close to God.* (Ora cada día para que pueda permanecer cerca de Dios.)
- *She serves in the church **with a view to** helping others.* (Sirve en la iglesia con miras a ayudar a otros.)
- *The lesson was designed **for the purpose of** teaching the gospel.* (La lección fue diseñada con el propósito de enseñar el evangelio.)
- *Be watchful, **lest** you should fall into temptation.* (Velad, no sea que caigáis en tentación.)
- *They were silent **for fear that** they would be judged.* (Guardaron silencio por temor a ser juzgados.)

**Edificación:** El Evangelio de Juan fue escrito con un propósito claro: que creamos en Cristo. Aprendemos a usar conectores de propósito avanzados para articular la intención divina detrás de la revelación y la misión de la iglesia.

---

### Lección 35 – Repaso: "Consequently, We Have Hope"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de conectores de concesión, causa, consecuencia y propósito.

**Actividad de repaso:** El estudiante escribe 12 oraciones usando diferentes conectores avanzados.

**Ejemplo:**
1. ***Notwithstanding** the trials, I trust in God.** (Concesión)
2. ***Albeit** weak, he was strong in faith.** (Concesión)
3. ***Inasmuch as** he loved us, we should love others.** (Causa)
4. ***Given that** God is faithful, we can trust him.** (Causa)
5. ***Consequently**, we have peace with God.** (Consecuencia)
6. ***As a result** of his death, we have life.** (Consecuencia)
7. ***Therefore**, let us serve him.** (Consecuencia)
8. ***So that** we may believe, the Bible was written.** (Propósito)
9. ***In order that** we might live, he died.** (Propósito)
10. ***Lest** we fall, let us watch and pray.** (Propósito)
11. ***For fear that** we might be lost, he saved us.** (Propósito)
12. ***Wherefore**, let us hold fast our faith.** (Consecuencia)

---

## UNIDAD 8: SINTAXIS COMPLEJA Y ESTILO AVANZADO
*Lecciones 36 a 40*

---

### Lección 36 – "The Lord, Having Considered the Heart, Saw the Truth"
**Gramática focal:** Sintaxis compleja con cláusulas absolutas, participiales y relativas anidadas.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The Lord, having considered the heart, saw the truth."* (Adaptado de 1 Samuel 16:7 – *"Man looks on the outward appearance, but the Lord looks on the heart."*)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – 1 Samuel 16:6-13, ESV):** 
> *"When they came, he looked on Eliab and thought, 'Surely the Lord's anointed is before him.' But the Lord said to Samuel, 'Do not look on his appearance or on the height of his stature, because I have rejected him. For the Lord sees not as man sees: man looks on the outward appearance, but the Lord looks on the heart.' Then Jesse called Abinadab and made him pass before Samuel. And he said, 'Neither has the Lord chosen this one.' Then Jesse made Shammah pass by. And he said, 'Neither has the Lord chosen this one.' And Jesse made seven of his sons pass before Samuel. And Samuel said to Jesse, 'The Lord has not chosen these.' Then Samuel said to Jesse, 'Are all your sons here?' And he said, 'There remains yet the youngest, but behold, he is keeping the sheep.' And Samuel said to Jesse, 'Send and get him, for we will not sit down till he comes here.' And he sent and brought him in. Now he was ruddy and had beautiful eyes and was handsome. And the Lord said, 'Arise, anoint him, for this is he.' Then Samuel took the horn of oil and anointed him in the midst of his brothers. And the Spirit of the Lord rushed upon David from that day forward."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| appearance | apariencia | height | altura |
| stature | estatura | rejected | rechazado |
| outward | externo | heart | corazón |
| youngest | el más joven | keeping | cuidando |
| sheep | ovejas | ruddy | rubio / de piel rojiza |
| handsome | apuesto | anoint | ungir |
| horn | cuerno | oil | aceite |
| rushed upon | vino sobre | | |

**Sintaxis compleja – Cláusulas anidadas:**

| Nivel | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| **Cláusula principal** | *The Lord saw the truth.* |
| **Cláusula participial** | ***Having considered the heart**, the Lord saw the truth.* |
| **Cláusula absoluta** | *The Lord, **his heart full of wisdom**, saw the truth.* |
| **Cláusula relativa** | *The Lord, **who considers the heart**, saw the truth.* |
| **Cláusula adverbial** | *The Lord, **having considered the heart**, saw the truth.* |
| **Cláusula condicional** | *The Lord, **if he considers the heart**, saw the truth.* |

**Ejemplo de sintaxis compleja (anidada):**

> *"The Lord, who, having considered the heart of David, which was pure and devoted to him, saw the truth that others could not see."*

**Estructura de la oración compleja:**
- **Cláusula principal:** *The Lord saw the truth.*
- **Cláusula relativa 1:** *who having considered the heart of David*
- **Cláusula participial:** *having considered the heart of David*
- **Cláusula relativa 2:** *which was pure and devoted to him*
- **Cláusula de resultado:** *that others could not see*

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo literario avanzado):**

- *The Lord, **who, having seen the heart of man, judges with perfect righteousness**, is worthy of all praise.* (El Señor, quien, habiendo visto el corazón del hombre, juzga con perfecta justicia, es digno de toda alabanza.)
- *David, **whose heart, having been purified by faith, was devoted to God**, was chosen as king.* (David, cuyo corazón, habiendo sido purificado por la fe, estaba dedicado a Dios, fue elegido como rey.)
- *The Spirit, **having been poured out on the day of Pentecost**, filled the disciples with power.* (El Espíritu, habiendo sido derramado en el día de Pentecostés, llenó a los discípulos de poder.)
- *The gospel, **which, having been preached throughout the world**, continues to transform lives, is the power of God unto salvation.* (El evangelio, el cual, habiendo sido predicado en todo el mundo, continúa transformando vidas, es el poder de Dios para salvación.)

**Edificación:** Dios no mira la apariencia exterior, sino el corazón. Aprendemos a construir oraciones complejas para expresar la profundidad de la teología bíblica con precisión y estilo.

---

### Lección 37 – "The Gospel, Which Is the Power of God, Is Preached to All"
**Gramática focal:** Sintaxis compleja con cláusulas relativas no-definitorias, definitorias y anidadas.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The gospel, which is the power of God, is preached to all."* (Adaptado de Romanos 1:16)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Romanos 1:16-17, ESV):** 
> *"For I am not ashamed of the gospel, for it is the power of God for salvation to everyone who believes, to the Jew first and also to the Greek. For in it the righteousness of God is revealed from faith for faith, as it is written, 'The righteous shall live by faith.'"*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| ashamed | avergonzado | gospel | evangelio |
| power | poder | salvation | salvación |
| righteousness | justicia | revealed | revelada |
| faith | fe | righteous | justo |

**Tipos de cláusulas relativas:**

| Tipo | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Definitoria** | Especifica a qué persona/cosa nos referimos | *The gospel **that is preached** is powerful.* |
| **No-definitoria** | Da información adicional (con comas) | *The gospel, **which is the power of God**, is preached.* |
| **Anidada** | Relativa dentro de otra relativa | *The gospel, **which is the power of God that saves all who believe**, is preached.* |

**Cláusulas relativas con preposiciones:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Preposición + whom/which* | *The gospel **in which** we believe.* |
| *Preposición + who/which* (final) | *The gospel **which** we believe **in**.* |

**Cláusulas relativas con *whose* y *whom*:**

| Pronombre | Uso | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *whose* | Posesión (personas) | *The man **whose** faith was strong.* |
| *whom* | Objeto (personas) | *The apostle **whom** Jesus loved.* |

**Ejemplo de sintaxis compleja con relativas anidadas:**

> *"The gospel, which is the power of God for salvation to everyone who believes, to the Jew first and also to the Greek, is the message that Paul preached, which he received from the Lord, who appeared to him on the road to Damascus."*

**Estructura:**
1. *The gospel is the message.* (Principal)
2. ***which** is the power of God...* (No-definitoria)
3. ***who** believes* (Definitoria)
4. ***that** Paul preached* (Definitoria)
5. ***which** he received from the Lord* (No-definitoria)
6. ***who** appeared to him* (No-definitoria)

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo literario):**

- *The gospel, **which is the power of God for salvation**, is the message **that** I believe.* (El evangelio, que es el poder de Dios para salvación, es el mensaje que creo.)
- *Jesus, **who** is the Son of God, died for our sins, **which** were many.* (Jesús, que es el Hijo de Dios, murió por nuestros pecados, los cuales eran muchos.)
- *The apostles, **whom** Jesus chose, preached the gospel to all nations, **which** was their commission.* (Los apóstoles, a quienes Jesús escogió, predicaron el evangelio a todas las naciones, lo cual era su comisión.)
- *The church, **whose** mission is to make disciples, continues the work **that** Jesus began.* (La iglesia, cuya misión es hacer discípulos, continúa la obra que Jesús comenzó.)
- *The Scriptures, **which** are inspired by God, are useful for teaching, **in which** we find wisdom.* (Las Escrituras, que son inspiradas por Dios, son útiles para enseñar, en las cuales encontramos sabiduría.)

**Edificación:** Pablo no se avergüenza del evangelio, porque es el poder de Dios para salvación. Aprendemos a construir oraciones complejas con cláusulas relativas anidadas para expresar la riqueza de la teología bíblica.

---

### Lección 38 – "Should Anyone Ask You, Tell Them..."
**Gramática focal:** Sintaxis condicional y concesiva compleja (*should, were, had* con inversión; *albeit, notwithstanding*).

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"Should anyone ask you, tell them..."* (Adaptado de Marcos 11:3)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Marcos 11:1-6, ESV):** 
> *"Now when they drew near to Jerusalem, to Bethphage and Bethany, at the Mount of Olives, Jesus sent two of his disciples and said to them, 'Go into the village in front of you, and immediately as you enter it you will find a colt tied, on which no one has ever sat. Untie it and bring it. If anyone says to you, "Why are you doing this?" say, "The Lord has need of it and will send it back here immediately."' And they went away and found a colt tied at a door outside in the street, and they untied it. And some of those standing there said to them, 'What are you doing, untying the colt?' And they told them what Jesus had said, and they let them go."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| drew near | se acercaron | village | aldea |
| colt | pollino | tied | atado |
| untie | desatar | standing | de pie |
| street | calle | let them go | los dejaron ir |

**Inversión condicional con *should*:**

| Estructura | Significado | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *Should + sujeto + verbo* | Si llegara a... (primer condicional formal) | ***Should anyone ask** you, tell them.* |
| *Had + sujeto + pp* | Si hubiera... (tercer condicional formal) | ***Had I known**, I would have come.* |
| *Were + sujeto + to + infinitivo* | Si fuera a... (segundo condicional formal) | ***Were I to ask**, would you answer?* |
| *Were + sujeto* | Si yo fuera... (condicional presente) | ***Were I you**, I would pray.* |

**Concesión con *albeit* y *notwithstanding*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Albeit + adjetivo/adverbio* | *He was weak, **albeit** determined.* |
| *Notwithstanding* (adverbio) | *He suffered; **notwithstanding**, he trusted.* |
| *Notwithstanding + sustantivo* | ***Notwithstanding** the difficulties, he persevered.* |
| *Be that as it may* | ***Be that as it may**, I will serve the Lord.* |

**Ejemplos de sintaxis condicional y concesiva compleja:**

> *"Should anyone ask you about the hope that is in you, be prepared to give an answer; however, should they oppose you, be gentle in your response, albeit firm in your conviction."*

**Estructura:**
- *Should anyone ask...* (Condicional formal)
- *be prepared to give an answer* (Imperativo)
- *should they oppose you* (Condicional formal)
- *be gentle* (Imperativo)
- *albeit firm* (Concesión)

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo formal y pastoral):**

- ***Should anyone question** your faith, be ready to answer with gentleness and respect.* (Si alguien cuestiona tu fe, estate listo para responder con mansedumbre y respeto.)
- ***Had I known** the truth earlier, I would have followed Christ sooner.* (Si hubiera conocido la verdad antes, habría seguido a Cristo más pronto.)
- ***Were I to give** you advice, I would tell you to trust in the Lord.* (Si fuera a darte un consejo, te diría que confíes en el Señor.)
- *He was persecuted, **albeit** he never wavered in his faith.* (Fue perseguido, aunque nunca vaciló en su fe.)
- ***Notwithstanding** the opposition, the church grew.* (A pesar de la oposición, la iglesia creció.)
- ***Be that as it may**, I will continue to preach the gospel.* (Sea como sea, continuaré predicando el evangelio.)

**Edificación:** Jesús instruyó a sus discípulos sobre cómo responder si alguien les preguntaba. Aprendemos a usar la sintaxis condicional formal para expresar instrucciones y consejos pastorales.

---

### Lección 39 – "So Great Was His Love That He Gave His Son"
**Gramática focal:** Sintaxis enfática e inversión con *so... that, such... that, only, not only*.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"So great was his love that he gave his only Son."* (Adaptado de Juan 3:16)

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Juan 3:16-21, ESV):** 
> *"For God so loved the world, that he gave his only Son, that whoever believes in him should not perish but have eternal life. For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world, but in order that the world might be saved through him. Whoever believes in him is not condemned, but whoever does not believe is condemned already, because he has not believed in the name of the only Son of God. And this is the judgment: the light has come into the world, and people loved the darkness rather than the light because their works were evil. For everyone who does wicked things hates the light and does not come to the light, lest his works should be exposed. But whoever does what is true comes to the light, so that it may be clearly seen that his works have been carried out in God."*

**Vocabulario extraído del texto:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| loved | amó | gave | dio |
| perish | perecer | eternal life | vida eterna |
| condemn | condenar | judgment | juicio |
| darkness | oscuridad | wicked | malvados |
| exposed | expuestos | | |

**Inversión enfática con *so... that* y *such... that*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *So + adjetivo/adverbio + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + that...* | ***So great was his love** that he gave his Son.* |
| *So + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + that...* | ***So great did he love** that he gave his Son.* |
| *Such + be + sujeto + that...* | ***Such was his love** that he gave his Son.* |
| *Such + sustantivo + be + sujeto + that...* | ***Such a great love was his** that he gave his Son.* |

**Inversión con *only* y *not only*:**

| Estructura | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|
| *Only + adverbio + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Only by faith can we be saved.** * |
| *Not only + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo + but also* | ***Not only did he die**, but also he rose.* |
| *Only when + cláusula + auxiliar + sujeto + verbo* | ***Only when we believe** do we receive.* |

**Ejemplo de sintaxis enfática compleja:**

> *"So great was the love of God for the world that he gave his only Son; and not only did he give him, but he also sent the Spirit, so that all who believe might be saved."*

**Estructura:**
- ***So great was the love...*** (Inversión enfática)
- ***that he gave...*** (Cláusula de resultado)
- ***not only did he give...*** (Inversión adicional)
- ***but also he sent...*** (Adición)
- ***so that all who believe might be saved*** (Propósito)

**Aplicación Cotidiana (Estilo retórico):**

- ***So great was God's mercy** that he forgave all our sins.* (Tan grande fue la misericordia de Dios que perdonó todos nuestros pecados.)
- ***Such was the power of the Spirit** that thousands were converted.* (Tal fue el poder del Espíritu que miles fueron convertidos.)
- ***Not only did he heal** the sick, but also he raised the dead.* (No solo sanó a los enfermos, sino que también resucitó a los muertos.)
- ***Only by grace can we be saved.** * (Solo por gracia podemos ser salvos.)
- ***Only when we repent do we receive** forgiveness.* (Solo cuando nos arrepentimos recibimos perdón.)
- ***So profound is God's love** that it surpasses all understanding.* (Tan profundo es el amor de Dios que sobrepasa todo entendimiento.)

**Edificación:** El amor de Dios es tan grande que dio a su Hijo. Aprendemos a usar la sintaxis enfática e inversión para proclamar la grandeza del amor divino.

---

### Lección 40 – Repaso Final: "The Love of Christ, Which Surpasses Knowledge"
**Gramática focal:** Repaso de todos los temas del nivel C1.

**Versículo Clave:** 
> *"The love of Christ, which surpasses knowledge, that you may be filled with all the fullness of God."* — **Efesios 3:19**

**Texto Extendido (Lectura – Efesios 3:14-21, ESV):** 
> *"For this reason I bow my knees before the Father, from whom every family in heaven and on earth is named, that according to the riches of his glory he may grant you to be strengthened with power through his Spirit in your inner being, so that Christ may dwell in your hearts through faith—that you, being rooted and grounded in love, may have strength to comprehend with all the saints what is the breadth and length and height and depth, and to know the love of Christ that surpasses knowledge, that you may be filled with all the fullness of God. Now to him who is able to do far more abundantly than all we ask or think, according to the power at work within us, to him be glory in the church and in Christ Jesus throughout all generations, forever and ever. Amen."*

**Vocabulario final:**

| Palabra | Significado | Palabra | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| bow my knees | doblar mis rodillas | family | familia |
| riches | riquezas | glory | gloria |
| strengthened | fortalecido | inner being | ser interior |
| dwell | morar | rooted | arraigado |
| grounded | cimentado | comprehend | comprender |
| breadth | anchura | length | longitud |
| height | altura | depth | profundidad |
| surpasses | sobrepasa | fullness | plenitud |
| abundantly | abundantemente | generations | generaciones |

---

## Actividad Final de Evaluación – Nivel C1

El estudiante debe escribir un **ensayo teológico-exegético** de **500-600 palabras** sobre el siguiente tema:

**"La profundidad del amor de Cristo y su implicación para la vida del creyente" (Efesios 3:14-21)**

Debe incluir al menos **20** de las siguientes estructuras avanzadas del nivel C1 (marcar claramente cada una):

1. **Inversión condicional** (*Had I known, Were I to, Should you*)
2. **Inversión con adverbios negativos** (*Never have I, Seldom do we*)
3. **Inversión con *so... that* / *such... that***
4. **Fronting** (*What we need is, In him we trust*)
5. **Cleft sentences** (*It was Christ who...*)
6. **Pseudo-cleft sentences** (*What I believe is...*)
7. **Participios perfectivos** (*Having loved, Having been sent*)
8. **Frases absolutas** (*His heart burning, With faith unshaken*)
9. **Cláusulas relativas anidadas** (*The gospel, which is the power of God that saves...*)
10. **Nominalización** (*salvation, redemption, justification, sanctification*)
11. **Voz pasiva con verbos de percepción** (*He was seen to, She was heard to*)
12. **Modales de deducción en pasado** (*must have been, might have been*)
13. **Modales de necesidad en pasado** (*needn't have, didn't need to*)
14. **Reporting verbs con infinitivo perfectivo** (*claim to have, deny having*)
15. **Subjuntivo en cláusulas de necesidad** (*It is necessary that he be*)
16. **Conectores de concesión avanzados** (*notwithstanding, albeit, nevertheless*)
17. **Conectores causales avanzados** (*inasmuch as, insofar as, given that*)
18. **Conectores de consecuencia avanzados** (*consequently, hence, thus*)
19. **Conectores de propósito avanzados** (*so that, in order that, lest*)
20. **Construcciones con *he who* / *the one who* / *whoever***
21. **Discurso indirecto avanzado** (con verbos de reporte complejos)
22. **Participios pasivos perfectivos** (*having been forgiven, being justified*)

---

## Ejemplo de Ensayo Final (para guía del estudiante)

> *"The love of Christ, which surpasses knowledge, is the central theme of the apostle Paul's prayer in Ephesians 3. **So profound is this love** that Paul bows his knees before the Father, asking that the believers **may have strength to comprehend** its breadth, length, height, and depth. **Having been** inspired by the Spirit, Paul writes with passion and theological depth, **urging that the church be** filled with all the fullness of God.*
>
> *The apostle, **whose heart was devoted to Christ**, prays that believers **would be strengthened** with power through the Spirit in their inner being. **Were I to summarize** Paul's prayer, I would say that it is a plea for spiritual depth. **Had it not been for** Christ's sacrificial love, we **would have remained** in our sins. **Not only did he die** for us, **but also he rose** from the dead, **so that** we might live through him. **Consequently**, we are called to live **rooted and grounded** in love.*
>
> *The **knowledge** of Christ's love is not merely intellectual; **it is an experiential knowledge** that transforms the believer. **Inasmuch as** we are in Christ, **insofar as** we abide in his love, we are empowered to comprehend **what surpasses understanding**. **Nevertheless**, this comprehension is not fully achieved in this life; **rather, it is a progressive revelation** of God's glory. **Notwithstanding** our limitations, Paul assures us that God **is able to do far more abundantly** than all we ask or think.*
>
> ***Should anyone ask** me about the hope that is in me, I **would point** to the love of Christ. **He who** has experienced this love **can never be** the same. **The one who** believes in Christ **is filled** with all the fullness of God. **Never have I known** a love so deep, so wide, so high, and so unsearchable. **Such was the love of God** that he gave his only Son, **so that** we might have eternal life. **All we can do** is bow our knees and worship.*
>
> *In conclusion, the love of Christ, **which is the foundation of our faith**, **surpasses all knowledge** and **fills us** with the fullness of God. **To him be glory** in the church and in Christ Jesus **throughout all generations, forever and ever.** Amen."*

---

## Apéndice 1: Tabla de Conectores Avanzados C1

| Categoría | Conectores | Uso |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Adición** | *moreover, furthermore, in addition, besides, not only... but also, additionally* | Añadir información |
| **Contraste** | *nevertheless, nonetheless, whereas, whilst, yet, albeit, notwithstanding, for all that, be that as it may* | Expresar contraste |
| **Causa** | *inasmuch as, insofar as, in that, given that, seeing that, forasmuch as, owing to, due to* | Expresar causa |
| **Consecuencia** | *consequently, as a result, hence, thus, therefore, accordingly, wherefore, for this reason* | Expresar resultado |
| **Propósito** | *so that, in order that, with a view to, for the purpose of, lest, for fear that, to the end that* | Expresar propósito |
| **Concesión** | *although, though, even though, albeit, notwithstanding, despite, in spite of, while, whilst* | Expresar concesión |
| **Condición** | *if, unless, provided that, on condition that, as long as, assuming that, given that* | Expresar condición |
| **Reformulación** | *that is to say, in other words, namely, i.e., to put it another way* | Reformular |
| **Ejemplificación** | *for instance, for example, to illustrate, such as, e.g.* | Ejemplificar |
| **Conclusión** | *in conclusion, to sum up, in summary, to conclude, ultimately* | Concluir |

---

## Apéndice 2: Verbos de Reporte Avanzados para C1

| Verbo | Estructura | Significado |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *assert* | *assert that* | afirmar (con autoridad) |
| *maintain* | *maintain that* | sostener / mantener |
| *contend* | *contend that* | sostener / argumentar |
| *affirm* | *affirm that* | afirmar (con certeza) |
| *allege* | *allege that* | alegar (sin prueba) |
| *postulate* | *postulate that* | postular |
| *hypothesize* | *hypothesize that* | hipotetizar |
| *concede* | *concede that* | conceder |
| *acknowledge* | *acknowledge that* | reconocer |
| *emphasize* | *emphasize that* | enfatizar |
| *highlight* | *highlight that* | destacar |
| *underscore* | *underscore that* | subrayar |
| *elaborate* | *elaborate on* | elaborar sobre |
| *expound* | *expound on* | exponer / desarrollar |
| *exhort* | *exhort someone to do* | exhortar |
| *implore* | *implore someone to do* | implorar |
| *beseech* | *beseech someone to do* | suplicar |

---

## Apéndice 3: Modismos y Expresiones Bíblicas en Inglés

| Expresión | Significado | Origen |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *"The writing is on the wall."* | La evidencia del juicio está clara | Daniel 5 |
| *"A drop in the bucket."* | Una cantidad insignificante | Isaías 40:15 |
| *"Eye for an eye."* | Justicia retributiva | Éxodo 21:24 |
| *"Nothing new under the sun."* | Todo es vanidad | Eclesiastés 1:9 |
| *"A still small voice."* | Una voz suave y apacible | 1 Reyes 19:12 |
| *"Go the extra mile."* | Hacer más de lo requerido | Mateo 5:41 |
| *"Turn the other cheek."* | No resistir al malvado | Mateo 5:39 |
| *"The salt of the earth."* | Personas de gran valor | Mateo 5:13 |
| *"By the skin of my teeth."* | Por poco / apenas | Job 19:20 |
| *"The handwriting on the wall."* | Señal de juicio inminente | Daniel 5:5-6 |

---

## Conclusión del Curso

Al completar este nivel C1, el estudiante será capaz de:

- Comprender una amplia gama de textos largos y exigentes, incluyendo la Biblia en versiones estándar (ESV, NIV, NASB), reconociendo significados implícitos.
- Expresarse con fluidez y espontaneidad sin esfuerzo aparente.
- Utilizar el idioma de manera flexible y efectiva para fines sociales, académicos y profesionales, incluyendo la enseñanza y la predicación.
- Producir textos claros, bien estructurados y detallados sobre temas complejos, incluyendo la teología y la exégesis bíblica.

**Edificación Final:**

> *"Y conoceréis la verdad, y la verdad os hará libres."* — Juan 8:32

El estudiante ha recorrido un camino desde el nivel A1 hasta el C1. Ahora puede leer la Biblia en inglés en cualquier versión con comprensión profunda, puede discutir su fe con otros en inglés con fluidez y precisión, puede enseñar y predicar en inglés, y puede seguir creciendo en el conocimiento de la Palabra. Este curso ha sido un instrumento para que la Palabra de Dios more abundantemente en su corazón en el idioma inglés.

**"Toda la Escritura es inspirada por Dios y útil para enseñar, para redargüir, para corregir, para instruir en justicia, a fin de que el hombre de Dios sea perfecto, enteramente preparado para toda buena obra."** – 2 Timoteo 3:16-17

---

**¡A Él sea la gloria en la iglesia y en Cristo Jesús por todas las generaciones, por los siglos de los siglos! Amén.** (Efesios 3:21)
# CURSO DE INGLÉS BÍBLICO – NIVEL C2 (MCER)

## Documento Maestro del Estudiante

---

## Introducción

Este curso es la culminación de la serie y está diseñado para llevar al estudiante desde un nivel avanzado (C1) hasta un **nivel de dominio (C2)** del Marco Común Europeo de Referencia (MCER). En este nivel, el estudiante alcanza una competencia lingüística comparable a la de un hablante nativo culto, con la capacidad de comprender prácticamente todo lo que lee o escucha, y de expresarse con precisión, fluidez y sutileza.

**Versiones de la Biblia recomendadas:**
- **King James Version (KJV)** – para apreciación de la lengua inglesa clásica, estilo literario y retórico.
- **English Standard Version (ESV)** – para precisión teológica y riqueza literaria formal.
- **New American Standard Bible (NASB)** – para estudio detallado con traducción literal.
- **New International Version (NIV)** – para claridad y equilibrio contemporáneo.
- **New Living Translation (NLT)** – para pasajes narrativos y poéticos.
- **The Message (MSG)** – para comparación de estilos y expresiones idiomáticas contemporáneas.
- **Robert Alter's Hebrew Bible Translation** – para apreciación literaria del Antiguo Testamento.
- **David Bentley Hart's New Testament** – para matices teológicos y filosóficos.

**Metodología:**
> *"Leemos la Biblia para aprender inglés, y no al revés."*

El nivel C2 se enfoca en:
1. **Análisis literario profundo** – estructura narrativa, poética, retórica y teológica.
2. **Exégesis y hermenéutica** – interpretación de textos bíblicos en su contexto lingüístico y cultural.
3. **Producción escrita avanzada** – ensayos teológicos, sermones, estudios bíblicos.
4. **Discurso oral avanzado** – debates, predicaciones, conferencias.
5. **Análisis retórico** – identificación y uso de figuras retóricas, estructuras argumentativas.
6. **Estilo y registro** – capacidad de adaptar el lenguaje a diferentes contextos formales e informales.

---

## Estructura del Curso

**Total de lecciones:** 40 lecciones

**Unidades:** 8 unidades de 5 lecciones cada una

**Duración estimada por lección:** 4 - 4.5 horas de instrucción + 4-5 horas de trabajo autónomo

**Duración total estimada:** 160-180 horas de instrucción + 160-200 horas de trabajo autónomo

---

## Contenido Gramatical y Discursivo del Nivel C2

| Categoría | Estructuras C2 |
|:---|:---|
| **Sintaxis Compleja** | Clausulas anidadas múltiples; inversión avanzada; estructuras de énfasis; estilo literario y retórico |
| **Voz Pasiva** | Pasiva en todas sus formas con verbos modales, perfectivos y de percepción; pasiva en discurso indirecto complejo |
| **Modales** | Modales de deducción, necesidad, obligación, crítica (profundización); modales en combinación con verbos de percepción y reporte |
| **Subjuntivo** | Subjuntivo en cláusulas de deseo, necesidad, concesión, condición, propósito; subjuntivo en estilo formal y literario |
| **Discurso Indirecto** | Backshifting avanzado con todos los tiempos y modales; estilo indirecto libre; discurso reportado en narrativa literaria |
| **Conectores** | Conectores de adición, contraste, causa, consecuencia, propósito, concesión, condición, reformulación, ejemplificación, conclusión (profundización) |
| **Clausulas** | Clausulas de relativo (profundización); clausulas de tiempo, lugar, modo, comparación, concesión, propósito, resultado, condición (profundización) |
| **Nominalización** | Transformación de verbos, adjetivos y clausulas en sustantivos; estilo académico y teológico |
| **Figuras Retóricas** | Metáfora, símil, personificación, hipérbole, ironía, paradoja, quiasmo, paralelismo, antítesis, retórica bíblica |
| **Estilo y Registro** | Estilo formal e informal; registro académico, literario, poético, conversacional, predicador; adaptación a diferentes contextos |
| **Puntuación Avanzada** | Uso de punto y coma, dos puntos, guiones, paréntesis, comillas en textos complejos |
| **Análisis Textual** | Análisis de estructura narrativa, poética, argumentativa; identificación de temas, motivos, arcos narrativos |
| **Metadiscurso** | Referencia al propio discurso; organización de ideas; marcadores discursivos avanzados |

---

## UNIDAD 1: ANÁLISIS LITERARIO Y RETÓRICO DEL TEXTO BÍBLICO
*Lecciones 1 a 5*

---

### Lección 1 – "In the Beginning God Created the Heavens and the Earth"
**Gramática focal:** Estructura narrativa, paralelismo, quiasmo y figuras retóricas en el texto bíblico.

**Texto Base (KJV – Génesis 1:1-5):**
> *"In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth. And the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters. And God said, Let there be light: and there was light. And God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness. And God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day."*

**Texto Comparativo (ESV – Génesis 1:1-5):**
> *"In the beginning, God created the heavens and the earth. The earth was without form and void, and darkness was over the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God was hovering over the face of the waters. And God said, 'Let there be light,' and there was light. And God saw that the light was good. And God separated the light from the darkness. God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And there was evening and there was morning, the first day."*

**Vocabulario y Conceptos Literarios:**

| Término | Definición | Ejemplo del Texto |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *void* | vacío, sin contenido | *without form, and void* |
| *deep* | abismo, profundo | *darkness was upon the face of the deep* |
| *hovering* | moviéndose, cerniéndose | *Spirit of God was hovering* |
| *divided/separated* | separado | *divided the light from the darkness* |
| *evening/morning* | tarde/mañana | *the evening and the morning* |

**Figuras Retóricas en el Texto:**

| Figura Retórica | Definición | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Paralelismo** | Estructura repetitiva con variación | *God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night.* |
| **Quiasmo** | Estructura en forma de quiasmo (A-B-B-A) | *"In the beginning God created..." y "The Spirit of God moved..."* (estructura quiástica en la narrativa) |
| **Anáfora** | Repetición de palabras al inicio | *"And God said... And God saw... And God divided..."* |
| **Epífora** | Repetición de palabras al final | *"...and there was light"* (como refuerzo de la creación) |
| **Metonimia** | Substitución de un término por otro relacionado | *"face of the deep"* (profundidad como entidad) |
| **Hipérbole** | Exageración retórica | *"without form, and void"* (énfasis en el caos original) |

**Análisis Estilístico:**

1. **Vocabulario:** El texto utiliza un vocabulario simple pero de gran peso teológico. Las palabras clave son monosílabas o bisílabas: *God, light, day, night, good*. Esta simplicidad da autoridad al texto.

2. **Estructura:** La narrativa sigue un patrón repetitivo: "And God said... and it was so... and God saw that it was good." Este patrón establece el ritmo y la autoridad divina.

3. **Paralelismo:** El versículo 5 presenta un paralelismo antitético: *"God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night."* La estructura A-B-A-B refuerza el contraste.

4. **Quiasmo:** La estructura de los primeros versículos puede leerse como un quiasmo:
   - A: *"In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth."* (Creación)
   - B: *"The earth was without form, and void."* (Caos)
   - C: *"The Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters."* (Vida)
   - B': *"Let there be light: and there was light."* (Orden)
   - A': *"God saw the light, that it was good."* (Evaluación)

**Aplicación en Producción Escrita (Análisis Literario):**

El estudiante debe escribir un análisis de 300-400 palabras sobre el estilo literario de Génesis 1:1-5, identificando al menos 5 figuras retóricas y explicando su función teológica.

**Ejemplo de Análisis:**

> *"The opening verses of Genesis present a literary masterpiece that establishes the theological foundations of creation. The text employs a deliberate rhythm through the repetition of 'and' (the Hebrew waw-consecutive), creating a sense of inexorable divine action. The parallelism between 'light' and 'darkness' is not merely a literary device but a theological statement: the divine Word brings order out of chaos. The chiastic structure of verses 1-2 suggests a movement from creation to chaos to life and back to order, with the Spirit of God hovering as the agent of life. The text's use of simple, concrete language—'light,' 'day,' 'night,' 'good'—belies its theological depth. Each word is weighted with meaning, and the repetition of 'good' establishes a moral and aesthetic dimension to creation. The text operates on multiple levels: it is at once a historical narrative, a poetic hymn, and a theological treatise on the nature of God and his relationship to the world."*

**Edificación:** El texto de Génesis 1:1-5 no es solo un relato histórico; es una declaración teológica y literaria que establece el ritmo y la autoridad de la creación divina.

---

### Lección 2 – "The Lord Is My Shepherd; I Shall Not Want"
**Gramática focal:** Poesía hebrea, paralelismo, metáfora, símil, personificación en los Salmos.

**Texto Base (KJV – Salmo 23:1-6):**
> *"The Lord is my shepherd; I shall not want. He maketh me to lie down in green pastures: he leadeth me beside the still waters. He restoreth my soul: he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake. Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil: for thou art with me; thy rod and thy staff they comfort me. Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies: thou anointest my head with oil; my cup runneth over. Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life: and I will dwell in the house of the Lord for ever."*

**Texto Comparativo (NIV – Salmo 23:1-6):**
> *"The Lord is my shepherd, I lack nothing. He makes me lie down in green pastures, he leads me beside quiet waters, he refreshes my soul. He guides me along the right paths for his name's sake. Even though I walk through the darkest valley, I will fear no evil, for you are with me; your rod and your staff, they comfort me. You prepare a table before me in the presence of my enemies. You anoint my head with oil; my cup overflows. Surely your goodness and love will follow me all the days of my life, and I will dwell in the house of the Lord forever."*

**Vocabulario y Conceptos Literarios:**

| Término | Definición | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| *pastures* | pastos, prados | *green pastures* |
| *still waters* | aguas tranquilas | *beside the still waters* |
| *restoreth* | restaura, renueva | *He restoreth my soul* |
| *paths of righteousness* | senderos de justicia | *leads me in the paths of righteousness* |
| *valley of the shadow of death* | valle de sombra de muerte | *walk through the valley...* |
| *rod and staff* | cayado y vara | *rod and thy staff* |
| *anoint* | ungir | *anointest my head with oil* |
| *cup runneth over* | copa rebosa | *my cup runneth over* |

**Figuras Retóricas en el Texto:**

| Figura Retórica | Definición | Ejemplo |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Metáfora** | Imagen que compara dos cosas sin usar "como" | *"The Lord is my shepherd"* |
| **Paralelismo Sinonímico** | Repetición del mismo concepto con palabras diferentes | *"He makes me lie down in green pastures... he leads me beside still waters"* |
| **Paralelismo Antitético** | Contraste entre dos ideas | *"green pastures" vs. "valley of the shadow of death"* |
| **Personificación** | Atribución de características humanas a lo inanimado | *"goodness and mercy shall follow me"* |
| **Hipérbole** | Exageración | *"my cup runneth over"* |
| **Imaginería** | Uso de imágenes sensoriales | *"green pastures," "still waters," "rod and staff"* |
| **Anáfora** | Repetición de "I shall not want" (implícito) y "He..." | *"He maketh... He leadeth... He restoreth..."* |

**Análisis Estilístico:**

1. **Metáfora de Pastor:** La metáfora central del pastor es rica en significado. El pastor provee, guía, protege y cuida a las ovejas. Esta imagen establece la relación entre Dios y el creyente.

2. **Paralelismo:** Todo el salmo está construido sobre paralelismos: cada línea se repite con variación para reforzar el mensaje. Ejemplo: *"The Lord is my shepherd"* y *"I shall not want"* son dos formas de decir lo mismo.

3. **Estructura Quiástica:** El salmo tiene una estructura quiástica:
   - A: Provisión (vv. 1-2)
   - B: Guía (v. 3)
   - C: Protección en la adversidad (v. 4)
   - B': Guía (v. 5 - mesa)
   - A': Provisión y bendición (v. 6)

4. **Transición de Tercera Persona a Segunda Persona:** El salmo cambia de *"He"* a *"Thou"* (tú) en el versículo 4. Este cambio es significativo: el salmista pasa de hablar sobre Dios a hablar directamente con Dios.

**Aplicación en Producción Escrita (Poesía y Exégesis):**

El estudiante debe escribir un análisis exegético de 400-500 palabras sobre el Salmo 23, identificando y explicando las figuras retóricas y su función teológica.

**Ejemplo de Análisis:**

> *"Psalm 23 stands as one of the most beloved and theologically rich passages in the Hebrew Bible. Its literary genius lies in its simplicity and depth. The central metaphor—God as shepherd—operates on multiple levels. In the ancient Near Eastern context, the shepherd was a figure of authority and care, but also of intimacy. The verb 'lead' (nahal) suggests not merely direction but provision and protection. The opening statement, 'I shall not want,' is the logical consequence of the metaphor: if God is shepherd, then all needs are met. The psalm's structure moves from public provision ('green pastures,' 'still waters') to private restoration ('restoreth my soul') to divine guidance ('paths of righteousness'), and then to the protection in the face of death. The shift from third-person to second-person address in verse 4 marks a moment of intimacy: the psalmist is no longer speaking about God but to God. The 'rod and staff' are not merely tools of protection but symbols of divine authority and comfort. The final verses transition from past and present provision to future hope: 'I will dwell in the house of the Lord forever.' The imagery of the table prepared in the presence of enemies suggests not only provision but vindication—a declaration of divine favor in the face of opposition. The psalm is a masterclass in theological poetry, weaving together metaphor, parallelism, and personal testimony into a coherent and theologically profound meditation on divine care."*

**Edificación:** El Salmo 23 es un ejemplo de la poesía hebrea en su máxima expresión, donde la belleza literaria y la profundidad teológica se unen para ofrecer consuelo y esperanza.

---

### Lección 3 – "The Word Was Made Flesh, and Dwelt Among Us"
**Gramática focal:** Análisis del prólogo del Evangelio de Juan (Juan 1:1-18), estructura retórica, paralelismo, inclusio, y características literarias del cuarto evangelio.

**Texto Base (KJV – Juan 1:1-14):**
> *"In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God. The same was in the beginning with God.
